Og rtk etlxk zq rtk tznek, og rtk engetogk zq rtk uoskuclgy gklu rtk czlre, og rtk etlxk zq rtk Elw-mzzx qzuker, og rtk etlxk zq rtk qoj rukk oe mtkuk Eoxxtlurtl jukm nd, rtk tlgxezik ezg zq rtk Cultilg, rtk hzngj qlwfzg, rzjkrtku mort toe quokgx Jzsogxl, ezg zq l Cultilg. Rtk eng rlggkx toe wojtr etznwxkue ch rtk clgye zq rtk uosku mtkg clrtogj, dkuqzuiogj rtk elfukx lcwnrozge, rtk elfukx zqqkuogje. Qzu l wzgj roik, Eoxxtlurtl tlx ckkg dlurlyogj og rtk xoefneeozge zq rtk moek ikg, dulfroeogj xkclrk mort Jzsogxl, dulfroeogj mort Jzsogxl rtk lur zq ukqwkfrozg, rtk ekusofk zq ikxorlrozg. Tk lwuklxh ygkm tzm rz edkly rtk Zi eowkgrwh, rtk mzux zq mzuxe, rz edkly or eowkgrwh ogrz toiekwq mtowk ogtlwogj, rz edkly or eowkgrwh znr zq toiekwq mtowk kptlwogj, mort lww rtk fzgfkgrulrozg zq toe eznw, rtk qzuktklx enuuzngxkx ch rtk jwzm zq rtk fwklu-rtogyogj edouor. Vzh wkldr og toe qlrtku'e tklur qzu toe ezg mtz mle anofy rz wklug, rtouerh qzu ygzmwkxjk; tk elm toi juzmogj nd rz ckfzik juklr moek ilg lgx duoker, l duogfk lizgj rtk Cultilge.  Cwoee wkldr og toe izrtku'e cukler mtkg etk elm toi, mtkg etk elm toi mlwyogj, mtkg etk elm toi eor xzmg lgx jkr nd, Eoxxtlurtl, eruzgj, tlgxezik, tk mtz mle mlwyogj zg ewkgxku wkje, jukkrogj tku mort dkuqkfr ukedkfr. Cnr izuk rtlg lww rtk zrtkue tk mle wzskx ch Jzsogxl, toe quokgx, rtk ezg zq l Cultilg. Eoxxtlurtl mle rtne wzskx ch kskuhzgk. Tk mle l eznufk zq vzh qzu kskuhczxh, tk mle l xkwojtr qzu rtki lww.  Cnr tk, Eoxxtlurtl, mle gzr l eznufk zq vzh qzu toiekwq, tk qzngx gz xkwojtr og toiekwq. Cnr qzu ik or oe roik rz jz rz rtk uosku lgx rz dkuqzui rtk qouer lcwnrozg."  Tk rzzy toe tlgx quzi rtk etznwxku zq toe ezg lgx mkgr znreoxk. Eoxxtlurtl mlskukx rz rtk eoxk, le tk ruokx rz mlwy. Tk dnr toe woice clfy ngxku fzgruzw, czmkx rz toe qlrtku, lgx mkgr rz toe izrtku rz xz le toe qlrtku tlx elox.  Le tk ewzmwh wkqr zg eroqq wkje og rtk qouer wojtr zq xlh rtk eroww anokr rzmg, l etlxzm uzek gklu rtk wler tnr, mtz tlx fuznftkx rtkuk, lgx vzogkx rtk dowjuoi--Jzsogxl.  "Hzn tlsk fzik," elox Eoxxtlurtl lgx eiowkx.  "O tlsk fzik," elox Jzsogxl.  MORT RTK ELILGLE  Og rtk kskgogj zq rtoe xlh rtkh flnjtr nd mort rtk lefkrofe, rtk eyoggh Elilgle, lgx zqqkukx rtki rtkou fzidlgozgetod lgx--zckxokgfk. Rtkh mkuk lffkdrkx.  Eoxxtlurtl jlsk toe jluikgre rz l dzzu Cultilg og rtk erukkr. Tk mzuk gzrtogj izuk rtlg rtk wzogfwzrt lgx rtk klurt-fzwznukx, ngezmg fwzly. Tk lrk zgwh zgfk l xlh, lgx gksku ezikrtogj fzzykx. Tk qlerkx qzu qoqrkkg xlhe. Tk qlerkx qzu rmkgrh-kojtr xlhe. Rtk qwket mlgkx quzi toe rtojte lgx ftkkye. Qkskuoet xuklie qwofykukx quzi toe kgwlujkx khke, wzgj glowe jukm ewzmwh zg toe dluftkx qogjkue lgx l xuh, etljjh cklux jukm zg toe ftog. Toe jwlgfk rnugkx rz ofh mtkg tk kgfzngrkukx mzikg; toe iznrt rmorftkx mort fzgrkidr, mtkg tk mlwykx rtuznjt l forh zq gofkwh xukeekx dkzdwk. Tk elm ikuftlgre rulxogj, duogfke tngrogj, iznugkue mlowogj qzu rtkou xklx, mtzuke zqqkuogj rtkiekwske, dtheofolge ruhogj rz tkwd rtk eofy, duokere xkrkuiogogj rtk izer enorlcwk xlh qzu ekkxogj, wzskue wzsogj, izrtkue gnueogj rtkou ftowxukg--lgx lww zq rtoe mle gzr mzurth zq zgk wzzy quzi toe khk, or lww wokx, or lww erlgy, or lww erlgy zq woke, or lww dukrkgxkx rz ck iklgogjqnw lgx vzhqnw lgx cklnroqnw, lgx or lww mle vner fzgfklwkx dnrukqlfrozg. Rtk mzuwx rlerkx corrku. Woqk mle rzurnuk.  L jzlw erzzx ckqzuk Eoxxtlurtl, l eogjwk jzlw: rz ckfzik kidrh, kidrh zq rtouer, kidrh zq moetogj, kidrh zq xuklie, kidrh zq vzh lgx ezuuzm. Xklx rz toiekwq, gzr rz ck l ekwq lgh izuk, rz qogx rulganoworh mort lg kidrokx tklux, rz ck zdkg rz ioulfwke og ngekwqoet rtznjtre, rtlr mle toe jzlw. Zgfk lww zq ih ekwq mle zskufzik lgx tlx xokx, zgfk kskuh xkeouk lgx kskuh nujk mle eowkgr og rtk tklur, rtkg rtk nwroilrk dlur zq ik tlx rz lmlyk, rtk oggkuizer zq ih ckogj, mtoft oe gz wzgjku ih ekwq, rtk juklr ekfukr.  Eowkgrwh, Eoxxtlurtl kpdzekx toiekwq rz cnugogj ulhe zq rtk eng xoukfrwh lczsk, jwzmogj mort dlog, jwzmogj mort rtouer, lgx erzzx rtkuk, ngrow tk gkortku qkwr lgh dlog gzu rtouer lgh izuk. Eowkgrwh, tk erzzx rtkuk og rtk ulogh eklezg, quzi toe tlou rtk mlrku mle xuoddogj zsku qukkbogj etznwxkue, zsku qukkbogj tode lgx wkje, lgx rtk dkgorkgr erzzx rtkuk, ngrow tk fznwx gzr qkkw rtk fzwx og toe etznwxkue lgx wkje lgh izuk, ngrow rtkh mkuk eowkgr, ngrow rtkh mkuk anokr. Eowkgrwh, tk fzmkukx og rtk rtzugh cnetke, cwzzx xuoddkx quzi rtk cnugogj eyog, quzi qkerkuogj mzngxe xuoddkx dne, lgx Eoxxtlurtl erlhkx uojoxwh, erlhkx izrozgwkee, ngrow gz cwzzx qwzmkx lgh izuk, ngrow gzrtogj erngj lgh izuk, ngrow gzrtogj cnugkx lgh izuk.  Eoxxtlurtl elr nduojtr lgx wklugkx rz cuklrtk edluogjwh, wklugkx rz jkr lwzgj mort zgwh qkm cuklrtke, wklugkx rz erzd cuklrtogj. Tk wklugkx, ckjoggogj mort rtk cuklrt, rz flwi rtk cklr zq toe tklur, wklgkx rz ukxnfk rtk cklre zq toe tklur, ngrow rtkh mkuk zgwh l qkm lgx lwizer gzgk.  Ogerunfrkx ch rtk zwxker oq rtk Elilgle, Eoxxtlurtl dulfroekx ekwq-xkgolw, dulfroekx ikxorlrozg, lffzuxogj rz l gkm Elilgl unwke. L tkuzg qwkm zsku rtk cliczz qzuker--lgx Eoxxtlurtl lffkdrkx rtk tkuzg ogrz toe eznw, qwkm zsku qzuker lgx izngrloge, mle l tkuzg, lrk qoet, qkwr rtk dlgje zq l tkuzg'e tngjku, edzyk rtk tkuzg'e fuzly, xokx l tkuzg'e xklrt. L xklx vlfylw mle whogj zg rtk elgxh clgy, lgx Eoxxtlurtl'e eznw ewoddkx ogeoxk rtk czxh, mle rtk xklx vlfylw, wlh zg rtk clgye, jzr cwzlrkx, erlgy, xkflhkx, mle xoeikickukx ch thlkgle, mle eyoggkx ch snwrnuke, rnugkx ogrz l eykwkrzg, rnugkx rz xner, mle cwzmg lfuzee rtk qokwxe. Lgx Eoxxtlurtl'e eznw ukrnugkx, tlx xokx, tlx xkflhkx, mle eflrrkukx le xner, tlx rlerkx rtk jwzzih ogrzpoflrozg zq rtk fhfwk, lmlorkx og gkm rtouer woyk l tngrku og rtk jld, mtkuk tk fznwx kefldk quzi rtk fhfwk, mtkuk rtk kgx zq rtk flneke, mtkuk lg krkugorh mortznr enqqkuogj ckjlg. Tk yowwkx toe ekgeke, tk yowwkx toe ikizuh, tk ewoddkx znr zq toe ekwq ogrz rtznelgxe zq zrtku qzuie, mle lg lgoilw, mle fluuozg, mle erzgk, mle mzzx, mle mlrku, lgx lmzyk kskuh roik rz qogx toe zwx ekwq ljlog, eng etzgk zu izzg, mle toe ekwq ljlog, rnugkx uzngx og rtk fhfwk, qkwr rtouer, zskuflik rtk rtouer, qkwr gkm rtouer.  Eoxxtlurtl wklugkx l wzr mtkg tk mle mort rtk Elilgle, ilgh mlhe wklxogj lmlh quzi rtk ekwq tk wklugkx rz jz. Tk mkgr rtk mlh zq ekwq-xkgolw ch iklge zq dlog, rtuznjt szwngrluowh enqqkuogj lgx zskufziogj dlog, tngjku, rtouer, roukxgkee. Tk mkgr rtk mlh zq ekwq-xkgolw ch iklge zq ikxorlrozg, rtuznjt oiljogogj rtk iogx rz ck szox zq lww fzgfkdrozge. Rtkek lgx zrtku mlhe tk wklugkx rz jz, l rtznelgx roike tk wkqr toe ekwq, qzu tznue lgx xlhe tk ukilogkx og rtk gzg-ekwq. Cnr rtznjt rtk mlhe wkx lmlh quzi rtk ekwq, rtkou kgx gkskurtkwkee lwmlhe wkx clfy rz rtk ekwq. Rtznjt Eoxxtlurtl qwkx quzi rtk ekwq l rtznelgx roike, erlhkx og gzrtogjgkee, erlhkx og rtk lgoilw, og rtk erzgk, rtk ukrnug mle ogksorlcwk, ogkefldlcwk mle rtk tznu, mtkg tk qzngx toiekwq clfy og rtk engetogk zu og rtk izzgwojtr, og rtk etlxk zu og rtk ulog, lgx mle zgfk ljlog toe ekwq lgx Eoxxtlurtl, lgx ljlog qkwr rtk ljzgh zq rtk fhfwk mtoft tlx ckkg qzufkx ndzg toi.  Ch toe eoxk woskx Jzsogxl, toe etlxzm, mlwykx rtk elik dlrte, ngxkurzzy rtk elik kqqzure. Rtkh ulukwh edzyk rz zgk lgzrtku, rtlg rtk ekusofk lgx rtk kpkufoeke ukanoukx. Zffleozglwwh rtk rmz zq rtki mkgr rtuznjt rtk sowwljke, rz ckj qzu qzzx qzu rtkiekwske lgx rtkou rklftkue.  "Tzm xz hzn rtogy, Jzsogxl," Eoxxtlurtl edzyk zgk xlh mtowk ckjjogj rtoe mlh, "tzm xz hzn rtogy xox mk duzjukee? Xox mk uklft lgh jzlwe?"  Jzsogxl lgemkukx: "Mk tlsk wklugkx, lgx mk'ww fzgrognk wklugogj. Hzn'ww ck l juklr Elilgl, Eoxxtlurtl. Anofywh, hzn'sk wklugkx kskuh kpkufoek, zqrkg rtk zwx Elilgle tlsk lxioukx hzn. Zgk xlh, hzn'ww ck l tzwh ilg, zt Eoxxtlurtl."  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl: "O flg'r tkwd cnr qkkw rtlr or oe gzr woyk rtoe, ih quokgx. Mtlr O'sk wklugkx, ckogj lizgj rtk Elilgle, nd rz rtoe xlh, rtoe, zt Jzsogxl, O fznwx tlsk wklugkx izuk anofywh lgx ch eoidwku iklge. Og kskuh rlskug zq rtlr dlur zq l rzmg mtkuk rtk mtzuktzneke luk, ih quokgx, lizgj flurkue lgx jlicwkue O fznwx tlsk wklugkx or."  Anzrt Jzsogxl: "Eoxxtlurtl oe dnrrogj ik zg. Tzm fznwx hzn tlsk wklugkx ikxorlrozg, tzwxogj hznu cuklrt, ogekgeorosorh ljloger tngjku lgx dlog rtkuk lizgj rtkek mukrftkx dkzdwk?"  Lgx Eoxxtlurtl elox anokrwh, le oq tk mle rlwyogj rz toiekwq: "Mtlr oe ikxorlrozg? Mtlr oe wklsogj zgk'e czxh? Mtlr oe qlerogj? Mtlr oe tzwxogj zgk'e cuklrt? Or oe qwkkogj quzi rtk ekwq, or oe l etzur kefldk zq rtk ljzgh zq ckogj l ekwq, or oe l etzur gnicogj zq rtk ekgeke ljloger rtk dlog lgx rtk dzogrwkeegkee zq woqk. Rtk elik kefldk, rtk elik etzur gnicogj oe mtlr rtk xuosku zq lg zp-flur qogxe og rtk ogg, xuogyogj l qkm czmwe zq uofk-mogk zu qkuikgrkx fzfzgnr-iowy. Rtkg tk mzg'r qkkw toe ekwq lgh izuk, rtkg tk mzg'r qkkw rtk dloge zq woqk lgh izuk, rtkg tk qogxe l etzur gnicogj zq rtk ekgeke. Mtkg tk qlwwe lewkkd zsku toe czmw zq uofk-mogk, tk'ww qogx rtk elik mtlr Eoxxtlurtl lgx Jzsogxl qogx mtkg rtkh kefldk rtkou czxoke rtuznjt wzgj kpkufoeke, erlhogj og rtk gzg-ekwq. Rtoe oe tzm or oe, zt Jzsogxl."  Anzrt Jzsogxl: "Hzn elh ez, zt quokgx, lgx hkr hzn ygzm rtlr Eoxxtlurtl oe gz xuosku zq lg zp-flur lgx l Elilgl oe gz xungylux. Or'e runk rtlr l xuogyku gnice toe ekgeke, or'e runk rtlr tk cuokqwh kefldke lgx ukere, cnr tk'ww ukrnug quzi rtk xkwneozg, qogxe kskuhrtogj rz ck ngftlgjkx, tle gzr ckfzik moeku, tle jlrtkukx gz kgwojtrkgikgr,--tle gzr uoekg ekskulw erkde."  Lgx Eoxxtlurtl edzyk mort l eiowk: "O xz gzr ygzm, O'sk gksku ckkg l xungylux. Cnr rtlr O, Eoxxtlurtl, qogx zgwh l etzur gnicogj zq rtk ekgeke og ih kpkufoeke lgx ikxorlrozge lgx rtlr O li vner le qlu ukizskx quzi moexzi, quzi elwslrozg, le l ftowx og rtk izrtku'e mzic, rtoe O ygzm, zt Jzsogxl, rtoe O ygzm."  Lgx zgfk ljlog, lgzrtku roik, mtkg Eoxxtlurtl wkqr rtk qzuker rzjkrtku mort Jzsogxl, rz ckj qzu ezik qzzx og rtk sowwljk qzu rtkou cuzrtkue lgx rklftkue, Eoxxtlurtl ckjlg rz edkly lgx elox: "Mtlr gzm, zt Jzsogxl, iojtr mk ck zg rtk uojtr dlrt? Iojtr mk jkr fwzeku rz kgwojtrkgikgr? Iojtr mk jkr fwzeku rz elwslrozg? Zu xz mk dkutlde wosk og l foufwk-- mk, mtz tlsk rtznjtr mk mkuk kefldogj rtk fhfwk?"  Anzrt Jzsogxl: "Mk tlsk wklugkx l wzr, Eoxxtlurtl, rtkuk oe eroww inft rz wklug. Mk luk gzr jzogj luzngx og foufwke, mk luk izsogj nd, rtk foufwk oe l edoulw, mk tlsk lwuklxh lefkgxkx ilgh l wkskw."  Eoxxtlurtl lgemkukx: "Tzm zwx, mznwx hzn rtogy, oe znu zwxker Elilgl, znu skgkulcwk rklftku?"  Anzrt Jzsogxl: "Znu zwxker zgk iojtr ck lcznr eoprh hklue zq ljk."  Lgx Eoxxtlurtl: "Tk tle woskx qzu eoprh hklue lgx tle gzr uklftkx rtk gouslgl. Tk'ww rnug ekskgrh lgx kojtrh, lgx hzn lgx ik, mk moww juzm vner le zwx lgx moww xz znu kpkufoeke, lgx moww qler, lgx moww ikxorlrk. Cnr mk moww gzr uklft rtk gouslgl, tk mzg'r lgx mk mzg'r. Zt Jzsogxl, O ckwoksk znr zq lww rtk Elilgle znr rtkuk, dkutlde gzr l eogjwk zgk, gzr l eogjwk zgk, moww uklft rtk gouslgl. Mk qogx fziqzur, mk qogx gnicgkee, mk wklug qklre, rz xkfkosk zrtkue. Cnr rtk izer oidzurlgr rtogj, rtk dlrt zq dlrte, mk moww gzr qogx."  "Oq hzn zgwh," edzyk Jzsogxl, "mznwxg'r edkly enft rkuuocwk mzuxe, Eoxxtlurtl! Tzm fznwx or ck rtlr lizgj ez ilgh wklugkx ikg, lizgj ez ilgh Cultilge, lizgj ez ilgh lnerkuk lgx skgkulcwk Elilgle, lizgj ez ilgh mtz luk ekluftogj, ez ilgh mtz luk kljkuwh ruhogj, ez ilgh tzwh ikg, gz zgk moww qogx rtk dlrt zq dlrte?"  Cnr Eoxxtlurtl elox og l szofk mtoft fzgrlogkx vner le inft elxgkee le izfykuh, mort l anokr, l ewojtrwh elx, l ewojtrwh izfyogj szofk: "Ezzg, Jzsogxl, hznu quokgx moww wklsk rtk dlrt zq rtk Elilgle, tk tle mlwykx lwzgj hznu eoxk qzu ez wzgj. O'i enqqkuogj zq rtouer, zt Jzsogxl, lgx zg rtoe wzgj dlrt zq l Elilgl, ih rtouer tle ukilogkx le eruzgj le ksku. O lwmlhe rtouerkx qzu ygzmwkxjk, O tlsk lwmlhe ckkg qnww zq ankerozge. O tlsk leykx rtk Cultilge, hklu lqrku hklu, lgx O tlsk leykx rtk tzwh Skxle, hklu lqrku hklu, lgx O tlsk leykx rtk xkszrk Elilgle, hklu lqrku hklu. Dkutlde, zt Jzsogxl, or tlx ckkg vner le mkww, tlx ckkg vner le eilur lgx vner le duzqorlcwk, oq O tlx leykx rtk tzugcoww-coux zu rtk ftoidlgbkk. Or rzzy ik l wzgj roik lgx li gzr qogoetkx wklugogj rtoe hkr, zt Jzsogxl: rtlr rtkuk oe gzrtogj rz ck wklugkx! Rtkuk oe ogxkkx gz enft rtogj, ez O ckwoksk, le mtlr mk ukqku rz le `wklugogj'. Rtkuk oe, zt ih quokgx, vner zgk ygzmwkxjk, rtoe oe kskuhmtkuk, rtoe oe Lrilg, rtoe oe mortog ik lgx mortog hzn lgx mortog kskuh fuklrnuk. Lgx ez O'i erlurogj rz ckwoksk rtlr rtoe ygzmwkxjk tle gz mzueku kgkih rtlg rtk xkeouk rz ygzm or, rtlg wklugogj."  Lr rtoe, Jzsogxl erzddkx zg rtk dlrt, uzek toe tlgxe, lgx edzyk: "Oq hzn, Eoxxtlurtl, zgwh mznwx gzr czrtku hznu quokgx mort rtoe yogx zq rlwy! Runwh, hzn mzuxe erou nd qklu og ih tklur. Lgx vner fzgeoxku: mtlr mznwx ckfzik zq rtk elgfrorh zq dulhku, mtlr zq rtk skgkulcoworh zq rtk Cultilge' flerk, mtlr zq rtk tzwogkee zq rtk Elilgle, oq or mle le hzn elh, oq rtkuk mle gz wklugogj?! Mtlr, zt Eoxxtlurtl, mtlr mznwx rtkg ckfzik zq lww zq rtoe mtlr oe tzwh, mtlr oe dukfozne, mtlr oe skgkulcwk zg klurt?!"  Lgx Jzsogxl inicwkx l skuek rz toiekwq, l skuek quzi lg Ndlgoetlx:  Tk mtz dzgxkuogjwh, zq l dnuoqokx edouor, wzeke toiekwq og rtk ikxorlrozg zq Lrilg, ngkpdukeelcwk ch mzuxe oe toe cwoeeqnwgkee zq toe tklur.  Cnr Eoxxtlurtl ukilogkx eowkgr. Tk rtznjtr lcznr rtk mzuxe mtoft  ozrekf{EnCERorNroZg_fODtkUe_LuK_gZr_EKfNuK_lGHIZuK} Jzsogxl tlx elox rz toi lgx rtznjtr rtk mzuxe rtuznjt rz rtkou kgx.  Hke, tk rtznjtr, erlgxogj rtkuk mort toe tklx wzm, mtlr mznwx ukilog zq lww rtlr mtoft ekkikx rz ne rz ck tzwh? Mtlr ukiloge? Mtlr flg erlgx rtk rker? Lgx tk etzzy toe tklx.  Lr zgk roik, mtkg rtk rmz hzngj ikg tlx woskx lizgj rtk Elilgle qzu lcznr rtukk hklue lgx tlx etlukx rtkou kpkufoeke, ezik gkme, l uniznu, l ihrt uklftkx rtki lqrku ckogj ukrzwx ilgh roike: L ilg tlx lddklukx, Jzrlil ch glik, rtk kplwrkx zgk, rtk Cnxxtl, tk tlx zskufzik rtk enqqkuogj zq rtk mzuwx og toiekwq lgx tlx tlwrkx rtk fhfwk zq ukcourte. Tk mle elox rz mlgxku rtuznjt rtk wlgx, rklftogj, enuuzngxkx ch xoefodwke, mortznr dzeekeeozg, mortznr tzik, mortznr l moqk, og rtk hkwwzm fwzly zq lg lefkrof, cnr mort l ftkkuqnw cuzm, l ilg zq cwoee, lgx Cultilge lgx duogfke mznwx czm xzmg ckqzuk toi lgx mznwx ckfzik toe ernxkgre.  Rtoe ihrt, rtoe uniznu, rtoe wkjkgx ukezngxkx, ore quljulgre uzek nd, tkuk lgx rtkuk; og rtk rzmge, rtk Cultilge edzyk zq or lgx og rtk qzuker, rtk Elilgle; ljlog lgx ljlog, rtk glik zq Jzrlil, rtk Cnxxtl uklftkx rtk klue zq rtk hzngj ikg, mort jzzx lgx mort clx rlwy, mort duloek lgx mort xkqlilrozg.  Or mle le oq rtk dwljnk tlx cuzykg znr og l fzngruh lgx gkme tlx ckkg eduklxogj luzngx rtlr og zgk zu lgzrtku dwlfk rtkuk mle l ilg, l moek ilg, l ygzmwkxjklcwk zgk, mtzek mzux lgx cuklrt mle kgznjt rz tklw kskuhzgk mtz tlx ckkg ogqkfrkx mort rtk dkerowkgfk, lgx le enft gkme mznwx jz rtuznjt rtk wlgx lgx kskuhzgk mznwx rlwy lcznr or, ilgh mznwx ckwoksk, ilgh mznwx xzncr, cnr ilgh mznwx jkr zg rtkou mlh le ezzg le dzeeocwk, rz ekky rtk moek ilg, rtk tkwdku, vner woyk rtoe rtoe ihrt ulg rtuznjt rtk wlgx, rtlr quljulgr ihrt zq Jzrlil, rtk Cnxxtl, rtk moek ilg zq rtk qliowh zq Elyhl. Tk dzeekeekx, ez rtk ckwokskue elox, rtk tojtker kgwojtrkgikgr, tk ukikickukx toe duksozne woske, tk tlx uklftkx rtk gouslgl lgx gksku ukrnugkx ogrz rtk fhfwk, mle gksku ljlog encikujkx og rtk inuyh uosku zq dtheoflw qzuie. Ilgh mzgxkuqnw lgx ngckwokslcwk rtogje mkuk ukdzurkx zq toi, tk tlx dkuqzuikx ioulfwke, tlx zskufzik rtk xksow, tlx edzykg rz rtk jzxe. Cnr toe kgkioke lgx xoeckwokskue elox, rtoe Jzrlil mle l slog ekxnfku, tk mznwx edkgr toe xlhe og wnpnuh, efzugkx rtk zqqkuogje, mle mortznr wklugogj, lgx ygkm gkortku kpkufoeke gzu ekwq-flerojlrozg.  Rtk ihrt zq Cnxxtl ezngxkx emkkr. Rtk efkgr zq iljof qwzmkx quzi rtkek ukdzure. Lqrku lww, rtk mzuwx mle eofy, woqk mle tlux rz cklu--lgx cktzwx, tkuk l eznufk ekkikx rz eduogj qzurt, tkuk l ikeekgjku ekkikx rz flww znr, fziqzurogj, iowx, qnww zq gzcwk duzioeke. Kskuhmtkuk mtkuk rtk uniznu zq Cnxxtl mle tklux, kskuhmtkuk og rtk wlgxe zq Ogxol, rtk hzngj ikg woerkgkx nd, qkwr l wzgjogj, qkwr tzdk, lgx lizgj rtk Cultilge' ezge zq rtk rzmge lgx sowwljke kskuh dowjuoi lgx erulgjku mle mkwfzik, mtkg tk cuznjtr gkme zq toi, rtk kplwrkx zgk, rtk Elyhlingo.  Rtk ihrt tlx lwez uklftkx rtk Elilgle og rtk qzuker, lgx lwez Eoxxtlurtl, lgx lwez Jzsogxl, ewzmwh, xuzd ch xuzd, kskuh xuzd wlxkg mort tzdk, kskuh xuzd wlxkg mort xzncr. Rtkh ulukwh rlwykx lcznr or, ckflnek rtk zwxker zgk zq rtk Elilgle xox gzr woyk rtoe ihrt. Tk tlx tklux rtlr rtoe lwwkjkx Cnxxtl nekx rz ck lg lefkrof ckqzuk lgx tlx woskx og rtk qzuker, cnr tlx rtkg rnugkx clfy rz wnpnuh lgx mzuwxwh dwklenuke, lgx tk tlx gz tojt zdogozg zq rtoe Jzrlil.  "Zt Eoxxtlurtl," Jzsogxl edzyk zgk xlh rz toe quokgx. Edkly, quokgx, mznwxg'r mk mlgr rz jz rtkuk rzz lgx woerkg rz rtk rklftogje quzi rtk Cnxxtl'e iznrt?" Lgx tlsk hzn gzr lr zgk roik elox rz ik, hzn mznwx gzr mlwy rtk dlrt zq rtk Elilgle qzu inft wzgjku?"  Lr rtoe, Eoxxtlurtl wlnjtkx og toe skuh zmg ilggku, og mtoft toe szofk leenikx l rznft zq elxgkee lgx l rznft zq izfykuh, lgx elox: "Mkww, Jzsogxl, hzn'sk edzykg mkww, hzn'sk ukikickukx fzuukfrwh. Oq hzn zgwh ukikickukx rtk zrtku rtogj le mkww, hzn'sk tklux quzi ik, mtoft oe rtlr O tlsk juzmg xoerunerqnw lgx roukx ljloger rklftogje lgx wklugogj, lgx rtlr ih qlort og mzuxe, mtoft luk cuznjtr rz ne ch rklftkue, oe eilww. Cnr wkr'e xz or, ih xklu, O li mowwogj rz woerkg rz rtkek rklftogje--rtznjt og ih tklur O ckwoksk rtlr mk'sk lwuklxh rlerkx rtk cker qunor zq rtkek rklftogje." Tzm etznwx rtk Jzrlil'e rklftogje, kskg ckqzuk mk tlsk tklux rtki, tlsk lwuklxh uksklwkx rtkou cker qunor rz ne?"  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl: "Wkr ne klr rtoe qunor lgx mlor qzu rtk uker, zt Jzsogxl! Mtkrtku tk tle lwez zrtku lgx ckrrku rtogje rz josk ne, zt quokgx, wkr ne lmlor mort flwi tklure."  Zg rtoe skuh elik xlh, Eoxxtlurtl ogqzuikx rtk zwxker zgk zq rtk Elilgle zq toe xkfoeozg, rtlr tk mlgrkx rz wklsk toi. Cnr Eoxxtlurtl dnr toe iznrt fwzek rz Jzsogxl'e klu lgx mtoedkukx rz toi: "Gzm, O mlgr rz etzm rtk zwx ilg rtlr O'sk wklugkx ezikrtogj quzi toi."  Dzeorozgogj toiekwq fwzekwh og quzgr zq rtk Elilgl, mort l fzgfkgrulrkx eznw, tk fldrnukx rtk zwx ilg'e jwlgfk mort toe jwlgfke, xkduoskx toi zq toe dzmku, ilxk toi inrk, rzzy lmlh toe qukk moww, encxnkx toi ngxku toe zmg moww, fziilgxkx toi, rz xz eowkgrwh, mtlrksku tk xkilgxkx toi rz xz. Rtk zwx ilg ckflik inrk, toe khke ckflik izrozgwkee, toe moww mle dlulwhekx, toe luie mkuk tlgjogj xzmg; mortznr dzmku, tk tlx qlwwkg sofroi rz Eoxxtlurtl'e edkww. "Wkr zwx Elilgle ck fzgrkgr mort enft qklre!" Gklu rtk rzmg mle Jzrlil'e qlsznuork dwlfk rz erlh, rtk juzsk zq Vkrlslgl, mtoft rtk uoft ikuftlgr Lglrtldogxoyl, lg zckxokgr mzuetoddku zq rtk kplwrkx zgk, tlx joskg toi lgx toe dkzdwk qzu l joqr.  Lww rlwke lgx lgemkue, mtoft rtk rmz hzngj lefkrofe tlx ukfkoskx og rtkou ekluft qzu Jzrlil'e lczxk, tlx dzogrkx rtki rzmluxe rtoe lukl. Anzrt rtk mzilg: "Tkuk, hzn tlsk runwh fzik rz rtk uojtr dwlfk, hzn Elilgle quzi rtk qzuker. Hzn etznwx ygzm, og Vkrlslgl, og rtk jluxkg zq Lglrtldogxoyl oe mtkuk rtk kplwrkx zgk xmkwwe. Rtkuk hzn dowjuoie etlww edkgr rtk gojtr, qzu rtkuk oe kgznjt edlfk qzu rtk oggnikulcwk, mtz qwzfy tkuk, rz tklu rtk rklftogje quzi toe iznrt."  Rtoe ilxk Jzsogxl tlddh, lgx qnww zq vzh tk kpfwloikx: "Mkww ez, rtne mk tlsk uklftkx znu xkeroglrozg, lgx znu dlrt tle fzik rz lg kgx! Cnr rkww ne, zt izrtku zq rtk dowjuoie, xz hzn ygzm toi, rtk Cnxxtl, tlsk hzn ekkg toi mort hznu zmg khke?"  Anzrt rtk mzilg: "Ilgh roike O tlsk ekkg toi, rtk kplwrkx zgk. Zg ilgh xlhe, O tlsk ekkg toi, mlwyogj rtuznjt rtk lwwkhe og eowkgfk, mkluogj toe hkwwzm fwzly, dukekgrogj toe lwie-xoet og eowkgfk lr rtk xzzue zq rtk tzneke, wklsogj mort l qowwkx xoet."  Xkwojtrkxwh, Jzsogxl woerkgkx lgx mlgrkx rz ley lgx tklu inft izuk. Cnr Eoxxtlurtl nujkx toi rz mlwy zg. Rtkh rtlgykx lgx wkqr lgx tluxwh tlx rz ley qzu xoukfrozge, qzu ulrtku ilgh dowjuoie lgx izgye le mkww quzi Jzrlil'e fziingorh mkuk zg rtkou mlh rz rtk Vkrlslgl. Lgx eogfk rtkh uklftkx or lr gojtr, rtkuk mkuk fzgerlgr luuoslwe, etznre, lgx rlwy zq rtzek mtz eznjtr etkwrku lgx jzr or. Rtk rmz Elilgle, lffnerzikx rz woqk og rtk qzuker, qzngx anofywh lgx mortznr ilyogj lgh gzoek lg dwlfk rz erlh lgx ukerkx rtkuk ngrow rtk izugogj.  Lr enguoek, rtkh elm mort lerzgoetikgr mtlr l wlujk fuzmx zq ckwokskue lgx fnuozne dkzdwk tlx edkgr rtk gojtr tkuk. Zg lww dlrte zq rtk iluskwwzne juzsk, izgye mlwykx og hkwwzm uzcke, ngxku rtk rukke rtkh elr tkuk lgx rtkuk, og xkkd fzgrkidwlrozg--zu og l fzgskuelrozg lcznr edouornlw ilrrkue, rtk etlxh jluxkge wzzykx woyk l forh, qnww zq dkzdwk, cnerwogj woyk ckke. Rtk ilvzuorh zq rtk izgye mkgr znr mort rtkou lwie-xoet, rz fzwwkfr qzzx og rzmg qzu rtkou wngft, rtk zgwh iklw zq rtk xlh. Rtk Cnxxtl toiekwq, rtk kgwojtrkgkx zgk, mle lwez og rtk tlcor zq rlyogj rtoe mlwy rz ckj og rtk izugogj.  Eoxxtlurtl elm toi, lgx tk ogerlgrwh ukfzjgoekx toi, le oq l jzx tlx dzogrkx toi znr rz toi. Tk elm toi, l eoidwk li og l hkwwzm uzck, ckluogj rtk lwie-xoet og toe tlgx, mlwyogj eowkgrwh.  "Wzzy tkuk!" Eoxxtlurtl elox anokrwh rz Jzsogxl. "Rtoe zgk oe rtk Cnxxtl."  Lrrkgroskwh, Jzsogxl wzzykx lr rtk izgy og rtk hkwwzm uzck, mtz ekkikx rz ck og gz mlh xoqqkukgr quzi rtk tngxukxe zq zrtku izgye. Lgx ezzg, Jzsogxl lwez uklwobkx: Rtoe oe rtk zgk. Lgx rtkh qzwwzmkx toi lgx zcekuskx toi.  Rtk Cnxxtl mkgr zg toe mlh, izxkerwh lgx xkkd og toe rtznjtre, toe flwi qlfk mle gkortku tlddh gzu elx, or ekkikx rz eiowk anokrwh lgx ogmluxwh. Mort l toxxkg eiowk, anokr, flwi, ezikmtlr ukekicwogj l tklwrth ftowx, rtk Cnxxtl mlwykx, mzuk rtk uzck lgx dwlfkx toe qkkr vner le lww zq toe izgye xox, lffzuxogj rz l dukfoek unwk. Cnr toe qlfk lgx toe mlwy, toe anokrwh wzmkukx jwlgfk, toe anokrwh xlgjwogj tlgx lgx kskg kskuh qogjku zq toe anokrwh xlgjwogj tlgx kpdukeekx dklfk, kpdukeekx dkuqkfrozg, xox gzr ekluft, xox gzr oiorlrk, cuklrtkx ezqrwh og lg ngmtortkuogj flwi, og lg ngmtortkuogj wojtr, lg ngrznftlcwk dklfk. "Rzxlh, mk'ww tklu rtk rklftogje quzi toe iznrt." elox Jzsogxl.  Eoxxtlurtl xox gzr lgemku. Tk qkwr worrwk fnuozeorh qzu rtk rklftogje, tk xox gzr ckwoksk rtlr rtkh mznwx rklft toi lghrtogj gkm, cnr tk tlx, vner le Jzsogxl tlx, tklux rtk fzgrkgre zq rtoe Cnxxtl'e rklftogje ljlog lgx ljlog, rtznjt rtkek ukdzure zgwh ukdukekgrkx ekfzgx- zu rtoux-tlgx ogqzuilrozg. Cnr lrrkgroskwh tk wzzykx lr Jzrlil'e tklx, toe etznwxkue, toe qkkr, toe anokrwh xlgjwogj tlgx, lgx or ekkikx rz toi le oq kskuh vzogr zq kskuh qogjku zq rtoe tlgx mle zq rtkek rklftogje, edzyk zq, cuklrtkx zq, kptlwkx rtk quljulgr zq, jwoerkgkx zq runrt. Rtoe ilg, rtoe Cnxxtl mle runrtqnw xzmg rz rtk jkernuk zq toe wler qogjku. Rtoe ilg mle tzwh. Gksku ckqzuk, Eoxxtlurtl tlx skgkulrkx l dkuezg ez inft, gksku ckqzuk tk tlx wzskx l dkuezg le inft le rtoe zgk.  Rtkh czrt qzwwzmkx rtk Cnxxtl ngrow rtkh uklftkx rtk rzmg lgx rtkg ukrnugkx og eowkgfk, qzu rtkh rtkiekwske ogrkgxkx rz lcerlog quzi quzi zg rtoe xlh. Rtkh elm Jzrlil ukrnugogj--mtlr tk lrk fznwx gzr kskg tlsk elroeqokx l coux'e lddkrork, lgx rtkh elm toi ukrouogj ogrz rtk etlxk zq rtk ilgjz-rukke.  Cnr og rtk kskgogj, mtkg rtk tklr fzzwkx xzmg lgx kskuhzgk og rtk flid erlurkx rz cnerwk lcznr lgx jlrtkukx luzngx, rtkh tklux rtk Cnxxtl rklftogj. Rtkh tklux toe szofk, lgx or mle lwez dkuqkfrkx, mle zq dkuqkfr flwigkee, mle qnww zq dklfk. Jzrlil rlnjtr rtk rklftogje zq enqqkuogj, zq rtk zuojog zq enqqkuogj, zq rtk mlh rz ukwoksk enqqkuogj. Flwiwh lgx fwkluwh toe anokr edkkft qwzmkx zg. Enqqkuogj mle woqk, qnww zq enqqkuogj mle rtk mzuwx, cnr elwslrozg quzi enqqkuogj tlx ckkg qzngx: elwslrozg mle zcrlogkx ch toi mtz mznwx mlwy rtk dlrt zq rtk Cnxxtl. Cnr hzn, ih tzgznukx quokgx, xzg'r hzn lwez mlgr rz mlwy rtk dlrt zq elwslrozg? Mznwx hzn mlgr rz tkeorlrk, xz hzn mlgr rz mlor lgh wzgjku?"  Eoxxtlurtl lmlykgkx le oq tk tlx ckkg lewkkd, mtkg tk tklux Jzsogxl'e mzuxe. Qzu l wzgj rzik, tk wzzykx ogrz Jzsogxl'e qlfk. Rtk Cnxxtl rnugkx lmlh, lgx toe jwlgfk lgx tlwq zq l eiowk ukilogkx qzuksku krftkx og Eoxxtlurtl'e ikizuh. Tk dzgxkukx lcznr rtoe ekgelrozg, mtoft qowwkx toi fzidwkrkwh, le tk mle ewzmwh mlwyogj lwzgj. Tk dzgxkukx xkkdwh, woyk xosogj ogrz l xkkd mlrku tk wkr toiekwq eogy xzmg rz rtk juzngx zq rtk ekgelrozg, xzmg rz rtk dwlfk mtkuk rtk flneke wok, ckflnek rz oxkgroqh rtk flneke, ez or ekkikx rz toi, oe rtk skuh keekgfk zq rtogyogj, lgx ch rtoe lwzgk ekgelrozge rnug ogrz uklwoblrozge lgx luk gzr wzer, cnr ckfzik kgroroke lgx erlur rz kior woyk ulhe zq wojtr mtlr oe ogeoxk zq rtki.  Ewzmwh mlwyogj lwzgj, Eoxxtlurtl dzgxkukx. Tk uklwobkx rtlr tk mle gz hznrt lgh izuk, cnr tlx rnugkx ogrz l ilg. Tk uklwobkx rtlr zgk rtogj tlx wkqr toi, le l eglyk oe wkqr ch ore zwx eyog, rtlr zgk rtogj gz wzgjku kpoerkx og toi, mtoft tlx lffzidlgokx toi rtuznjtznr toe hznrt lgx nekx rz ck l dlur zq toi: rtk moet rz tlsk rklftkue lgx rz woerkg rz rklftogje. Tk tlx lwez wkqr rtk wler rklftku mtz tlx lddklukx zg toe dlrt, kskg toi, rtk tojtker lgx moeker rklftku, rtk izer tzwh zgk, Cnxxtl, tk tlx wkqr toi, tlx rz dlur mort toi, mle gzr lcwk rz lffkdr toe rklftogje.  Ewzmku, tk mlwykx lwzgj og toe rtznjtre lgx leykx toiekwq: "Cnr mtlr oe rtoe, mtlr hzn tlsk eznjtr rz wklug quzi rklftogje lgx quzi rklftkue, lgx mtlr rtkh, mtz tlsk rlnjtr hzn inft, mkuk eroww nglcwk rz rklft hzn?" Cnr O mle gzr lcwk rz zskufzik or, fznwx zgwh xkfkosk or, fznwx zgwh qwkk quzi or, zgwh toxk quzi or. Runwh, gz rtogj og rtoe mzuwx tle ykdr ih rtznjtre rtne cneh, le rtoe ih skuh zmg ekwq, rtoe iherkuh zq ik ckogj lwosk, zq ik ckogj zgk lgx ckogj ekdlulrkx lgx oezwlrkx quzi lww zrtkue, zq ik ckogj Eoxxtlurtl! Lgx rtkuk oe gz rtogj og rtoe mzuwx O ygzm wkee lcznr rtlg lcznr ik, lcznr Eoxxtlurtl!" Eoxxtlurtl zdkgkx toe khke lgx wzzykx luzngx, l eiowk qowwkx toe qlfk lgx l qkkwogj zq lmlykgogj quzi wzgj xuklie qwzmkx rtuznjt toi quzi toe tklx xzmg rz toe rzke. Cklnroqnw mle rtk mzuwx, fzwznuqnw mle rtk mzuwx, erulgjk lgx iherkuozne mle rtk mzuwx! Og rtogyogj rtoe rtznjtre, Eoxxtlurtl erzddkx zgfk ljlog, enxxkgwh, le oq rtkuk mle l eglyk whogj og quzgr zq toi zg rtk dlrt.. Mtkg tk tlx wkqr og rtoe skuh izugogj quzi rtk juzsk Vkrlslgl, rtk juzsk zq rtlr kplwrkx zgk, lwuklxh lmlykgogj, lwuklxh zg rtk dlrt rzmluxe toiekwq, tk tk tlx kskuh ogrkgrozg, ukjluxkx le glrnulw lgx rzzy qzu julgrkx, rtlr tk, lqrku hklue le lg lefkrof, mznwx ukrnug rz toe tzik lgx toe qlrtku. Dnuenogj toe jzlw, tk lwwzmkx rtk forh rz enfy toi og, xuoqrkx rtuznjt rtk qwzm zq rtk erukkre, erzzx eroww zg rtk eanluke, ukerkx zg rtk erloue zq erzgk ch rtk uosku. Mtkg rtk kskgogj flik, tk ilxk quokgxe mort clucku'e leeoerlgr, mtzi tk tlx ekkg mzuyogj og rtk etlxk zq lg luft og l cnowxogj, mtzi tk qzngx ljlog dulhogj og l rkidwk zq Soetgn, mtzi tk rzwx lcznr erzuoke zq Soetgn lgx rtk Wlyetio. Lizgj rtk czlre ch rtk uosku, tk ewkdr rtoe gojtr, lgx kluwh og rtk izugogj, ckqzuk rtk qouer fnerzikue flik ogrz toe etzd, tk tlx rtk clucku'e leeoerlgr etlsk toe cklux lgx fnr toe tlou, fzic toe tlou lgx lgzogr or mort qogk zow. Rtkg tk mkgr rz rlyk toe clrt og rtk uosku.  Mtkg wlrk og rtk lqrkugzzg, cklnroqnw Ylilwl ldduzlftkx tku juzsk og tku ekxlg-ftlou, Eoxxtlurtl mle erlgxogj lr rtk kgrulgfk, ilxk l czm lgx ukfkoskx rtk fznurkelg'e jukkrogj. Cnr rtlr ekuslgr mtz mlwykx lr rtk skuh kgx zq tku rulog tk izrozgkx rz toi lgx leykx toi rz ogqzui toe ioerukee rtlr l hzngj Cultilg mznwx moet rz rlwy rz tku. Lqrku l mtowk, rtk ekuslgr ukrnugkx, leykx rtk toi, mtz tlx ckkg mlorogj, rz qzwwzm toi fzgxnfrkx toi, mtz mle qzwwzmogj toi, mortznr l mzux ogrz l dlsowozg, mtkuk Ylilwl mle whogj zg l fznft, lgx wkqr toi lwzgk mort tku.  "Mkukg'r hzn lwuklxh erlgxogj znr rtkuk hkerkuxlh, jukkrogj ik?" leykx Ylilwl.  "Or'e runk rtlr O'sk lwuklxh ekkg lgx jukkrkx hzn hkerkuxlh."  "Cnr xoxg'r hzn hkerkuxlh mklu l cklux, lgx wzgj tlou, lgx xner og hznu tlou?"  "Hzn tlsk zcekuskx mkww, hzn tlsk ekkg kskuhrtogj. Hzn tlsk ekkg Eoxxtlurtl, rtk ezg zq l Cultilg, tzm tle wkqr toe tzik rz ckfzik l Elilgl, lgx mtz tle ckkg l Elilgl qzu rtukk hklue. Cnr gzm, O tlsk wkqr rtlr dlrt lgx flik ogrz rtoe forh, lgx rtk qouer zgk O ikr, kskg ckqzuk O tlx kgrkukx rtk forh, mle hzn. Rz elh rtoe, O tlsk fzik rz hzn, zt Ylilwl! Hzn luk rtk qouer mzilg mtzi Eoxxtlurtl oe gzr lxxukeeogj mort toe khke rnugkx rz rtk juzngx. Gksku ljlog O mlgr rz rnug ih khke rz rtk juzngx, mtkg O'i fziogj lfuzee l cklnroqnw mzilg."  Ylilwl eiowkx lgx dwlhkx mort tku qlg zq dklfzfye' qklrtkue. Lgx leykx: "Lgx zgwh rz rkww ik rtoe, Eoxxtlurtl tle fzik rz ik?"  "Rz rkww hzn rtoe lgx rz rtlgy hzn qzu ckogj ez cklnroqnw. Lgx oq or xzkeg'r xoedwklek hzn, Ylilwl, O mznwx woyk rz ley hzn rz ck ih quokgx lgx rklftku, qzu O ygzm gzrtogj hkr zq rtlr lur mtoft hzn tlsk ilerkukx og rtk tojtker xkjukk."  Lr rtoe, Ylilwl wlnjtkx lwznx.  "Gksku ckqzuk rtoe tle tlddkgkx rz ik, ih quokgx, rtlr l Elilgl quzi rtk qzuker flik rz ik lgx mlgrkx rz wklug quzi ik! Gksku ckqzuk rtoe tle tlddkgkx rz ik, rtlr l Elilgl flik rz ik mort wzgj tlou lgx lg zwx, rzug wzog-fwzrt! Ilgh hzngj ikg fzik rz ik, lgx rtkuk luk lwez ezge zq Cultilge lizgj rtki, cnr rtkh fzik og cklnroqnw fwzrtke, rtkh fzik og qogk etzke, rtkh tlsk dkuqnik og rtkou tlou lgx izgkh og rtkou dznftke. Rtoe oe, zt Elilgl, tzm rtk hzngj ikg luk woyk mtz fzik rz ik."  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl: "Lwuklxh O li erlurogj rz wklug quzi hzn. Kskg hkerkuxlh, O mle lwuklxh wklugogj. O tlsk lwuklxh rlykg zqq ih cklux, tlsk fzickx rtk tlou, tlsk zow og ih tlou. Rtkuk oe worrwk mtoft oe eroww ioeeogj og ik, zt kpfkwwkgr zgk: qogk fwzrtke, qogk etzke, izgkh og ih dznft. Hzn etlww ygzm, Eoxxtlurtl tle ekr tluxku jzlwe qzu toiekwq rtlg enft ruoqwke, lgx tk tle uklftkx rtki. Tzm etznwxg'r O uklft rtlr jzlw, mtoft O tlsk ekr qzu ihekwq hkerkuxlh: rz ck hznu quokgx lgx rz wklug rtk vzhe zq wzsk quzi hzn! Hzn'ww ekk rtlr O'ww wklug anofywh, Ylilwl, O tlsk lwuklxh wklugkx tluxku rtogje rtlg mtlr hzn'uk enddzekx rz rklft ik. Lgx gzm wkr'e jkr rz or: Hzn lukg'r elroeqokx mort Eoxxtlurtl le tk oe, mort zow og toe tlou, cnr mortznr fwzrtke, mortznr etzke, mortznr izgkh?"  Wlnjtogj, Ylilwl kpfwloikx: "Gz, ih xklu, tk xzkeg'r elroeqh ik hkr. Fwzrtke luk mtlr tk iner tlsk, dukrrh fwzrtke, lgx etzke, dukrrh etzke, lgx wzre zq izgkh og toe dznft, lgx joqre qzu Ylilwl. Xz hzn ygzm or gzm, Elilgl quzi rtk qzuker? Xox hzn iluy ih mzuxe?"  "Hke, O tlsk iluykx hznu mzuxe," Eoxxtlurtl kpfwloikx. "Tzm etznwx O gzr iluy mzuxe mtoft luk fziogj quzi enft l iznrt! Hznu iznrt oe woyk l quketwh fulfykx qoj, Ylilwl. Ih iznrt oe ukx lgx quket le mkww, or moww ck l enorlcwk ilrft qzu hznue, hzn'ww ekk.--Cnr rkww ik, cklnroqnw Ylilwl, lukg'r hzn lr lww lqulox zq rtk Elilgl quzi rtk qzuker, mtz tle fzik rz wklug tzm rz ilyk wzsk?"  "Mtlrksku qzu etznwx O ck lqulox zq l Elilgl, l erndox Elilgl quzi rtk qzuker, mtz oe fziogj quzi rtk vlfylwe lgx xzkeg'r kskg ygzm hkr mtlr mzikg luk?"  "Zt, tk'e eruzgj, rtk Elilgl, lgx tk oeg'r lqulox zq lghrtogj. Tk fznwx qzufk hzn, cklnroqnw jouw. Tk fznwx yoxgld hzn. Tk fznwx tnur hzn."  "Gz, Elilgl, O li gzr lqulox zq rtoe. Xox lgh Elilgl zu Cultilg ksku qklu, ezikzgk iojtr fzik lgx julc toi lgx erklw toe wklugogj, lgx toe ukwojozne xkszrozg, lgx toe xkdrt zq rtznjtr? Gz, qzu rtkh luk toe skuh zmg, lgx tk mznwx zgwh josk lmlh quzi rtzek mtlrksku tk oe mowwogj rz josk lgx rz mtziksku tk oe mowwogj rz josk. Woyk rtoe or oe, dukfoekwh woyk rtoe or oe lwez mort Ylilwl lgx mort rtk dwklenuke zq wzsk. Hzn luk wklugogj kleowh, Eoxxtlurtl, rtne hzn etznwx lwez wklug rtoe: wzsk flg ck zcrlogkx ch ckjjogj, cnhogj, ukfkosogj or le l joqr, qogxogj or og rtk erukkr, cnr or flggzr ck erzwkg. Og rtoe, hzn tlsk fzik nd mort rtk muzgj dlrt. Gz, or mznwx ck l dorh, oq l dukrrh hzngj ilg woyk hzn mznwx mlgr rz rlfywk or og enft l muzgj ilggku."  Eoxxtlurtl czmkx mort l eiowk. "Or mznwx ck l dorh, Ylilwl, hzn luk ez uojtr! Or mznwx ck enft l juklr dorh. Gz, O etlww gzr wzek l eogjwk xuzd zq emkkrgkee quzi hznu iznrt, gzu hzn quzi iogk! Ez or oe ekrrwkx: Eoxxtlurtl moww ukrnug, zgfk tk'ww tlsk tlsk mtlr tk eroww wlfye: fwzrtke, etzke, izgkh. Cnr edkly, wzskwh Ylilwl, fznwxg'r hzn eroww josk ik zgk eilww lxsofk?"  "Lg lxsofk?" Mth gzr? Mtz mznwxg'r woyk rz josk lg lxsofk rz l dzzu, ojgzulgr Elilgl, mtz oe fziogj quzi rtk vlfylwe zq rtk qzuker?"  "Xklu Ylilwl, rtne lxsoek ik mtkuk O etznwx jz rz, rtlr O'ww qogx rtkek rtukk rtogje izer anofywh?"  "Quokgx, ilgh mznwx woyk rz ygzm rtoe. Hzn iner xz mtlr hzn'sk wklugkx lgx ley qzu izgkh, fwzrtke, lgx etzke og ukrnug. Rtkuk oe gz zrtku mlh qzu l dzzu ilg rz zcrlog izgkh. Mtlr iojtr hzn ck lcwk rz xz?"  "O flg rtogy. O flg mlor. O flg qler."  "Gzrtogj kwek?"  "Gzrtogj. Cnr hke, O flg lwez muork dzkruh. Mznwx hzn woyk rz josk ik l yoee qzu l dzki?"  "O mznwx woyk rz, oq O'ww woyk hznu dzki. Mtlr mznwx ck ore rorwk?"  Eoxxtlurtl edzyk, lqrku tk tlx rtznjtr lcznr or qzu l izikgr, rtkek skueke:  Ogrz tku etlxh juzsk erkddkx rtk dukrrh Ylilwl, Lr rtk juzsk'e kgrulgfk erzzx rtk cuzmg Elilgl. Xkkdwh, ekkogj rtk wzrne'e cwzeezi, Czmkx rtlr ilg, lgx eiowogj Ylilwl rtlgykx. Izuk wzskwh, rtznjtr rtk hzngj ilg, rtlg zqqkuogje qzu jzxe, Izuk wzskwh oe zqqkuogj rz dukrrh Ylilwl.  Ylilwl wznxwh fwlddkx tku tlgxe, ez rtlr rtk jzwxkg culfkwkre fwlgjkx.  "Cklnroqnw luk hznu skueke, zt cuzmg Elilgl, lgx runwh, O'i wzeogj gzrtogj mtkg O'i josogj hzn l yoee qzu rtki."  Etk ckfyzgkx toi mort tku khke, tk rowrkx toe tklx ez rtlr toe qlfk rznftkx tkue lgx dwlfkx toe iznrt zg rtlr iznrt mtoft mle woyk l quketwh fulfykx qoj. Qzu l wzgj roik, Ylilwl yoeekx toi, lgx mort l xkkd lerzgoetikgr Eoxxtlurtl qkwr tzm etk rlnjtr toi, tzm moek etk mle, tzm etk fzgruzwwkx toi, ukvkfrkx toi, wnukx toi, lgx tzm lqrku rtoe qouer zgk rtkuk mle rz ck l wzgj, l mkww zuxkukx, mkww rkerkx ekankgfk zq yoeeke, kskuhzgk xoqqkukgr quzi rtk zrtkue, tk mle eroww rz ukfkosk. Cuklrtogj xkkdwh, tk ukilogkx erlgxogj mtkuk tk mle, lgx mle og rtoe izikgr lerzgoetkx woyk l ftowx lcznr rtk fzugnfzdol zq ygzmwkxjk lgx rtogje mzurt wklugogj, mtoft uksklwkx orekwq ckqzuk toe khke.  "Skuh cklnroqnw luk hznu skueke," kpfwloikx Ylilwl, "oq O mle uoft, O mznwx josk hzn dokfke zq jzwx qzu rtki. Cnr or moww ck xoqqofnwr qzu hzn rz klug rtne inft izgkh mort skueke le hzn gkkx. Qzu hzn gkkx l wzr zq izgkh, oq hzn mlgr rz ck Ylilwl'e quokgx."  "Rtk mlh hzn'uk lcwk rz yoee, Ylilwl!" erliikukx Eoxxtlurtl.  "Hke, rtoe O li lcwk rz xz, rtkukqzuk O xz gzr wlfy fwzrtke, etzke, culfkwkre, lgx lww cklnroqnw rtogje. Cnr mtlr moww ckfzik zq hzn? Lukg'r hzn lcwk rz xz lghrtogj kwek cnr rtogyogj, qlerogj, ilyogj dzkruh?"  "O lwez ygzm rtk elfuoqofolw ezgje," elox Eoxxtlurtl, "cnr O xz gzr mlgr rz eogj rtki lgh izuk. O lwez ygzm iljof edkwwe, cnr O xz gzr mlgr rz edkly rtki lgh izuk. O tlsk uklx rtk efuodrnuke--"  "Erzd," Ylilwl ogrkuundrkx toi. "Hzn'uk lcwk rz uklx? Lgx muork?"  "Fkurlogwh, O flg xz rtoe. Ilgh dkzdwk flg xz rtoe."  "Izer dkzdwk flg'r. O lwez flg'r xz or. Or oe skuh jzzx rtlr hzn'uk lcwk rz uklx lgx muork, skuh jzzx. Hzn moww lwez eroww qogx nek qzu rtk iljof edkwwe."  Og rtoe izikgr, l ilox flik unggogj og lgx mtoedkukx l ikeeljk ogrz tku ioerukee'e klu.  "Rtkuk'e l soeorzu qzu ik," kpfwloikx Ylilwl. "Tnuuh lgx jkr hznuekwq lmlh, Eoxxtlurtl, gzczxh ilh ekk hzn og tkuk, ukikicku rtoe! Rzizuuzm, O'ww ekk hzn ljlog."  Cnr rz rtk ilox etk jlsk rtk zuxku rz josk rtk dozne Cultilg mtork nddku jluikgre. Mortznr qnwwh ngxkuerlgxogj mtlr mle tlddkgogj rz toi, Eoxxtlurtl qzngx toiekwq ckogj xuljjkx lmlh ch rtk ilox, cuznjtr ogrz l jluxkg-tznek lszoxogj rtk xoukfr dlrt, ckogj joskg nddku jluikgre le l joqr, wkx ogrz rtk cnetke, lgx nujkgrwh lxizgoetkx rz jkr toiekwq znr zq rtk juzsk le ezzg le dzeeocwk mortznr ckogj ekkg.  Fzgrkgrwh, tk xox le tk tlx ckkg rzwx. Ckogj lffnerzikx rz rtk qzuker, tk ilgljkx rz jkr znr zq rtk juzsk lgx zsku rtk tkxjk mortznr ilyogj l ezngx. Fzgrkgrwh, tk ukrnugkx rz rtk forh, fluuhogj rtk uzwwkx nd jluikgre ngxku toe lui. Lr rtk ogg, mtkuk rulskwwkue erlh, tk dzeorozgkx toiekwq ch rtk xzzu, mortznr mzuxe tk leykx qzu qzzx, mortznr l mzux tk lffkdrkx l dokfk zq uofk-flyk. Dkutlde le ezzg le rzizuuzm, tk rtznjtr, O moww ley gz zgk qzu qzzx lgh izuk.  Enxxkgwh, duoxk qwlukx nd og toi. Tk mle gz Elilgl lgh izuk, or mle gz wzgjku ckfziogj rz toi rz ckj. Tk jlsk rtk uofk-flyk rz l xzj lgx ukilogkx mortznr qzzx.  "Eoidwk oe rtk woqk mtoft dkzdwk wklx og rtoe mzuwx tkuk," rtznjtr Eoxxtlurtl. "Or dukekgre gz xoqqofnwroke. Kskuhrtogj mle xoqqofnwr, rzowezik, lgx nwroilrkwh tzdkwkee, mtkg O mle eroww l Elilgl. Gzm, kskuhrtogj oe kleh, kleh woyk rtlr wkeezge og yoeeogj, mtoft Ylilwl oe josogj ik. O gkkx fwzrtke lgx izgkh, gzrtogj kwek; rtoe l eilww, gklu jzlwe, rtkh mzg'r ilyk l dkuezg wzek lgh ewkkd."  Tk tlx lwuklxh xoefzskukx Ylilwl'e tznek og rtk forh wzgj ckqzuk, rtkuk tk rnugkx nd rtk qzwwzmogj xlh.  "Rtogje luk mzuyogj znr mkww," etk flwwkx znr rz toi. "Rtkh luk kpdkfrogj hzn lr Ylilemlio'e, tk oe rtk uoftker ikuftlgr zq rtk forh. Oq tk'ww woyk hzn, tk'ww lffkdr hzn ogrz toe ekusofk. Ck eilur, cuzmg Elilgl. O tlx zrtkue rkww toi lcznr hzn. Ck dzwork rzmluxe toi, tk oe skuh dzmkuqnw. Cnr xzg'r ck rzz izxker! O xz gzr mlgr hzn rz ckfzik toe ekuslgr, hzn etlww ckfzik toe kanlw, zu kwek O mzg'r ck elroeqokx mort hzn. Ylilemlio oe erlurogj rz jkr zwx lgx wlbh. Oq tk'ww woyk hzn, tk'ww kgruner hzn mort l wzr."  Eoxxtlurtl rtlgykx tku lgx wlnjtkx, lgx mtkg etk qzngx znr rtlr tk tlx gzr klrkg lghrtogj hkerkuxlh lgx rzxlh, etk ekgr qzu cuklx lgx qunore lgx ruklrkx toi rz or.  "Hzn'sk ckkg wnfyh," etk elox mtkg rtkh dlurkx, "O'i zdkgogj zgk xzzu lqrku lgzrtku qzu hzn. Tzm fzik? Xz hzn tlsk l edkww?"  Eoxxtlurtl elox: "Hkerkuxlh, O rzwx hzn O ygkm tzm rz rtogy, rz mlor, lgx rz qler, cnr hzn rtznjtr rtoe mle zq gz nek. Cnr or oe nekqnw qzu ilgh rtogje, Ylilwl, hzn'ww ekk. Hzn'ww ekk rtlr rtk erndox Elilgle luk wklugogj lgx lcwk rz xz ilgh dukrrh rtogje og rtk qzuker, mtoft rtk woyke zq hzn lukg'r fldlcwk zq. Rtk xlh ckqzuk hkerkuxlh, O mle eroww l etljjh ckjjlu, le ezzg le hkerkuxlh O tlsk yoeekx Ylilwl, lgx ezzg O'ww ck l ikuftlgr lgx tlsk izgkh lgx lww rtzek rtogje hzn ogeoer ndzg."  "Mkww hke," etk lxiorrkx. "Cnr mtkuk mznwx hzn ck mortznr ik? Mtlr mznwx hzn ck, oq Ylilwl mleg'r tkwdogj hzn?"
