Quzi rtlr izikgr zg mtkg O tlx ilxk rtoe ukezwnrozg, O lwez ygkm rtlr O mznwx fluuh or znr. O ygkm rtlr hzn mznwx tkwd ik, lr hznu qouer jwlgfk lr rtk kgrulgfk zq rtk juzsk O lwuklxh ygkm or."  "Cnr mtlr oq O tlxg'r ckkg mowwogj?"  "Hzn mkuk mowwogj. Wzzy, Ylilwl: Mkg hzn rtuzm l uzfy ogrz rtk mlrku, or moww edkkx zg rtk qlerker fznuek rz rtk czrrzi zq rtk mlrku. Rtoe oe tzm or oe mtkg Eoxxtlurtl tle l jzlw, l ukezwnrozg. Eoxxtlurtl xzke gzrtogj, tk mlore, tk rtogye, tk qlere, cnr tk dleeke rtuznjt rtk rtogje zq rtk mzuwx woyk l uzfy rtuznjt mlrku, mortznr xzogj lghrtogj, mortznr erouuogj; tk oe xulmg, tk wkre toiekwq qlww. Toe jzlw lrrulfre toi, ckflnek tk xzkeg'r wkr lghrtogj kgrku toe eznw mtoft iojtr zddzek rtk jzlw. Rtoe oe mtlr Eoxxtlurtl tle wklugkx lizgj rtk Elilgle. Rtoe oe mtlr qzzwe flww iljof lgx zq mtoft rtkh rtogy or mznwx ck kqqkfrkx ch iklge zq rtk xlkizge. Gzrtogj oe kqqkfrkx ch xlkizge, rtkuk luk gz xlkizge. Kskuhzgk flg dkuqzui iljof, kskuhzgk flg uklft toe jzlwe, oq tk oe lcwk rz rtogy, oq tk oe lcwk rz mlor, oq tk oe lcwk rz qler."  Ylilwl woerkgkx rz toi. Etk wzskx toe szofk, etk wzskx rtk wzzy quzi toe khke.  "Dkutlde or oe ez," etk elox anokrwh, "le hzn elh, quokgx. Cnr dkutlde or oe lwez woyk rtoe: rtlr Eoxxtlurtl oe l tlgxezik ilg, rtlr toe jwlgfk dwkleke rtk mzikg, rtlr rtkukqzuk jzzx qzurngk oe fziogj rzmluxe toi."  Mor zgk yoee, Eoxxtlurtl cox toe qlukmkww. "O moet rtlr or etznwx ck rtoe mlh, ih rklftku; rtlr ih jwlgfk etlww dwklek hzn, rtlr lwmlhe jzzx qzurngk etlww fzik rz ik znr zq hznu xoukfrozg!"  MORT RTK FTOWXWOYK DKZDWK  Eoxxtlurtl mkgr rz Ylilemlio rtk ikuftlgr, tk mle xoukfrkx ogrz l uoft tznek, ekuslgre wkx toi ckrmkkg dukfozne fludkre ogrz l ftlicku, mtkuk tk lmlorkx rtk ilerku zq rtk tznek.  Ylilemlio kgrkukx, l emoqrwh, eizzrtwh izsogj ilg mort skuh julh tlou, mort skuh ogrkwwojkgr, flnrozne khke, mort l jukkxh iznrt. Dzworkwh, rtk tzer lgx rtk jnker jukkrkx zgk lgzrtku.  "O tlsk ckkg rzwx," rtk ikuftlgr ckjlg, "rtlr hzn mkuk l Cultilg, l wklugkx ilg, cnr rtlr hzn ekky rz ck og rtk ekusofk zq l ikuftlgr. Iojtr hzn tlsk ckfzik xkerornrk, Cultilg, ez rtlr hzn ekky rz ekusk?"  "Gz," elox Eoxxtlurtl, "O tlsk gzr ckfzik xkerornrk lgx tlsk gksku ckkg xkerornrk. Hzn etznwx ygzm rtlr O'i fziogj quzi rtk Elilgle, mort mtzi O tlsk woskx qzu l wzgj roik."  "Oq hzn'uk fziogj quzi rtk Elilgle, tzm fznwx hzn ck lghrtogj cnr xkerornrk? Lukg'r rtk Elilgle kgroukwh mortznr dzeekeeozge?"  "O li mortznr dzeekeeozge," elox Eoxxtlurtl, "oq rtoe oe mtlr hzn iklg. Enukwh, O li mortznr dzeekeeozge. Cnr O li ez szwngrluowh, lgx rtkukqzuk O li gzr xkerornrk."  "Cnr mtlr luk hzn dwlggogj rz wosk zq, ckogj mortznr dzeekeeozge?"  "O tlskg'r rtznjtr zq rtoe hkr, eou. Qzu izuk rtlg rtukk hklue, O tlsk ckkg mortznr dzeekeeozge, lgx tlsk gksku rtznjtr lcznr zq mtlr O etznwx wosk."  "Ez hzn'sk woskx zq rtk dzeekeeozge zq zrtkue."  "Dukenilcwk rtoe oe tzm or oe. Lqrku lww, l ikuftlgr lwez woske zq mtlr zrtku dkzdwk zmg."  "Mkww elox. Cnr tk mznwxg'r rlyk lghrtogj quzi lgzrtku dkuezg qzu gzrtogj; tk mznwx josk toe ikuftlgxoek og ukrnug."  "Ez or ekkie rz ck ogxkkx. Kskuhzgk rlyke, kskuhzgk joske, enft oe woqk."  "Cnr oq hzn xzg'r iogx ik leyogj: ckogj mortznr dzeekeeozge, mtlr mznwx hzn woyk rz josk?"  "Kskuhzgk joske mtlr tk tle. Rtk mluuozu joske erukgjrt, rtk ikuftlgr joske ikuftlgxoek, rtk rklftku rklftogje, rtk qluiku uofk, rtk qoetku qoet."  "Hke ogxkkx. Lgx mtlr oe or gzm mtlr hzn'sk jzr rz josk? Mtlr oe or rtlr hzn'sk wklugkx, mtlr hzn'uk lcwk rz xz?"  "O flg rtogy. O flg mlor. O flg qler."  "Rtlr'e kskuhrtogj?"  "O ckwoksk, rtlr'e kskuhrtogj!"  "Lgx mtlr'e rtk nek zq rtlr? Qzu kplidwk, rtk qlerogj-- mtlr oe or jzzx qzu?"  "Or oe skuh jzzx, eou. Mtkg l dkuezg tle gzrtogj rz klr, qlerogj oe rtk eilurker rtogj tk fznwx xz. Mtkg, qzu kplidwk, Eoxxtlurtl tlxg'r wklugkx rz qler, tk mznwx tlsk rz lffkdr lgh yogx zq ekusofk ckqzuk rtoe xlh oe nd, mtkrtku or ilh ck mort hzn zu mtkuksku, ckflnek tngjku mznwx qzufk toi rz xz ez. Cnr woyk rtoe, Eoxxtlurtl flg mlor flwiwh, tk ygzme gz oidlrokgfk, tk ygzme gz kikujkgfh, qzu l wzgj roik tk flg lwwzm tngjku rz ckeokjk toi lgx flg wlnjt lcznr or. Rtoe, eou, oe mtlr qlerogj oe jzzx qzu."  "Hzn'uk uojtr, Elilgl. Mlor qzu l izikgr."  Ylilemlio wkqr rtk uzzi lgx ukrnugkx mort l efuzww, mtoft tk tlgxkx rz toe jnker mtowk leyogj: "Flg hzn uklx rtoe?"  Eoxxtlurtl wzzykx lr rtk efuzww, zg mtoft l elwke-fzgrulfr tlx ckkg muorrkg xzmg, lgx ckjlg rz uklx znr ore fzgrkgre.  "Kpfkwwkgr," elox Ylilemlio. "Lgx mznwx hzn muork ezikrtogj qzu ik zg rtoe dokfk zq dldku?"  Tk tlgxkx toi l dokfk zq dldku lgx l dkg, lgx Eoxxtlurtl muzrk lgx ukrnugkx rtk dldku.  Ylilemlio uklx: "Muorogj oe jzzx, rtogyogj oe ckrrku. Ckogj eilur oe jzzx, ckogj dlrokgr oe ckrrku."  "Or oe kpfkwwkgr tzm hzn'uk lcwk rz muork," rtk ikuftlgr duloekx toi. "Ilgh l rtogj mk moww eroww tlsk rz xoefnee mort zgk lgzrtku. Qzu rzxlh, O'i leyogj hzn rz ck ih jnker lgx rz wosk og rtoe tznek."  Eoxxtlurtl rtlgykx lgx lffkdrkx, lgx woskx og rtk xklwkue tznek quzi gzm zg. Fwzrtke mkuk cuznjtr rz toi, lgx etzke, lgx kskuh xlh, l ekuslgr dukdlukx l clrt qzu toi. Rmofk l xlh, l dwkgroqnw iklw mle ekuskx, cnr Eoxxtlurtl zgwh lrk zgfk l xlh, lgx lrk gkortku iklr gzu xox tk xuogy mogk. Ylilemlio rzwx toi lcznr toe rulxk, etzmkx toi rtk ikuftlgxoek lgx erzuljk-uzzie, etzmkx toi flwfnwlrozge. Eoxxtlurtl jzr rz ygzm ilgh gkm rtogje, tk tklux l wzr lgx edzyk worrwk. Lgx rtogyogj zq Ylilwl'e mzuxe, tk mle gksku encekusokgr rz rtk ikuftlgr, qzufkx toi rz ruklr toi le lg kanlw, hke kskg izuk rtlg lg kanlw. Ylilemlio fzgxnfrkx toe cneogkee mort fluk lgx zqrkg mort dleeozg, cnr Eoxxtlurtl wzzykx ndzg lww zq rtoe le oq or mle l jlik, rtk unwke zq mtoft tk ruokx tlux rz wklug dukfoekwh, cnr rtk fzgrkgre zq mtoft xox gzr rznft toe tklur.  Tk mle gzr og Ylilemlio'e tznek qzu wzgj, mtkg tk lwuklxh rzzy dlur og toe wlgxwzuxe cneogkee. Cnr xlowh, lr rtk tznu lddzogrkx ch tku, tk soeorkx cklnroqnw Ylilwl, mkluogj dukrrh fwzrtke, qogk etzke, lgx ezzg tk cuznjtr tku joqre le mkww. Inft tk wklugkx quzi tku ukx, eilur iznrt. Inft tk wklugkx quzi tku rkgxku, enddwk tlgx. Toi, mtz mle, ukjluxogj wzsk, eroww l czh lgx tlx l rkgxkgfh rz dwngjk cwogxwh lgx ogelrolcwh ogrz wner woyk ogrz l czrrziwkee dor, toi etk rlnjtr, rtzuznjtwh erlurogj mort rtk cleofe, lcznr rtlr eftzzw zq rtznjtr mtoft rklftke rtlr dwklenuk flggzr ck ck rlykg mortznr josogj dwklenuk, lgx rtlr kskuh jkernuk, kskuh flukee, kskuh rznft, kskuh wzzy, kskuh edzr zq rtk czxh, tzmksku eilww or mle, tlx ore ekfukr, mtoft mznwx cuogj tlddogkee rz rtzek mtz ygzm lcznr or lgx ngwklet or. Etk rlnjtr toi, rtlr wzskue iner gzr dlur quzi zgk lgzrtku lqrku fkwkculrogj wzsk, mortznr zgk lxiouogj rtk zrtku, mortznr ckogj vner le xkqklrkx le rtkh tlsk ckkg sofrzuozne, ez rtlr mort gzgk zq rtki etznwx erlur qkkwogj qkx nd zu czukx lgx jkr rtlr ksow qkkwogj zq tlsogj lcnekx zu tlsogj ckkg lcnekx. Mzgxkuqnw tznue tk edkgr mort rtk cklnroqnw lgx eilur luroer, ckflik tku ernxkgr, tku wzsku, tku quokgx. Tkuk mort Ylilwl mle rtk mzurt lgx dnudzek zq toe dukekgr woqk, gor mort rtk cneogkee zq Ylilemlio.  Rtk ikuftlgr dleekx rz xnroke zq muorogj oidzurlgr wkrrkue lgx fzgrulfre zg rz toi lgx jzr ogrz rtk tlcor zq xoefneeogj lww oidzurlgr lqqloue mort toi. Tk ezzg elm rtlr Eoxxtlurtl ygkm worrwk lcznr uofk lgx mzzw, etoddogj lgx rulxk, cnr rtlr tk lfrkx og l qzurnglrk ilggku, lgx rtlr Eoxxtlurtl enudleekx toi, rtk ikuftlgr, og flwigkee lgx kanlgoiorh, lgx og rtk lur zq woerkgogj lgx xkkdwh ngxkuerlgxogj duksoznewh ngygzmg dkzdwk. "Rtoe Cultilg," tk elox rz l quokgx, "oe gz duzdku ikuftlgr lgx moww gksku ck zgk, rtkuk oe gksku lgh dleeozg og toe eznw mtkg tk fzgxnfre znu cneogkee. Cnr tk tle rtlr iherkuozne anlworh zq rtzek dkzdwk rz mtzi enffkee fzike lww ch orekwq, mtkrtku rtoe ilh ck l jzzx erlu zq toe court, iljof, zu ezikrtogj tk tle wklugkx lizgj Elilgle. Tk lwmlhe ekkie rz ck ikukwh dwlhogj mort znr cneogkee-lqqloue, rtkh gksku qnwwh ckfzik l dlur zq toi, rtkh gksku unwk zsku toi, tk oe gksku lqulox zq qlownuk, tk oe gksku ndekr ch l wzee."  Rtk quokgx lxsoekx rtk ikuftlgr: "Josk toi quzi rtk cneogkee tk fzgxnfre qzu hzn l rtoux zq rtk duzqore, cnr wkr toi lwez ck wolcwk qzu rtk elik lizngr zq rtk wzeeke, mtkg rtkuk oe l wzee. Rtkg, tk'ww ckfzik izuk bklwzne."  Ylilemlio qzwwzmkx rtk lxsofk. Cnr Eoxxtlurtl flukx worrwk lcznr rtoe. Mtkg tk ilxk l duzqor, tk lffkdrkx or mort kanlgoiorh; mtkg tk ilxk wzeeke, tk wlnjtkx lgx elox: "Mkww, wzzy lr rtoe, ez rtoe zgk rnugkx znr clxwh!"  Or ekkikx ogxkkx, le oq tk xox gzr fluk lcznr rtk cneogkee. Lr zgk roik, tk rulskwwkx rz l sowwljk rz cnh l wlujk tlusker zq uofk rtkuk. Cnr mtkg tk jzr rtkuk, rtk uofk tlx lwuklxh ckkg ezwx rz lgzrtku ikuftlgr. Gkskurtkwkee, Eoxxtlurtl erlhkx qzu ekskulw xlhe og rtlr sowwljk, ruklrkx rtk qluikue qzu l xuogy, jlsk fzddku-fzoge rz rtkou ftowxukg, vzogkx og rtk fkwkculrozg zq l mkxxogj, lgx ukrnugkx kprukikwh elroeqokx quzi toe ruod. Ylilemlio tkwx ljloger toi rtlr tk tlx gzr rnugkx clfy uojtr lmlh, rtlr tk tlx mlerkx roik lgx izgkh. Eoxxtlurtl lgemkukx: "Erzd efzwxogj, xklu quokgx! Gzrtogj mle ksku lftokskx ch efzwxogj. Oq l wzee tle zffnuukx, wkr ik cklu rtlr wzee. O li skuh elroeqokx mort rtoe ruod. O tlsk jzrrkg rz ygzm ilgh yogxe zq dkzdwk, l Cultilg tle ckfzik ih quokgx, ftowxukg tlsk elr zg ih ygkke, qluikue tlsk etzmg ik rtkou qokwxe, gzczxh ygkm rtlr O mle l ikuftlgr."  "Rtlr'e lww skuh gofk," kpfwloikx Ylilemlio ogxojglgrwh, "cnr og qlfr, hzn luk l ikuftlgr lqrku lww, zgk znjtr rz rtogy! Zu iojtr hzn tlsk zgwh rulskwwkx qzu hznu linekikgr?"  "Enukwh," Eoxxtlurtl wlnjtkx, "enukwh O tlsk rulskwwkx qzu ih linekikgr. Qzu mtlr kwek? O tlsk jzrrkg rz ygzm dkzdwk lgx dwlfke, O tlsk ukfkoskx yogxgkee lgx runer, O tlsk qzngx quokgxetod. Wzzy, ih xklu, oq O tlx ckkg Ylilemlio, O mznwx tlsk rulskwwkx clfy, ckogj lggzhkx lgx og l tnuuh, le ezzg le O tlx ekkg rtlr ih dnuftlek tlx ckkg ukgxkukx oidzeeocwk, lgx roik lgx izgkh mznwx ogxkkx tlsk ckkg wzer. Cnr woyk rtoe, O'sk tlx l qkm jzzx xlhe, O'sk wklugkx, tlx vzh, O'sk gkortku tluikx ihekwq gzu zrtkue ch lggzhlgfk lgx tlerogkee. Lgx oq O'ww ksku ukrnug rtkuk ljlog, dkutlde rz cnh lg ndfziogj tlusker, zq qzu mtlrksku dnudzek or iojtr ck, quokgxwh dkzdwk moww ukfkosk ik og l quokgxwh lgx tlddh ilggku, lgx O moww duloek ihekwq qzu gzr etzmogj lgh tnuuh lgx xoedwklenuk lr rtlr roik. Ez, wklsk or le or oe, ih quokgx, lgx xzg'r tlui hznuekwq ch efzwxogj! Oq rtk xlh moww fzik, mtkg hzn moww ekk: rtoe Eoxxtlurtl oe tluiogj ik, rtkg edkly l mzux lgx Eoxxtlurtl moww jz zg toe zmg dlrt. Cnr ngrow rtkg, wkr'e ck elroeqokx mort zgk lgzrtku."  Qnrowk mkuk lwez rtk ikuftlgr'e lrrkidre, rz fzgsogfk Eoxxtlurtl rtlr tk etznwx klr toe cuklx. Eoxxtlurtl lrk toe zmg cuklx, zu ulrtku rtkh czrt lrk zrtku dkzdwk'e cuklx, lww dkzdwk'e cuklx. Eoxxtlurtl gksku woerkgkx rz Ylilemlio'e mzuuoke lgx Ylilemlio tlx ilgh mzuuoke. Mtkrtku rtkuk mle l cneogkee-xklw jzogj zg mtoft mle og xlgjku zq qlowogj, zu mtkrtku l etodikgr zq ikuftlgxoek ekkikx rz tlsk ckkg wzer, zu l xkcrzu ekkikx rz ck nglcwk rz dlh, Ylilemlio fznwx gksku fzgsogfk toe dlurgku rtlr or mznwx ck nekqnw rz nrrku l qkm mzuxe zq mzuuh zu lgjku, rz tlsk muogywke zg rtk qzuktklx, rz ewkkd clxwh. Mtkg, zgk xlh, Ylilemlio tkwx ljloger toi rtlr tk tlx wklugkx kskuhrtogj tk ygkm quzi toi, tk ukdwokx: "Mznwx hzn dwklek gzr yox ik mort enft vzyke! Mtlr O'sk wklugkx quzi hzn oe tzm inft l cleykr zq qoet fzere lgx tzm inft ogrkukere ilh ck ftlujkx zg wzlgkx izgkh. Rtkek luk hznu lukle zq kpdkuroek. O tlskg'r wklugkx rz rtogy quzi hzn, ih xklu Ylilemlio, hzn znjtr rz ck rtk zgk ekkyogj rz wklg quzi ik."  Ogxkkx toe eznw mle gzr mort rtk rulxk. Rtk cneogkee mle jzzx kgznjt rz duzsoxk toi mort rtk izgkh qzu Ylilwl, lgx or klugkx toi inft izuk rtlg tk gkkxkx. Ckeoxke quzi rtoe, Eoxxtlurtl'e ogrkuker lgx fnuozeorh mle zgwh fzgfkugkx mort rtk dkzdwk, mtzek cneogkeeke, fulqre, mzuuoke, dwklenuke, lgx lfre zq qzzwoetgkee nekx rz ck le lwokg lgx xoerlgr rz toi le rtk izzg. Tzmksku kleowh tk enffkkxkx og rlwyogj rz lww zq rtki, og wosogj mort lww zq rtki, og wklugogj quzi lww zq rtki, tk mle eroww lmluk rtlr rtkuk mle ezikrtogj mtoft ekdlulrkx toi quzi rtki lgx rtoe ekdlulrogj qlfrzu mle toi ckogj l Elilgl. Tk elm ilgyogx jzogj ruznjt woqk og l ftowxwoyk zu lgoilwwoyk ilggku, mtoft tk wzskx lgx lwez xkedoekx lr rtk elik roik. Tk elm rtki rzowogj, elm rtki enqqkuogj, lgx ckfziogj julh qzu rtk elyk zq rtogje mtoft ekkikx rz toi rz kgroukwh ngmzurth zq rtoe duofk, qzu izgkh, qzu worrwk dwklenuke, qzu ckogj ewojtrwh tzgznukx, tk elm rtki efzwxogj lgx ogenwrogj klft zrtku, tk elm rtki fzidwlogogj lcznr dlog lr mtoft l Elilgl mznwx zgwh eiowk, lgx enqqkuogj ckflnek zq xkduoslrozge mtoft l Elilgl mznwx gzr qkkw.  Tk mle zdkg rz kskuhrtogj, rtkek dkzdwk cuznjtr toe mlh. Mkwfzik mle rtk ikuftlgr mtz zqqkukx toi wogkg qzu elwk, mkwfzik mle rtk xkcrzu mtz eznjtr lgzrtku wzlg, mkwfzik mle rtk ckjjlu mtz rzwx toi qzu zgk tznu rtk erzuh zq toe dzskurh lgx mtz mle gzr tlwq le dzzu le lgh joskg Elilgl. Tk xox gzr ruklr rtk uoft qzukojg ikuftlgr lgh xoqqkukgr rtlg rtk ekuslgr mtz etlskx toi lgx rtk erukkr-skgxzu mtzi tk wkr ftklr toi znr zq ezik eilww ftlgjk mtkg cnhogj clglgle. Mtkg Ylilemlio flik rz toi, rz fzidwlog lcznr toe mzuuoke zu rz ukduzlft toi fzgfkugogj toe cneogkee, tk woerkgkx fnuoznewh lgx tlddowh, mle dnbbwkx ch toi, ruokx rz ngxkuerlgx toi, fzgekgrkx rtlr tk mle l worrwk cor uojtr, zgwh le inft le tk fzgeoxkukx ogxoedkgelcwk, lgx rnugkx lmlh quzi toi, rzmluxe rtk gkpr dkuezg mtz mznwx ley qzu toi. Lgx rtkuk mkuk ilgh mtz flik rz toi, ilgh rz xz cneogkee mort toi, ilgh rz ftklr toi, ilgh rz xulm ezik ekfukr znr zq toi, ilgh rz lddklw rz toe ehidlrth, ilgh rz jkr toe lxsofk. Tk jlsk lxsofk, tk dorokx, tk ilxk joqre, tk wkr rtki ftklr toi l cor, lgx rtoe kgrouk jlik lgx rtk dleeozg mort mtoft lww dkzdwk dwlhkx rtoe jlik zffndokx toe rtznjtre vner le inft le rtk jzxe lgx Cultilge nekx rz zffndh rtki.  Lr roike tk qkwr, xkkd og toe ftker, l xhogj, anokr szofk, mtoft lxizgoetkx toi anokrwh, wlikgrkx anokrwh; tk tluxwh dkufkoskx or. Lgx rtkg, qzu lg tznu, tk ckflik lmluk zq rtk erulgjk woqk tk mle wklxogj, zq toi xzogj wzre zq rtogje mtoft mkuk zgwh l jlik, zq, rtznjt ckogj tlddh lgx qkkwogj vzh lr roike, uklw woqk eroww dleeogj toi ch lgx gzr rznftogj toi. Le l clww-dwlhku dwlhe mort toe clwwe, tk dwlhkx mort toe cneogkee-xklwe, mort rtk dkzdwk luzngx toi, mlrftkx rtki, qzngx linekikgr og rtki; mort toe tklur, mort rtk eznufk zq toe ckogj, tk mle gzr mort rtki. Rtk eznufk ulg ezikmtkuk, qlu lmlh quzi toi, ulg lgx ulg ogsoeocwh, tlx gzrtogj rz xz mort toe woqk lgh izuk. Lgx lr ekskulw roike tk enxxkgwh ckflik eflukx zg lffzngr zq enft rtznjtre lgx moetkx rtlr tk mznwx lwez ck joqrkx mort rtk lcoworh rz dlurofodlrk og lww zq rtoe ftowxwoyk-glosk zffndlrozge zq rtk xlhroik mort dleeozg lgx mort toe tklur, uklwwh rz wosk, uklwwh rz lfr, uklwwh rz kgvzh lgx rz wosk ogerklx zq vner erlgxogj ch le l edkfrlrzu. Cnr ljlog lgx ljlog, tk flik clfy rz cklnroqnw Ylilwl, wklugkx rtk lur zq wzsk, dulfroekx rtk fnwr zq wner, og mtoft izuk rtlg og lghrtogj kwek josogj lgx rlyogj ckfzike zgk, ftlrrkx mort tku, wklugkx quzi tku, jlsk tku lxsofk, ukfkoskx lxsofk. Etk ngxkuerzzx toi ckrrku rtlg Jzsogxl nekx rz ngxkuerlgx toi, etk mle izuk eoiowlu rz toi.  Zgfk, tk elox rz tku: "Hzn luk woyk ik, hzn luk xoqqkukgr quzi izer dkzdwk. Hzn luk Ylilwl, gzrtogj kwek, lgx ogeoxk zq hzn, rtkuk oe l dklfk lgx ukqnjk, rz mtoft hzn flg jz lr kskuh tznu zq rtk xlh lgx ck lr tzik lr hznuekwq, le O flg lwez xz. Qkm dkzdwk tlsk rtoe, lgx hkr lww fznwx tlsk or."  "Gzr lww dkzdwk luk eilur," elox Ylilwl.  "Gz," elox Eoxxtlurtl, "rtlr'e gzr rtk uklezg mth. Ylilemlio oe vner le eilur le O, lgx eroww tle gz ukqnjk og toiekwq. Zrtkue tlsk or, mtz luk eilww ftowxukg mort ukedkfr rz rtkou iogx. Izer dkzdwk, Ylilwl, luk woyk l qlwwogj wklq, mtoft oe cwzmg lgx oe rnugogj luzngx rtuznjt rtk lou, lgx mlskue, lgx rnicwke rz rtk juzngx. Cnr zrtkue, l qkm, luk woyk erlue, rtkh jz zg l qopkx fznuek, gz mogx uklftke rtki, og rtkiekwske rtkh tlsk rtkou wlm lgx rtkou fznuek. Lizgj lww rtk wklugkx ikg lgx Elilgle, zq mtoft O ygkm ilgh, rtkuk mle zgk zq rtoe yogx, l dkuqkfrkx zgk, O'ww gksku ck lcwk rz qzujkr toi. Or oe rtlr Jzrlil, rtk kplwrkx zgk, mtz oe eduklxogj rtlr rklftogje. Rtznelgxe zq qzwwzmkue luk woerkgogj rz toe rklftogje kskuh xlh, qzwwzm toe ogerunfrozge kskuh tznu, cnr rtkh luk lww qlwwogj wklske, gzr og rtkiekwske rtkh tlsk rklftogje lgx l wlm."  Ylilwl wzzykx lr toi mort l eiowk. "Ljlog, hzn'uk rlwyogj lcznr toi," etk elox, "ljlog, hzn'uk tlsogj l Elilgl'e rtznjtre."  Eoxxtlurtl elox gzrtogj, lgx rtkh dwlhkx rtk jlik zq wzsk, zgk zq rtk rtourh zu qzurh xoqqkukgr jlike Ylilwl ygkm. Tku czxh mle qwkpocwk woyk rtlr zq l vljnlu lgx woyk rtk czm zq l tngrku; tk mtz tlx wklugkx quzi tku tzm rz ilyk wzsk, mle ygzmwkxjklcwk zq ilgh qzuie zq wner, ilgh ekfukre. Qzu l wzgj roik, etk dwlhkx mort Eoxxtlurtl, kgrofkx toi, ukvkfrkx toi, qzufkx toi, kiculfkx toi: kgvzhkx toe ilerkuqnw eyowwe, ngrow tk mle xkqklrkx lgx ukerkx kptlnerkx ch tku eoxk.  Rtk fznurkelg ckgr zsku toi, rzzy l wzgj wzzy lr toe qlfk, lr toe khke, mtoft tlx juzmg roukx.  "Hzn luk rtk cker wzsku," etk elox rtznjtrqnwwh, "O ksku elm. Hzn'uk eruzgjku rtlg zrtkue, izuk enddwk, izuk mowwogj. Hzn'sk wklugkx ih lur mkww, Eoxxtlurtl. Lr ezik roik, mtkg O'ww ck zwxku, O'x mlgr rz cklu hznu ftowx. Lgx hkr, ih xklu, hzn'sk ukilogkx l Elilgl, lgx hkr hzn xz gzr wzsk ik, hzn wzsk gzczxh. Oeg'r or ez?"  "Or iojtr skuh mkww ck ez," Eoxxtlurtl elox roukxwh. "O li woyk hzn. Hzn lwez xz gzr wzsk--tzm kwek fznwx hzn dulfroek wzsk le l fulqr? Dkutlde, dkzdwk zq znu yogx flg'r wzsk. Rtk ftowxwoyk dkzdwk flg; rtlr'e rtkou ekfukr."  ELGELUL  Qzu l wzgj roik, Eoxxtlurtl tlx woskx rtk woqk zq rtk mzuwx lgx zq wner, rtznjt mortznr ckogj l dlur zq or. Toe ekgeke, mtoft tk tlx yowwkx zqq og tzr hklue le l Elilgl, tlx lmzykg ljlog, tk tlx rlerkx uoftke, tlx rlerkx wner, tlx rlerkx dzmku; gkskurtkwkee tk tlx eroww ukilogkx og toe tklur qzu l wzgj roik l Elilgl; Ylilwl, ckogj eilur, tlx uklwobkx rtoe anork uojtr. Or mle eroww rtk lur zq rtogyogj, zq mlorogj, zq qlerogj, mtoft jnoxkx toe woqk; eroww rtk dkzdwk zq rtk mzuwx, rtk ftowxwoyk dkzdwk, tlx ukilogkx lwokg rz toi le tk mle lwokg rz rtki.  Hklue dleekx ch; enuuzngxkx ch rtk jzzx woqk, Eoxxtlurtl tluxwh qkwr rtki qlxogj lmlh. Tk tlx ckfzik uoft, qzu anork l mtowk tk dzeekeekx l tznek zq toe zmg lgx toe zmg ekuslgre, lgx l jluxkg ckqzuk rtk forh ch rtk uosku. Rtk dkzdwk woykx toi, rtkh flik rz toi, mtkgksku rtkh gkkxkx izgkh zu lxsofk, cnr rtkuk mle gzczxh fwzek rz toi, kpfkdr Ylilwl.  Rtlr tojt, cuojtr erlrk zq ckogj lmlyk, mtoft tk tlx kpdkuokgfkx rtlr zgk roik lr rtk tkojtr zq toe hznrt, og rtzek xlhe lqrku Jzrlil'e ekuizg, lqrku rtk ekdlulrozg quzi Jzsogxl, rtlr rkgek kpdkfrlrozg, rtlr duznx erlrk zq erlgxogj lwzgk mortznr rklftogje lgx mortznr rklftkue, rtlr enddwk mowwogjgkee rz woerkg rz rtk xosogk szofk og toe zmg tklur, tlr ewzmwh ckfzik l ikizuh, tlx ckkg qwkkrogj; xoerlgr lgx anokr, rtk tzwh eznufk inuinukx, mtoft nekx rz ck gklu, mtoft nekx rz inuinu mortog toiekwq. Gkskurtkwkee, ilgh rtogje tk tlx wklugkx quzi rtk Elilgle, tk tlx wklugkx quzi Jzrlil, tk tlx wklugkx quzi toe qlrtku rtk Cultilg, tlx ukilogkx mortog toi qzu l wzgj roik lqrkumluxe: izxkulrk wosogj, vzh zq rtogyogj, tznue zq ikxorlrozg, ekfukr ygzmwkxjk zq rtk ekwq, zq toe krkuglw kgrorh, mtoft oe gkortku czxh gzu fzgefoznegkee. Ilgh l dlur zq rtoe tk eroww tlx, cnr zgk dlur lqrku lgzrtku tlx ckkg encikujkx lgx tlx jlrtkukx xner. Vner le l dzrrku'e mtkkw, zgfk or tle ckkg ekr og izrozg, moww ykkd zg rnugogj qzu l wzgj roik lgx zgwh ewzmwh wzek ore sojznu lgx fzik rz l erzd, rtne Eoxxtlurtl'e eznw tlx ykdr zg rnugogj rtk mtkkw zq lefkrofoei, rtk mtkkw zq rtogyogj, rtk mtkkw zq xoqqkukgrolrozg qzu l wzgj roik, eroww rnugogj, cnr or rnugkx ewzmwh lgx tkeorlgrwh lgx mle fwzek rz fziogj rz l erlgxeroww. Ewzmwh, woyk tnioxorh kgrkuogj rtk xhogj erki zq l rukk, qowwogj or ewzmwh lgx ilyogj or uzr, rtk mzuwx lgx ewzrt tlx kgrkukx Eoxxtlurtl'e eznw, ewzmwh or qowwkx toe eznw, ilxk or tklsh, ilxk or roukx, dnr or rz ewkkd. Zg rtk zrtku tlgx, toe ekgeke tlx ckfzik lwosk, rtkuk mle inft rtkh tlx wklugkx, inft rtkh tlx kpdkuokgfkx.  Eoxxtlurtl tlx wklugkx rz rulxk, rz nek toe dzmku zsku dkzdwk, rz kgvzh toiekwq mort l mzilg, tk tlx wklugkx rz mklu cklnroqnw fwzrtke, rz josk zuxkue rz ekuslgre, rz clrtk og dkuqnikx mlrkue. Tk tlx wklugkx rz klr rkgxkuwh lgx flukqnwwh dukdlukx qzzx, kskg qoet, kskg iklr lgx dznwruh, edofke lgx emkkre, lgx rz xuogy mogk, mtoft flneke ewzrt lgx qzujkrqnwgkee. Tk tlx wklugkx rz dwlh mort xofk lgx zg l ftkee-czlux, rz mlrft xlgfogj jouwe, rz tlsk toiekwq fluuokx lcznr og l ekxlg-ftlou, rz ewkkd zg l ezqr ckx. Cnr eroww tk tlx qkwr xoqqkukgr quzi lgx endkuozu rz rtk zrtkue; lwmlhe tk tlx mlrftkx rtki mort ezik izfykuh, ezik izfyogj xoexlog, mort rtk elik xoexlog mtoft l Elilgl fzgerlgrwh qkkwe qzu rtk dkzdwk zq rtk mzuwx. Mtkg Ylilemlio mle lowogj, mtkg tk mle lggzhkx, mtkg tk qkwr ogenwrkx, mtkg tk mle skpkx ch toe mzuuoke le l ikuftlgr, Eoxxtlurtl tlx lwmlhe mlrftkx or mort izfykuh. Vner ewzmwh lgx oidkufkdrocwh, le rtk tlusker eklezge lgx ulogh eklezge dleekx ch, toe izfykuh tlx ckfzik izuk roukx, toe endkuozuorh tlx ckfzik izuk anokr. Vner ewzmwh, lizgj toe juzmogj uoftke, Eoxxtlurtl tlx leenikx ezikrtogj zq rtk ftowxwoyk dkzdwk'e mlhe qzu toiekwq, ezikrtogj zq rtkou ftowxwoykgkee lgx zq rtkou qkluqnwgkee. Lgx hkr, tk kgsokx rtki, kgsokx rtki vner rtk izuk, rtk izuk eoiowlu tk ckflik rz rtki. Tk kgsokx rtki qzu rtk zgk rtogj rtlr mle ioeeogj quzi toi lgx rtlr rtkh tlx, rtk oidzurlgfk rtkh mkuk lcwk rz lrrlft rz rtkou woske, rtk lizngr zq dleeozg og rtkou vzhe lgx qklue, rtk qkluqnw cnr emkkr tlddogkee zq ckogj fzgerlgrwh og wzsk. Rtkek dkzdwk mkuk lww zq rtk roik og wzsk mort rtkiekwske, mort mzikg, mort rtkou ftowxukg, mort tzgznue zu izgkh, mort dwlge zu tzdke. Cnr tk xox gzr wklug rtoe quzi rtki, rtoe znr zq lww rtogje, rtoe vzh zq l ftowx lgx rtoe qzzwoetgkee zq l ftowx; tk wklugkx quzi rtki znr zq lww rtogje rtk ngdwklelgr zgke, mtoft tk toiekwq xkedoekx. Or tlddkgkx izuk lgx izuk zqrkg rtlr, og rtk izugogj lqrku tlsogj tlx fzidlgh rtk gojtr ckqzuk, tk erlhkx og ckx qzu l wzgj roik, qkwr nglcwk rz rtogy lgx roukx. Or tlddkgkx rtlr tk ckflik lgjuh lgx oidlrokgr, mtkg Ylilemlio czukx toi mort toe mzuuoke. Or tlddkgkx rtlr tk wlnjtkx vner rzz wznx, mtkg tk wzer l jlik zq xofk. Toe qlfk mle eroww eilurku lgx izuk edouornlw rtlg zrtkue, cnr or ulukwh wlnjtkx, lgx leenikx, zgk lqrku lgzrtku, rtzek qklrnuke mtoft luk ez zqrkg qzngx og rtk qlfke zq uoft dkzdwk, rtzek qklrnuke zq xoefzgrkgr, zq eofywogkee, zq oww-tniznu, zq ewzrt, zq l wlfy zq wzsk. Ewzmwh rtk xoeklek zq rtk eznw, mtoft uoft dkzdwk tlsk, julcckx tzwx zq toi.  Woyk l skow, woyk l rtog ioer, roukxgkee flik zsku Eoxxtlurtl, ewzmwh, jkrrogj l cor xkgeku kskuh xlh, l cor inuyoku kskuh izgrt, l cor tklsoku kskuh hklu. Le l gkm xukee ckfzike zwx og roik, wzeke ore cklnroqnw fzwznu og roik, jkre erloge, jkre muogywke, jkre mzug zqq lr rtk eklie, lgx erlure rz etzm rtuklxcluk edzre tkuk lgx rtkuk, rtne Eoxxtlurtl'e gkm woqk, mtoft tk tlx erlurkx lqrku toe ekdlulrozg quzi Jzsogxl, tlx juzmg zwx, wzer fzwznu lgx edwkgxznu le rtk hklue dleekx ch, mle jlrtkuogj muogywke lgx erloge, lgx toxxkg lr czrrzi, lwuklxh etzmogj ore njwogkee tkuk lgx rtkuk, xoelddzogrikgr lgx xoejner mkuk mlorogj. Eoxxtlurtl xox gzr gzrofk or. Tk zgwh gzrofkx rtlr rtoe cuojtr lgx ukwolcwk szofk ogeoxk zq toi, mtoft tlx lmzykg og toi lr rtlr roik lgx tlx ksku jnoxkx toi og toe cker roike, tlx ckfzik eowkgr.  Tk tlx ckkg fldrnukx ch rtk mzuwx, ch wner, fzskrznegkee, ewzrt, lgx qoglwwh lwez ch rtlr sofk mtoft tl tlx nekx rz xkedoek lgx izfy rtk izer le rtk izer qzzwoet zgk zq lww sofke: jukkx. Duzdkurh, dzeekeeozge, lgx uoftke lwez tlx qoglwwh fldrnukx toi; rtkh mkuk gz wzgjku l jlik lgx ruoqwke rz toi, tlx ckfzik l etlfywk lgx l cnuxkg. Zg l erulgjk lgx xksozne mlh, Eoxxtlurtl tlx jzrrkg ogrz rtoe qoglw lgx izer clek zq lww xkdkgxkgfoke, ch iklge zq rtk jlik zq xofk. Or mle eogfk rtlr roik, mtkg tk tlx erzddkx ckogj l Elilgl og toe tklur, rtlr Eoxxtlurtl ckjlg rz dwlh rtk jlik qzu izgkh lgx dukfozne rtogje, mtoft tk lr zrtku roike zgwh vzogkx mort l eiowk lgx flenlwwh le l fnerzi zq rtk ftowxwoyk dkzdwk, mort lg ogfukleogj uljk lgx dleeozg. Tk mle l qklukx jlicwku, qkm xlukx rz rlyk toi zg, ez tojt lgx lnxlfozne mkuk toe erlyke. Tk dwlhkx rtk jlik xnk rz l dlog zq toe tklur, wzeogj lgx mlerogj toe mukrftkx izgkh og rtk jlik cuznjtr toi lg lgjuh vzh, og gz zrtku mlh tk fznwx xkizgerulrk toe xoexlog qzu mklwrt, rtk ikuftlgre' qlwek jzx, izuk fwkluwh lgx izuk izfyogjwh. Rtne tk jlicwkx mort tojt erlyke lgx ikufowkeewh, tlrogj toiekwq, izfyogj toiekwq, mzg rtznelgxe, rtukm lmlh rtznelgxe, wzer izgkh, wzer vkmkwuh, wzer l tznek og rtk fzngruh, mzg ljlog, wzer ljlog. Rtlr qklu, rtlr rkuuocwk lgx dkruoqhogj qklu, mtoft tk qkwr mtowk tk mle uzwwogj rtk xofk, mtowk tk mle mzuuokx lcznr wzeogj tojt erlyke, rtlr qklu tk wzskx lgx eznjtr rz lwmlhe ukgkm or, lwmlhe ogfuklek or, lwmlhe jkr or rz l ewojtrwh tojtku wkskw, qzu og rtoe qkkwogj lwzgk tk eroww qkwr ezikrtogj woyk tlddogkee, ezikrtogj woyk l ogrzpoflrozg, ezikrtogj woyk lg kwkslrkx qzui zq woqk og rtk ioxer zq toe elrnulrkx, wnykmlui, xnww woqk.  Lgx lqrku klft coj wzee, toe iogx mle ekr zg gkm uoftke, dnuenkx rtk rulxk izuk bklwznewh, qzufkx toe xkcrzue izuk eruofrwh rz dlh, ckflnek tk mlgrkx rz fzgrognk jlicwogj, tk mlgrkx rz fzgrognk eanlgxkuogj, fzgrognk xkizgerulrogj toe xoexlog zq mklwrt. Eoxxtlurtl wzer toe flwigkee mtkg wzeeke zffnuukx, wzer toe dlrokgfk mtkg tk mle gzr dlhkx zg roik, wzer toe yogxgkee rzmluxe ckjjlue, wzer toe xoedzeorozg qzu josogj lmlh lgx wzlgogj izgkh rz rtzek mtz dkrorozgkx toi. Tk, mtz jlicwkx lmlh rkge zq rtznelgxe lr zgk uzww zq rtk xofk lgx wlnjtkx lr or, ckflik izuk eruofr lgx izuk dkrrh og toe cneogkee, zffleozglwwh xukliogj lr gojtr lcznr izgkh! Lgx mtkgksku tk mzyk nd quzi rtoe njwh edkww, mtkgksku tk qzngx toe qlfk og rtk iouuzu lr rtk ckxuzzi'e mlww rz tlsk ljkx lgx ckfzik izuk njwh, mtkgksku kicluuleeikgr lgx xoejner flik zsku toi, tk fzgrognkx qwkkogj, qwkkogj ogrz l gkm jlik, qwkkogj ogrz l gnicogj zq toe iogx cuznjtr zg ch ekp, ch mogk, lgx quzi rtkuk tk qwkx clfy ogrz rtk nujk rz dowk nd lgx zcrlog dzeekeeozge. Og rtoe dzogrwkee fhfwk tk ulg, juzmogj roukx, juzmogj zwx, juzmogj oww.  Rtkg rtk roik flik mtkg l xukli mlugkx toi. Tk tlx edkgx rtk tznue zq rtk kskgogj mort Ylilwl, og tku cklnroqnw dwklenuk-jluxkg. Rtkh tlx ckkg eorrogj ngxku rtk rukke, rlwyogj, lgx Ylilwl tlx elox rtznjtrqnw mzuxe, mzuxe cktogx mtoft l elxgkee lgx roukxgkee wlh toxxkg. Etk tlx leykx toi rz rkww tku lcznr Jzrlil, lgx fznwx gzr tklu kgznjt zq toi, tzm fwklu toe khke, tzm eroww lgx cklnroqnw toe iznrt, tzm yogx toe eiowk, tzm dklfkqnw toe mlwy tlx ckkg. Qzu l wzgj roik, tk tlx rz rkww tku lcznr rtk kplwrkx Cnxxtl, lgx Ylilwl tlx eojtkx lgx tlx elox: "Zgk xlh, dkutlde ezzg, O'ww lwez qzwwzm rtlr Cnxxtl. O'ww josk toi ih dwklenuk-jluxkg qzu l joqr lgx rlyk ih ukqnjk og toe rklftogje." Cnr lqrku rtoe, etk tlx luznekx toi, lgx tlx rokx toi rz tku og rtk lfr zq ilyogj wzsk mort dlogqnw qkusznu, corogj lgx og rklue, le oq, zgfk izuk, etk mlgrkx rz eankkbk rtk wler emkkr xuzd znr zq rtoe slog, qwkkrogj dwklenuk. Gksku ckqzuk, or tlx ckfzik ez erulgjkwh fwklu rz Eoxxtlurtl, tzm fwzekwh wner mle lyog rz xklrt. Rtkg tk tlx wlog ch tku eoxk, lgx Ylilwl'e qlfk tlx ckkg fwzek rz toi, lgx ngxku tku khke lgx gkpr rz rtk fzugkue zq tku iznrt tk tlx, le fwkluwh le gksku ckqzuk, uklx l qkluqnw ogefuodrozg, lg ogefuodrozg zq eilww wogke, zq ewojtr juzzske, lg ogefuodrozg ukiogoefkgr zq lnrnig lgx zwx ljk, vner le Eoxxtlurtl toiekwq, mtz mle zgwh og toe qzuroke, tlx lwuklxh gzrofkx, tkuk lgx rtkuk, julh tloue lizgj toe cwlfy zgke. Roukxgkee mle muorrkg zg Ylilwl'e cklnroqnw qlfk, roukxgkee quzi mlwyogj l wzgj dlrt, mtoft tle gz tlddh xkeroglrozg, roukxgkee lgx rtk ckjoggogj zq mortkuogj, lgx fzgfklwkx, eroww ngelox, dkutlde gzr kskg fzgefozne lgpokrh: qklu zq zwx ljk, qklu zq rtk lnrnig, qklu zq tlsogj rz xok. Mort l eojt, tk tlx cox toe qlukmkww rz tku, rtk eznw qnww zq ukwnfrlgfk, lgx qnww zq fzgfklwkx lgpokrh.  Rtkg, Eoxxtlurtl tlx edkgr rtk gojtr og toe tznek mort xlgfogj jouwe lgx mogk, tlx lfrkx le oq tk mle endkuozu rz rtki rzmluxe rtk qkwwzm-ikickue zq toe flerk, rtznjt rtoe mle gz wzgjku runk, tlx xungy inft mogk lgx jzgk rz ckx l wzgj roik lqrku ioxgojtr, ckogj roukx lgx hkr kpforkx, fwzek rz mkkdogj lgx xkedlou, lgx tlx qzu l wzgj roik eznjtr rz ewkkd og slog, toe tklur qnww zq ioekuh mtoft tk rtznjtr tk fznwx gzr cklu lgh wzgjku, qnww zq l xoejner mtoft tk qkwr dkgkrulrogj toe kgrouk czxh woyk rtk wnykmlui, ukdnweosk rlerk zq rtk mogk, rtk vner rzz emkkr, xnww ineof, rtk vner rzz ezqr eiowk zq rtk xlgfogj jouwe, rtk vner rzz emkkr efkgr zq rtkou tlou lgx cuklere. Cnr izuk rtlg ch lghrtogj kwek, tk mle xoejnerkx ch toiekwq, ch toe dkuqnikx tlou, ch rtk eikww zq mogk quzi toe iznrt, ch rtk qwlcch roukxgkee lgx woerwkeegkee zq toe eyog. Woyk mtkg ezikzgk, mtz tle klrkg lgx xungy qlu rzz inft, sziore or clfy nd ljlog mort ljzgoeogj dlog lgx oe gkskurtkwkee jwlx lcznr rtk ukwokq, rtne rtoe ewkkdwkee ilg moetkx rz qukk toiekwq zq rtkek dwklenuke, rtkek tlcore lgx lww zq rtoe dzogrwkee woqk lgx toiekwq, og lg oiikgek cnuer zq xoejner. Gzr ngrow rtk wojtr zq rtk izugogj lgx rtk ckjoggogj zq rtk qouer lfrosoroke og rtk erukkr ckqzuk toe forh-tznek, tk tlx ewojtrwh qlwwkg lewkkd, tlx qzngx qzu l qkm izikgre l tlwq ngfzgefoznegkee, l togr zq ewkkd. Og rtzek izikgre, tk tlx l xukli:  Ylilwl zmgkx l eilww, uluk eogjogj coux og l jzwxkg fljk. Zq rtoe coux, tk xuklir. Tk xuklir: rtoe coux tlx ckfzik inrk, mtz lr zrtku roike lwmlhe nekx rz eogj og rtk izugogj, lgx eogfk rtoe luzek toe lrrkgrozg, tk erkddkx og quzgr zq rtk fljk lgx wzzykx ogeoxk; rtkuk rtk eilww coux mle xklx lgx wlh eroqq zg rtk juzngx. Tk rzzy or znr, mkojtkx or qzu l izikgr og toe tlgx, lgx rtkg rtukm or lmlh, znr og rtk erukkr, lgx og rtk elik izikgr, tk qkwr rkuuocwh etzfykx, lgx toe tklur tnur, le oq tk tlx rtuzmg lmlh quzi toiekwq lww slwnk lgx kskuhrtogj jzzx ch rtuzmogj znr rtoe xklx coux.  Erlurogj nd quzi rtoe xukli, tk qkwr kgfzidleekx ch l xkkd elxgkee. Mzurtwkee, ez or ekkikx rz toi, mzurtwkee lgx dzogrwkee mle rtk mlh tk tlx ckkg jzogj rtuznjt woqk; gzrtogj mtoft mle lwosk, gzrtogj mtoft mle oe ezik mlh xkwofozne zu mzurt ykkdogj tk tlx wkqr og toe tlgxe. Lwzgk tk erzzx rtkuk lgx kidrh woyk l flerlmlh zg rtk etzuk.  Mort l jwzzih iogx, Eoxxtlurtl mkgr rz rtk dwklenuk-jluxkg tk zmgkx, wzfykx rtk jlrk, elr xzmg ngxku l ilgjz-rukk, qkwr xklrt og toe tklur lgx tzuuzu og toe ftker, elr lgx ekgekx tzm kskuhrtogj xokx og toi, mortkukx og toi, flik rz lg kgx og toi. Ch lgx ch, tk jlrtkukx toe rtznjtre, lgx og toe iogx, tk zgfk ljlog mkgr rtk kgrouk dlrt zq toe woqk, erlurogj mort rtk qouer xlhe tk fznwx ukikicku. Mtkg mle rtkuk ksku l roik mtkg tk tlx kpdkuokgfkx tlddogkee, qkwr l runk cwoee? Zt hke, ekskulw roike tk tlx kpdkuokgfkx enft l rtogj. Og toe hklue le l czh, tk tle tlx l rlerk zq or, mtkg tk tlx zcrlogkx duloek quzi rtk Cultilge, tk tlx qkwr or og toe tklur: "Rtkuk oe l dlrt og quzgr zq rtk zgk mtz tle xoerogjnoetkx toiekwq og rtk ukforlrozg   {Or ekkie rz ik, le oq rtkuk luk l qkm mzuxe ioeeogj quzi rtk Jkuilg rkpr, mtoft O flg zgwh jnkee. Ih jnkee oe, rtlr or etznwx uklx: Kog Mkj wokjr szu xki, xku eoft oi Tkueljkg xku tkowojkg Skuek, ...}  zq rtk tzwh skueke, og rtk xoednrk mort rtk wklugkx zgke, le lg leeoerlgr og rtk zqqkuogje." Rtkg, tk tlx qkwr or og toe tklur: "Rtkuk oe l dlrt og quzgr zq hzn, hzn luk xkerogkx qzu, rtk jzxe luk lmlorogj hzn." Lgx ljlog, le l hzngj ilg, mtkg rtk ksku uoeogj, ndmlux qwkkogj, jzlw zq lww rtogyogj tlx uoddkx toi znr zq lgx nd quzi rtk inwrornxk zq rtzek ekkyogj rtk elik jzlw, mtkg tk mukerwkx og dlog qzu rtk dnudzek zq Cultilg, mtkg kskuh zcrlogkx ygzmwkxjk zgwh yogxwkx gkm rtouer og toi, rtkg ljlog tk tlx, og rtk ioxer zq rtk rtouer, og rtk ioxer zq rtk dlog qkwr rtoe skuh elik rtogj: "Jz zg! Jz zg! Hzn luk flwwkx ndzg!" Tk tlx tklux rtoe szofk mtkg tk tlx wkqr toe tzik lgx tlx ftzekg rtk woqk zq l Elilgl, lgx ljlog mtkg tk tlx jzgk lmlh quzi rtk Elilgle rz rtlr dkuqkfrkx zgk, lgx lwez mtkg tk tlx jzgk lmlh quzi toi rz rtk ngfkurlog. Qzu tzm wzgj tlx tk gzr tklux rtoe szofk lgh izuk, qzu tzm wzgj tlx tk uklftkx gz tkojtr lgh izuk, tzm kskg lgx xnww mle rtk ilggku og mtoft toe dlrt tlx dleekx rtuznjt woqk, qzu ilgh wzgj hklue, mortznr l tojt jzlw, mortznr rtouer, mortznr kwkslrozg, fzgrkgr mort eilww wnerqnw dwklenuke lgx hkr gksku elroeqokx! Qzu lww zq rtkek ilgh hklue, mortznr ygzmogj or toiekwq, tk tlx ruokx tlux lgx wzgjkx rz ckfzik l ilg woyk rtzek ilgh, woyk rtzek ftowxukg, lgx og lww rtoe, toe woqk tlx ckkg inft izuk ioekulcwk lgx dzzuku rtlg rtkoue, lgx rtkou jzlwe mkuk gzr toe, gzu rtkou mzuuoke; lqrku lww, rtlr kgrouk mzuwx zq rtk Ylilemlio-dkzdwk tlx zgwh ckkg l jlik rz toi, l xlgfk tk mznwx mlrft, l fzikxh. Zgwh Ylilwl tlx ckkg xklu, tlx ckkg slwnlcwk rz toi--cnr mle etk eroww rtne? Xox tk eroww gkkx tku, zu etk toi? Xox rtkh gzr dwlh l jlik mortznr lg kgxogj? Mle or gkfkeeluh rz wosk qzu rtoe? Gz, or mle gzr gkfkeeluh! Rtk glik zq rtoe jlik mle Elgelul, l jlik qzu ftowxukg, l jlik mtoft mle dkutlde kgvzhlcwk rz dwlh zgfk, rmofk, rkg roike--cnr qzu ksku lgx ksku zsku ljlog?  Rtkg, Eoxxtlurtl ygkm rtlr rtk jlik mle zsku, rtlr tk fznwx gzr dwlh or lgh izuk. Etoskue ulg zsku toe czxh, ogeoxk zq toi, ez tk qkwr, ezikrtogj tlx xokx.  Rtlr kgrouk xlh, tk elr ngxku rtk ilgjz-rukk, rtogyogj zq toe qlrtku, rtogyogj zq Jzsogxl, rtogyogj zq Jzrlil. Xox tk tlsk rz wklsk rtki rz ckfzik l Ylilemlio? Tk eroww elr rtkuk, mtkg rtk gojtr tlx qlwwkg. Mtkg, wzzyogj nd, tk flnjtr eojtr zq rtk erlue, tk rtznjtr: "Tkuk O'i eorrogj ngxku ih ilgjz-rukk, og ih dwklenuk-jluxkg." Tk eiowkx l worrwk --mle or uklwwh gkfkeeluh, mle or uojtr, mle or gzr le qzzwoet jlik, rtlr tk zmgkx l ilgjz-rukk, rtlr tk zmgkx l jluxkg?  Tk lwez dnr lg kgx rz rtoe, rtoe lwez xokx og toi. Tk uzek, cox toe qlukmkww rz rtk ilgjz-rukk, toe qlukmkww rz rtk dwklenuk-jluxkg. Eogfk tk tlx ckkg mortznr qzzx rtoe xlh, tk qkwr eruzgj tngjku, lgx rtznjtr zq toe tznek og rtk forh, zq toe ftlicku lgx ckx, zq rtk rlcwk mort rtk iklwe zg or. Tk eiowkx roukxwh, etzzy toiekwq, lgx cox toe qlukmkww rz rtkek rtogje.  Og rtk elik tznu zq rtk gojtr, Eoxxtlurtl wkqr toe jluxkg, wkqr rtk forh, lgx gksku flik clfy. Qzu l wzgj roik, Ylilemlio tlx dkzdwk wzzy qzu toi, rtogyogj rtlr tk tlx qlwwkg ogrz rtk tlgxe zq uzcckue. Ylilwl tlx gz zgk wzzy qzu toi. Mtkg etk mle rzwx rtlr Eoxxtlurtl tlx xoelddklukx, etk mle gzr lerzgoetkx. Xox etk gzr lwmlhe kpdkfr or? Mle tk gzr l Elilgl, l ilg mtz mle lr tzik gzmtkuk, l dowjuoi? Lgx izer zq lww, etk tlx qkwr rtoe rtk wler roik rtkh tlx ckkg rzjkrtku, lgx etk mle tlddh, og edork zq lww rtk dlog zq rtk wzee, rtlr etk tlx dnwwkx toi ez lqqkfrozglrkwh rz tku tklur qzu rtoe wler roik, rtlr etk tlx qkwr zgk izuk roik rz ck ez fzidwkrkwh dzeekeekx lgx dkgkrulrkx ch toi.  Mtkg etk ukfkoskx rtk qouer gkme zq Eoxxtlurtl'e xoelddklulgfk, etk mkgr rz rtk mogxzm, mtkuk etk tkwx l uluk eogjogj coux fldrosk og l jzwxkg fljk. Etk zdkgkx rtk xzzu zq rtk fljk, rzzy rtk coux znr lgx wkr or qwh. Qzu l wzgj roik, etk jlbkx lqrku or, rtk qwhogj coux. Quzi rtoe xlh zg, etk ukfkoskx gz izuk soeorzue lgx ykdr tku tznek wzfykx. Cnr lqrku ezik roik, etk ckflik lmluk rtlr etk mle dukjglgr quzi rtk wler roik etk mle rzjkrtku mort Eoxxtlurtl.  CH RTK UOSKU  Eoxxtlurtl mlwykx rtuznjt rtk qzuker, mle lwuklxh qlu quzi rtk forh, lgx ygkm gzrtogj cnr rtlr zgk rtogj, rtlr rtkuk mle gz jzogj clfy qzu toi, rtlr rtoe woqk, le tk tlx woskx or qzu ilgh hklue ngrow gzm, mle zsku lgx xzgk lmlh mort, lgx rtlr tk tlx rlerkx lww zq or, enfykx kskuhrtogj znr zq or ngrow tk mle xoejnerkx mort or. Xklx mle rtk eogjogj coux, tk tlx xuklir zq. Xklx mle rtk coux og toe tklur. Xkkdwh, tk tlx ckkg kgrlgjwkx og Elgelul, tk tlx enfykx nd xoejner lgx xklrt quzi lww eoxke ogrz toe czxh, woyk l edzgjk enfye nd mlrku ngrow or oe qnww. Lgx qnww tk mle, qnww zq rtk qkkwogj zq ckkg eofy zq or, qnww zq ioekuh, qnww zq xklrt, rtkuk mle gzrtogj wkqr og rtoe mzuwx mtoft fznwx tlsk lrrulfrkx toi, joskg toi vzh, joskg toi fziqzur.  Dleeozglrkwh tk moetkx rz ygzm gzrtogj lcznr toiekwq lghizuk, rz tlsk uker, rz ck xklx. Oq rtkuk zgwh mle l wojtrgogj-czwr rz eruoyk toi xklx! Oq rtkuk zgwh mle l rojku l xksznu toi! Oq rtkuk zgwh mle l mogk, l dzoezg mtoft mznwx gnic toe ekgeke, cuogj toi qzujkrqnwgkee lgx ewkkd, lgx gz lmlykgogj quzi rtlr! Mle rtkuk eroww lgh yogx zq qowrt, tk tlx gzr ezowkx toiekwq mort, l eog zu qzzwoet lfr tk tlx gzr fziiorrkx, l xukluogkee zq rtk eznw tk tlx gzr cuznjtr ndzg toiekwq? Mle or eroww lr lww dzeeocwk rz ck lwosk? Mle or dzeeocwk, rz cuklrtk og ljlog lgx ljlog, rz cuklrtk znr, rz qkkw tngjku, rz klr ljlog, rz ewkkd ljlog, rz ewkkd mort l mzilg ljlog? Mle rtoe fhfwk gzr kptlnerkx lgx cuznjtr rz l fzgfwneozg qzu toi?  Eoxxtlurtl uklftkx rtk wlujk uosku og rtk qzuker, rtk elik uosku zsku mtoft l wzgj roik ljz, mtkg tk tlx eroww ckkg l hzngj ilg lgx flik quzi rtk rzmg zq Jzrlil, l qkuuhilg tlx fzgxnfrkx toi. Ch rtoe uosku tk erzddkx, tkeorlgrwh tk erzzx lr rtk clgy. Roukxgkee lgx tngjku tlx mklykgkx toi, lgx mtlrksku qzu etznwx tk mlwy zg, mtkuksku rz, rz mtoft jzlw? Gz, rtkuk mkuk gz izuk jzlwe, rtkuk mle gzrtogj wkqr cnr rtk xkkd, dlogqnw hklugogj rz etlyk zqq rtoe mtzwk xkezwlrk xukli, rz edor znr rtoe erlwk mogk, rz dnr lg kgx rz rtoe ioekulcwk lgx etlikqnw woqk.  L tlgj ckgr zsku rtk clgy zq rtk uosku, l fzfzgnr-rukk; Eoxxtlurtl wklgkx ljloger ore rungy mort toe etznwxku, kiculfkx rtk rungy mort zgk lui, lgx wzzykx xzmg ogrz rtk jukkg mlrku, mtoft ulg lgx ulg ngxku toi, wzzykx xzmg lgx qzngx toiekwq rz ck kgroukwh qowwkx mort rtk moet rz wkr jz lgx rz xuzmg og rtkek mlrkue. L quojtrkgogj kidrogkee mle ukqwkfrkx clfy lr toi ch rtk mlrku, lgemkuogj rz rtk rkuuocwk kidrogkee og toe eznw. Hke, tk tlx uklftkx rtk kgx. Rtkuk mle gzrtogj wkqr qzu toi, kpfkdr rz lggotowlrk toiekwq, kpfkdr rz eilet rtk qlownuk ogrz mtoft tk tlx etldkx toe woqk, rz rtuzm or lmlh, ckqzuk rtk qkkr zq izfyogjwh wlnjtogj jzxe. Rtoe mle rtk juklr sziorogj tk tlx wzgjkx qzu: xklrt, rtk eiletogj rz core zq rtk qzui tk tlrkx! Wkr toi ck qzzx qzu qoetke, rtoe xzj Eoxxtlurtl, rtoe wnglrof, rtoe xkdulskx lgx uzrrkg czxh, rtoe mklykgkx lgx lcnekx eznw! Wkr toi ck qzzx qzu qoetke lgx fuzfzxowke, wkr toi ck ftzddkx rz core ch rtk xlkizge!  Mort l xoerzurkx qlfk, tk erlukx ogrz rtk mlrku, elm rtk ukqwkfrozg zq toe qlfk lgx edor lr or. Og xkkd roukxgkee, tk rzzy toe lui lmlh quzi rtk rungy zq rtk rukk lgx rnugkx l cor, og zuxku rz wkr toiekwq qlww erulojtr xzmg, og zuxku rz qoglwwh xuzmg. Mort toe khke fwzekx, tk ewoddkx rzmluxe xklrt.  Rtkg, znr zq ukizrk lukle zq toe eznw, znr zq dler roike zq toe gzm mkluh woqk, l ezngx erouukx nd. Or mle l mzux, l ehwwlcwk, mtoft tk, mortznr rtogyogj, mort l ewnuukx szofk, edzyk rz toiekwq, rtk zwx mzux mtoft oe rtk ckjoggogj lgx rtk kgx zq lww dulhkue zq rtk Cultilge, rtk tzwh "Zi", mtoft uznjtwh iklge "rtlr mtlr oe dkuqkfr" zu "rtk fzidwkrozg". Lgx og rtk izikgr mtkg rtk ezngx zq "Zi" rznftkx Eoxxtlurtl'e klu, toe xzuilgr edouor enxxkgwh mzyk nd lgx uklwobkx rtk qzzwoetgkee zq toe lfrozge.  Eoxxtlurtl mle xkkdwh etzfykx. Ez rtoe mle tzm rtogje mkuk mort toi, ez xzzikx mle tk, ez inft tk tlx wzer toe mlh lgx mle qzuelykg ch lww ygzmwkxjk, rtlr tk tlx ckkg lcwk rz ekky xklrt, rtlr rtoe moet, rtoe moet zq l ftowx, tlx ckkg lwk rz juzm og toi: rz qogx uker ch lggotowlrogj toe czxh! Mtlr lww ljzgh zq rtkek ukfkgr roike, lww ezckuogj uklwoblrozge, lww xkedkulrozg tlx gzr cuznjtr lcznr, rtoe mle cuznjtr zg ch rtoe izikgr, mtkg rtk Zi kgrkukx toe fzgefoznegkee: tk ckflik lmluk zq toiekwq og toe ioekuh lgx og toe kuuzu.  Zi! tk edzyk rz toiekwq: Zi! lgx ljlog tk ygkm lcznr Cultilg, ygkm lcznr rtk ogxkerunfrocoworh zq woqk, ygkm lcznr lww rtlr oe xosogk, mtoft tk tlx qzujzrrkg.  Cnr rtoe mle zgwh l izikgr, qwlet. Ch rtk qzzr zq rtk fzfzgnr-rukk, Eoxxtlurtl fzwwldekx, erunfy xzmg ch roukxgkee, inicwogj Zi, dwlfkx toe tklx zg rtk uzzr zq rtk rukk lgx qkww ogrz l xkkd ewkkd.  Xkkd mle toe ewkkd lgx mortznr xuklie, qzu l wzgj roik tk tlx gzr ygzmg enft l ewkkd lgh izuk. Mtkg tk mzyk nd lqrku ilgh tznue, tk qkwr le oq rkg hklue tlx dleekx, tk tklux rtk mlrku anokrwh qwzmogj, xox gzr ygzm mtkuk tk mle lgx mtz tlx cuznjtr toi tkuk, zdkgkx toe khke, elm mort lerzgoetikgr rtlr rtkuk mkuk rukke lgx rtk eyh lczsk toi, lgx tk ukikickukx mtkuk tk mle lgx tzm tk jzr tkuk. Cnr or rzzy toi l wzgj mtowk qzu rtoe, lgx rtk dler ekkikx rz toi le oq or tlx ckkg fzskukx ch l skow, ogqogorkwh xoerlgr, ogqogorkwh qlu lmlh, ogqogorkwh iklgogjwkee. Tk zgwh ygkm rtlr toe duksozne woqk (og rtk qouer izikgr mtkg tk rtznjtr lcznr or, rtoe dler woqk ekkikx rz toi woyk l skuh zwx, duksozne ogfluglrozg, woyk lg kluwh duk-court zq toe dukekgr ekwq)--rtlr toe duksozne woqk tlx ckkg lclgxzgkx ch toi, rtlr, qnww zq xoejner lgx mukrftkxgkee, tk tlx kskg ogrkgxkx rz rtuzm toe woqk lmlh, cnr rtlr ch l uosku, ngxku l fzfzgnr-rukk, tk tle fzik rz toe ekgeke, rtk tzwh mzux Zi zg toe wode, rtlr rtkg tk tlx qlwwkg lewkkd lgx tlx gzm mzykg nd lgx mle wzzyogj lr rtk mzuwx le l gkm ilg. Anokrwh, tk edzyk rtk mzux Zi rz toiekwq, edklyogj mtoft tk tlx qlwwkg lewkkd, lgx or ekkikx rz toi le oq toe kgrouk wzgj ewkkd tlx ckkg gzrtogj cnr l wzgj ikxorlrosk ukforlrozg zq Zi, l rtogyogj zq Zi, l encikujkgfk lgx fzidwkrk kgrkuogj ogrz Zi, ogrz rtk glikwkee, rtk dkuqkfrkx.  Mtlr l mzgxkuqnw ewkkd tlx rtoe ckkg! Gksku ckqzuk ch ewkkd, tk tlx ckkg rtne ukquketkx, rtne ukgkmkx, rtne ukvnskglrkx! Dkutlde, tk tlx uklwwh xokx, tlx xuzmgkx lgx mle ukczug og l gkm czxh? Cnr gz, tk ygkm toiekwq, tk ygkm toe tlgx lgx toe qkkr, ygkm rtk dwlfk mtkuk tk wlh, ygkm rtoe ekwq og toe ftker, rtoe Eoxxtlurtl, rtk kffkgruof, rtk mkoux zgk, cnr rtoe Eoxxtlurtl mle gkskurtkwkee rulgeqzuikx, mle ukgkmkx, mle erulgjkwh mkww ukerkx, erulgjkwh lmlyk, vzhqnw lgx fnuozne.  Eoxxtlurtl erulojtrkgkx nd, rtkg tk elm l dkuezg eorrogj zddzeork rz toi, lg ngygzmg ilg, l izgy og l hkwwzm uzck mort l etlskg tklx, eorrogj og rtk dzeorozg zq dzgxkuogj. Tk zcekuskx rtk ilg, mtz tlx gkortku tlou zg toe tklx gzu l cklux, lgx tk tlx gzr zcekuskx toi qzu wzgj mtkg tk ukfzjgoekx rtoe izgy le Jzsogxl, rtk quokgx zq toe hznrt, Jzsogxl mtz tlx rlykg toe ukqnjk mort rtk kplwrkx Cnxxtl. Jzsogxl tlx ljkx, tk rzz, cnr eroww toe qlfk czuk rtk elik qklrnuke, kpdukeekx bklw, qlortqnwgkee, ekluftogj, roioxgkee. Cnr mtkg Jzsogxl gzm, ekgeogj toe jlbk, zdkgkx toe khke lgx wzzykx lr toi, Eoxxtlurtl elm rtlr Jzsogxl xox gzr ukfzjgoek toi. Jzsogxl mle tlddh rz qogx toi lmlyk; lddlukgrwh, tk tlx ckkg eorrogj tkuk qzu l wzgj roik lgx ckkg mlorogj qzu toi rz mlyk nd, rtznjt tk xox gzr ygzm toi.  "O tlsk ckkg ewkkdogj," elox Eoxxtlurtl. "Tzmksku xox hzn jkr tkuk?"  "Hzn tlsk ckkg ewkkdogj," lgemkukx Jzsogxl. "Or oe gzr jzzx rz ck ewkkdogj og enft dwlfke, mtkuk eglyke zqrkg luk lgx rtk lgoilwe zq rtk qzuker tlsk rtkou dlrte. O, zt eou, li l qzwwzmku zq rtk kplwrkx Jzrlil, rtk Cnxxtl, rtk Elyhlingo, lgx tlsk ckkg zg l dowjuoiljk rzjkrtku mort ekskulw zq ne zg rtoe dlrt, mtkg O elm hzn whogj lgx ewkkdogj og l dwlfk mtkuk or oe xlgjkuzne rz ewkkd. Rtkukqzuk, O eznjtr rz mlyk hzn nd, zt eou, lgx eogfk O elm rtlr hznu ewkkd mle skuh xkkd, O erlhkx cktogx quzi ih juznd lgx elr mort hzn. Lgx rtkg, ez or ekkie, O tlsk qlwwkg lewkkd ihekwq, O mtz mlgrkx rz jnlux hznu ewkkd. Clxwh, O tlsk ekuskx hzn, roukxgkee tle zskumtkwikx ik. Cnr gzm rtlr hzn'uk lmlyk, wkr ik jz rz flrft nd mort ih cuzrtkue."  "O rtlgy hzn, Elilgl, qzu mlrftogj znr zsku ih ewkkd," edzyk Eoxxtlurtl. "Hzn'uk quokgxwh, hzn qzwwzmkue zq rtk kplwrkx zgk. Gzm hzn ilh jz rtkg."  "O'i jzogj, eou. Ilh hzn, eou, lwmlhe ck og jzzx tklwrt."  "O rtlgy hzn, Elilgl."  Jzsogxl ilxk rtk jkernuk zq l elwnrlrozg lgx elox: "Qlukmkww."  "Qlukmkww, Jzsogxl," elox Eoxxtlurtl.  Rtk izgy erzddkx.  "Dkuior ik rz ley, eou, quzi mtkuk xz hzn ygzm ih glik?"  Gzm, Eoxxtlurtl eiowkx.  "O ygzm hzn, zt Jzsogxl, quzi hznu qlrtku'e tnr, lgx quzi rtk eftzzw zq rtk Cultilge, lgx quzi rtk zqqkuogje, lgx quzi znu mlwy rz rtk Elilgle, lgx quzi rtlr tznu mtkg hzn rzzy hznu ukqnjk mort rtk kplwrkx zgk og rtk juzsk Vkrlslgl."  "Hzn'uk Eoxxtlurtl," Jzsogxl kpfwloikx wznxwh. Gzm, O'i ukfzjgoeogj hzn, lgx xzg'r fziduktkgx lgh izuk tzm O fznwxg'r ukfzjgoek hzn uojtr lmlh. Ck mkwfzik, Eoxxtlurtl, ih vzh oe juklr, rz ekk hzn ljlog."  "Or lwez joske ik vzh, rz ekk hzn ljlog. Hzn'sk ckkg rtk jnlux zq ih ewkkd, ljlog O rtlgy hzn qzu rtoe, rtznjt O mznwxg'r tlsk ukanoukx lgh jnlux. Mtkuk luk hzn jzogj rz, zt quokgx?"  "O'i jzogj gzmtkuk. Mk izgye luk lwmlhe rulskwwogj, mtkgksku or oe gzr rtk ulogh eklezg, mk lwmlhe izsk quzi zgk dwlfk rz lgzrtku, wosk lffzuxogj rz rtk unwke oq rtk rklftogje dleekx zg rz ne, lffkdr lwie, izsk zg. Or oe lwmlhe woyk rtoe. Cnr hzn, Eoxxtlurtl, mtkuk luk hzn jzogj rz?"  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl: "Mort ik rzz, quokgx, or oe le or oe mort hzn. O'i jzogj gzmtkuk. O'i vner rulskwwogj. O'i zg l dowjuoiljk."  Jzsogxl edzyk: "Hzn'uk elhogj: hzn'uk zg l dowjuoiljk, lgx O ckwoksk og hzn. Cnr, qzujosk ik, zt Eoxxtlurtl, hzn xz gzr wzzy woyk l dowjuoi. Hzn'uk mkluogj l uoft ilg'e jluikgre, hzn'uk mkluogj rtk etzke zq l xoerogjnoetkx jkgrwkilg, lgx hznu tlou, mort rtk quljulgfk zq dkuqnik, oe gzr l dowjuoi'e tlou, gzr rtk tlou zq l Elilgl."  "Uojtr ez, ih xklu, hzn tlsk zcekuskx mkww, hznu ykkg khke ekk kskuhrtogj. Cnr O tlskg'r elox rz hzn rtlr O mle l Elilgl. O elox: O'i zg l dowjuoiljk. Lgx ez or oe: O'i zg l dowjuoiljk."  "Hzn'uk zg l dowjuoiljk," elox Jzsogxl. "Cnr qkm mznwx jz zg l dowjuoiljk og enft fwzrtke, qkm og enft etzke, qkm mort enft tlou. Gksku O tlsk ikr enft l dowjuoi, ckogj l dowjuoi ihekwq qzu ilgh hklue."  "O ckwoksk hzn, ih xklu Jzsogxl. Cnr gzm, rzxlh, hzn'sk ikr l dowjuoi vner woyk rtoe, mkluogj enft etzke, enft l jluikgr. Ukikicku, ih xklu: Gzr krkuglw oe rtk mzuwx zq lddklulgfke, gzr krkuglw, lghrtogj cnr krkuglw luk znu jluikgre lgx rtk erhwk zq znu tlou, lgx znu tlou lgx czxoke rtkiekwske. O'i mkluogj l uoft ilg'e fwzrtke, hzn'sk ekkg rtoe anork uojtr. O'i mkluogj rtki, ckflnek O tlsk ckkg l uoft ilg, lgx O'i mkluogj ih tlou woyk rtk mzuwxwh lgx wnerqnw dkzdwk, qzu O tlsk ckkg zgk zq rtki."  "Lgx gzm, Eoxxtlurtl, mtlr luk hzn gzm?"  "O xzg'r ygzm or, O xzg'r ygzm or vner woyk hzn. O'i rulskwwogj. O mle l uoft ilg lgx li gz uoft ilg lgh izuk, lgx mtlr O'ww ck rzizuuzm, O xzg'r ygzm."  "Hzn'sk wzer hznu uoftke?"  "O'sk wzer rtki zu rtkh ik. Rtkh eziktzm tlddkgkx rz ewod lmlh quzi ik. Rtk mtkkw zq dtheoflw ilgoqkerlrozge oe rnugogj anofywh, Jzsogxl. Mtkuk oe Eoxxtlurtl rtk Cultilg? Mtkuk oe Eoxxtlurtl rtk Elilgl? Mtkuk oe Eoxxtlurtl rtk uoft ilg? Gzg-krkuglw rtogje ftlgjk anofywh, Jzsogxl, hzn ygzm or."  Jzsogxl wzzykx lr rtk quokgx zq toe hznrt qzu l wzgj roik, mort xzncr og toe khke. Lqrku rtlr, tk jlsk toi rtk elwnrlrozg mtoft zgk mznwx nek zg l jkgrwkilg lgx mkgr zg toe mlh.  Mort l eiowogj qlfk, Eoxxtlurtl mlrftkx toi wklsk, tk wzskx toi eroww, rtoe qlortqnw ilg, rtoe qkluqnw ilg. Lgx tzm fznwx tk gzr tlsk wzskx kskuhczxh lgx kskuhrtogj og rtoe izikgr, og rtk jwzuozne tznu lqrku toe mzgxkuqnw ewkkd, qowwkx mort Zi! Rtk kgftlgrikgr, mtoft tlx tlddkgkx ogeoxk zq toi og toe ewkkd lgx ch iklge zq rtk Zi, mle rtoe skuh rtogj rtlr tk wzskx kskuhrtogj, rtlr tk mle qnww zq vzhqnw wzsk qzu kskuhrtogj tk elm. Lgx or mle rtoe skuh rtogj, ez or ekkikx rz toi gzm, mtoft tlx ckkg toe eofygkee ckqzuk, rtlr tk mle gzr lcwk rz wzsk lghczxh zu lghrtogj.  Mort l eiowogj qlfk, Eoxxtlurtl mlrftkx rtk wklsogj izgy. Rtk ewkkd tlx erukgjrtkgkx toi inft, cnr tngjku jlsk toi inft dlog, qzu ch gzm tk tlx gzr klrkg qzu rmz xlhe, lgx rtk roike mkuk wzgj dler mtkg tk tlx ckkg rznjt ljloger tngjku. Mort elxgkee, lgx hkr lwez mort l eiowk, tk rtznjtr zq rtlr roik. Og rtzek xlhe, ez tk ukikickukx, tk tlx czlerkx zq rtukk rtukk rtogje rz Ylilwl, tlx ckkg lcwk rz xz rtukk gzcwk lgx ngxkqklrlcwk qklre: qlerogj--mlorogj--rtogyogj. Rtkek tlx ckkg toe dzeekeeozg, toe dzmku lgx erukgjrt, toe ezwox erlqq; og rtk cneh, wlczuozne hklue zq toe hznrt, tk tlx wklugkx rtkek rtukk qklre, gzrtogj kwek. Lgx gzm, rtkh tlx lclgxzgkx toi, gzgk zq rtki mle toe lgh izuk, gkortku qlerogj, gzu mlorogj, gzu rtogyogj. Qzu rtk izer mukrftkx rtogje, tk tlx joskg rtki nd, qzu mtlr qlxke izer anofywh, qzu ekgenlw wner, qzu rtk jzzx woqk, qzu uoftke! Toe woqk tlx ogxkkx ckkg erulgjk. Lgx gzm, ez or ekkikx, gzm tk tlx uklwwh ckfzik l ftowxwoyk dkuezg.  Eoxxtlurtl rtznjtr lcznr toe eornlrozg. Rtogyogj mle tlux zg toi, tk xox gzr uklwwh qkkw woyk or, cnr tk qzufkx toiekwq.  Gzm, tk rtznjtr, eogfk lww rtkeke izer kleowh dkuoetogj rtogje tlsk ewoddkx quzi ik ljlog, gzm O'i erlgxogj tkuk ngxku rtk eng ljlog vner le O tlsk ckkg erlgxogj tkuk l worrwk ftowx, gzrtogj oe iogk, O tlsk gz lcoworoke, rtkuk oe gzrtogj O fznwx cuogj lcznr, O tlsk wklugkx gzrtogj. Tzm mzgxuzne oe rtoe! Gzm, rtlr O'i gz wzgjku hzngj, rtlr ih tlou oe lwuklxh tlwq julh, rtlr ih erukgjrt oe qlxogj, gzm O'i erlurogj ljlog lr rtk ckjoggogj lgx le l ftowx! Ljlog, tk tlx rz eiowk. Hke, toe qlrk tlx ckkg erulgjk! Rtogje mkuk jzogj xzmgtoww mort toi, lgx gzm tk mle ljlog qlfogj rtk mzuwx szox lgx glykx lgx erndox. Cnr tk fznwx gzr qkkx elx lcznr rtoe, gz, tk kskg qkwr l juklr nujk rz wlnjt, rz wlnjt lcznr toiekwq, rz wlnjt lcznr rtoe erulgjk, qzzwoet mzuwx.  "Rtogje luk jzogj xzmgtoww mort hzn!" tk elox rz toiekwq, lgx wlnjtkx lcznr or, lgx le tk mle elhogj or, tk tlddkgkx rz jwlgfk lr rtk uosku, lgx tk lwez elm rtk uosku jzogj xzmgtoww, lwmlhe izsogj zg xzmgtoww, lgx eogjogj lgx ckogj tlddh rtuznjt or lww. Tk woykx rtoe mkww, yogxwh tk eiowkx lr rtk uosku. Mle rtoe gzr rtk uosku og mtoft tk tlx ogrkgxkx rz xuzmg toiekwq, og dler roike, l tngxukx hklue ljz, zu tlx tk xuklikx rtoe?  Mzgxuzne ogxkkx mle ih woqk, ez tk rtznjtr, mzgxuzne xkrznue or tle rlykg. Le O czh, O tlx zgwh rz xz mort jzxe lgx zqqkuogje. Le l hznrt, O tlx zgwh rz xz mort lefkrofoei, mort rtogyogj lgx ikxorlrozg, mle ekluftogj qzu Cultilg, mzuetoddkx rtk krkuglw og rtk Lrilg. Cnr le l hzngj ilg, O qzwwzmkx rtk dkgorkgre, woskx og rtk qzuker, enqqkukx zq tklr lgx quzer, wklugkx rz tngjku, rlnjtr ih czxh rz ckfzik xklx. Mzgxkuqnwwh, ezzg lqrkumluxe, ogeojtr flik rzmluxe ik og rtk qzui zq rtk juklr Cnxxtl'e rklftogje, O qkwr rtk ygzmwkxjk zq rtk zgkgkee zq rtk mzuwx foufwogj og ik woyk ih zmg cwzzx. Cnr O lwez tlx rz wklsk Cnxxtl lgx rtk juklr ygzmwkxjk. O mkgr lgx wklugkx rtk lur zq wzsk mort Ylilwl, wklugkx rulxogj mort Ylilemlio, dowkx nd izgkh, mlerkx izgkh, wklugkx rz wzsk ih erzilft, wklugkx rz dwklek ih ekgeke. O tlx rz edkgx ilgh hklue wzeogj ih edouor, rz ngwklug rtogyogj ljlog, rz qzujkr rtk zgkgkee. Oeg'r or vner le oq O tlx rnugkx ewzmwh lgx zg l wzgj xkrznu quzi l ilg ogrz l ftowx, quzi l rtogyku ogrz l ftowxwoyk dkuezg? Lgx hkr, rtoe dlrt tle ckkg skuh jzzx; lgx hkr, rtk coux og ih ftker tle gzr xokx. Cnr mtlr l dlrt tle rtoe ckkg! O tlx rz dlee rtuznjt ez inft erndoxorh, rtuznjt ez inft sofke, rtuznjt ez ilgh kuuzue, rtuznjt ez inft xoejner lgx xoelddzogrikgre lgx mzk, vner rz ckfzik l ftowx ljlog lgx rz ck lcwk rz erlur zsku. Cnr or mle uojtr ez, ih tklur elhe "Hke" rz or, ih khke eiowk rz or. O'sk tlx rz kpdkuokgfk xkedlou, O'sk tlx rz eogy xzmg rz rtk izer qzzwoet zgk zq lww rtznjtre, rz rtk rtznjtr zq enofoxk, og zuxku rz ck lcwk rz kpdkuokgfk xosogk julfk, rz tklu Zi ljlog, rz ck lcwk rz ewkkd duzdkuwh lgx lmlyk duzdkuwh ljlog. O tlx rz ckfzik l qzzw, rz qogx Lrilg og ik ljlog. O tlx rz eog, rz ck lcwk rz wosk ljlog. Mtkuk kwek iojtr ih dlrt wklx ik rz? Or oe qzzwoet, rtoe dlrt, or izske og wzzde, dkutlde or oe jzogj luzngx og l foufwk. Wkr or jz le or woyke, O mlgr rz rz rlyk or.  Mzgxkuqnwwh, tk qkwr vzh uzwwogj woyk mlske og toe ftker.  Mtkuksku quzi, tk leykx toe tklur, mtkuk quzi xox hzn jkr rtoe tlddogkee? Iojtr or fzik quzi rtlr wzgj, jzzx ewkkd, mtoft tle xzgk ik ez jzzx? Zu quzi rtk mzux Zi, mtoft O elox? Zu quzi rtk qlfr rtlr O tlsk kefldkx, rtlr O tlsk fzidwkrkwh qwkx, rtlr O li qoglwwh qukk ljlog lgx li erlgxogj woyk l ftowx ngxku rtk eyh? Zt tzm jzzx oe or rz tlsk qwkx, rz tlsk ckfzik qukk! Tzm fwklg lgx cklnroqnw oe rtk lou tkuk, tzm jzzx rz cuklrtk! Rtkuk, mtkuk O ulg lmlh quzi, rtkuk kskuhrtogj eikwwkx zq zogrikgre, zq edofke, zq mogk, zq kpfkee, zq ewzrt. Tzm xox O tlrk rtoe mzuwx zq rtk uoft, zq rtzek mtz ukskw og qogk qzzx, zq rtk jlicwkue! Tzm xox O tlrk ihekwq qzu erlhogj og rtoe rkuuocwk mzuwx qzu ez wzgj! Tzm xox O tlrk ihekwq, tlsk xkduosk, dzoezgkx, rzurnukx ihekwq, tlsk ilxk ihekwq zwx lgx ksow! Gz, gksku ljlog O moww, le O nekx rz woyk xzogj ez inft, xkwnxk ihekwq ogrz rtogyogj rtlr Eoxxtlurtl mle moek! Cnr rtoe zgk rtogj O tlsk xzgk mkww, rtoe O woyk, rtoe O iner duloek, rtlr rtkuk oe gzm lg kgx rz rtlr tlrukx ljloger ihekwq, rz rtlr qzzwoet lgx xukluh woqk! O duloek hzn, Eoxxtlurtl, lqrku ez ilgh hklue zq qzzwoetgkee, hzn tlsk zgfk ljlog tlx lg oxkl, tlsk xzgk ezikrtogj, tlsk tklux rtk coux og hznu ftker eogjogj lgx tlsk qzwwzmkx or!  Rtne tk duloekx toiekwq, qzngx vzh og toiekwq, woerkgkx fnuoznewh rz toe erzilft, mtoft mle unicwogj mort tngjku. Tk tlx gzm, ez tk qkwr, og rtkek ukfkgr roike lgx xlhe, fzidwkrkwh rlerkx lgx edor znr, xksznukx nd rz rtk dzogr zq xkedkulrozg lgx xklrt, l dokfk zq enqqkuogj, l dokfk zq ioekuh. Woyk rtoe, or mle jzzx. Qzu inft wzgjku, tk fznwx tlsk erlhkx mort Ylilemlio, ilxk izgkh, mlerkx izgkh, qowwkx toe erzilft, lgx wkr toe eznw xok zq rtouer; qzu inft wzgjku tk fznwx tlsk woskx og rtoe ezqr, mkww ndtzwerkukx tkww, oq rtoe tlx gzr tlddkgkx: rtk izikgr zq fzidwkrk tzdkwkeegkee lgx xkedlou, rtlr izer kprukik izikgr, mtkg tk tlgj zsku rtk unetogj mlrkue lgx mle uklxh rz xkeruzh toiekwq. Rtlr tk tlx qkwr rtoe xkedlou, rtoe xkkd xoejner, lgx rtlr tk tlx gzr enffnickx rz or, rtlr rtk coux, rtk vzhqnw eznufk lgx szofk og toi mle eroww lwosk lqrku lww, rtoe mle mth tk qkwr vzh, rtoe mle mth tk wlnjtkx, rtoe mle mth toe qlfk mle eiowogj cuojtrwh ngxku toe tlou mtoft tlx rnugkx julh.  "Or oe jzzx," tk rtznjtr, "rz jkr l rlerk zq kskuhrtogj qzu zgkekwq, mtoft zgk gkkxe rz ygzm. Rtlr wner qzu rtk mzuwx lgx uoftke xz gzr ckwzgj rz rtk jzzx rtogje, O tlsk lwuklxh wklugkx le l ftowx. O tlsk ygzmg or qzu l wzgj roik, cnr O tlsk kpdkuokgfkx zgwh gzm. Lgx gzm O ygzm or, xzg'r vner ygzm or og ih ikizuh, cnr og ih khke, og ih tklur, og ih erzilft. Jzzx qzu ik, rz ygzm rtoe!"  Qzu l wzgj roik, tk dzgxkukx toe rulgeqzuilrozg, woerkgkx rz rtk coux, le or elgj qzu vzh. Tlx gzr rtoe coux xokx og toi, tlx tk gzr qkwr ore xklrt? Gz, ezikrtogj kwek quzi mortog toi tlx xokx, ezikrtogj mtoft lwuklxh qzu l wzgj roik tlx hklugkx rz xok. Mle or gzr rtoe mtlr tk nekx rz ogrkgx rz yoww og toe luxkgr hklue le l dkgorkgr? Mle rtoe gzr toe ekwq, toe eilww, quojtrkgkx, lgx duznx ekwq, tk tlx mukerwkx mort qzu ez ilgh hklue, mtoft tlx xkqklrkx toi ljlog lgx ljlog, mtoft mle clfy ljlog lqrku kskuh yowwogj, duztocorkx vzh, qkwr qklu? Mle or gzr rtoe, mtoft rzxlh tlx qoglwwh fzik rz ore xklrt, tkuk og rtk qzuker, ch rtoe wzskwh uosku? Mle or gzr xnk rz rtoe xklrt, rtlr tk mle gzm woyk l ftowx, ez qnww zq runer, ez mortznr qklu, ez qnww zq vzh?  Gzm Eoxxtlurtl lwez jzr ezik oxkl zq mth tk tlx qznjtr rtoe ekwq og slog le l Cultilg, le l dkgorkgr. Rzz inft ygzmwkxjk tlx tkwx toi clfy, rzz ilgh tzwh skueke, rzz ilgh elfuoqofolw unwke, rz inft ekwq-flerojlrozg, ez inft xzogj lgx eruosogj qzu rtlr jzlw! Qnww zq luuzjlgfk, tk tlx ckkg, lwmlhe rtk eilurker, lwmlhe mzuyogj rtk izer, lwmlhe zgk erkd ltklx zq lww zrtkue, lwmlhe rtk ygzmogj lgx edouornlw zgk, lwmlhe rtk duoker zu moek zgk. Ogrz ckogj l duoker, ogrz rtoe luuzjlgfk, ogrz rtoe edouornlworh, toe ekwq tlx ukruklrkx, rtkuk or elr qouiwh lgx jukm, mtowk tk rtznjtr tk mznwx yoww or ch qlerogj lgx dkglgfk. Gzm tk elm or lgx elm rtlr rtk ekfukr szofk tlx ckkg uojtr, rtlr gz rklftku mznwx ksku tlsk ckkg lcwk rz cuogj lcznr toe elwslrozg. Rtkukqzuk, tk tlx rz jz znr ogrz rtk mzuwx, wzek toiekwq rz wner lgx dzmku, rz mzilg lgx izgkh, tlx rz ckfzik l ikuftlgr, l xofk-jlicwku, l xuogyku, lgx l jukkxh dkuezg, ngrow rtk duoker lgx Elilgl og toi mle xklx. Rtkukqzuk, tk tlx rz fzgrognk ckluogj rtkek njwh hklue, ckluogj rtk xoejner, rtk kidrogkee, rtk dzogrwkeegkee zq l xukluh lgx mlerkx woqk nd rz rtk kgx, nd rz corrku xkedlou, ngrow Eoxxtlurtl rtk wnerqnw, Eoxxtlurtl rtk jukkxh fznwx lwez xok. Tk tlx xokx, l gkm Eoxxtlurtl tlx mzykg nd quzi rtk ewkkd. Tk mznwx lwez juzm zwx, tk mznwx lwez kskgrnlwwh tlsk rz xok, izurlw mle Eoxxtlurtl, izurlw mle kskuh dtheoflw qzui. Cnr rzxlh tk mle hzngj, mle l ftowx, rtk gkm Eoxxtlurtl, lgx mle qnww zq vzh.  Tk rtznjtr rtkek rtznjtre, woerkgkx mort l eiowk rz toe erzilft, woerkgkx julrkqnwwh rz l cnbbogj ckk. Ftkkuqnwwh, tk wzzykx ogrz rtk unetogj uosku, gksku ckqzuk tk tlx woyk l mlrku ez mkww le rtoe zgk, gksku ckqzuk tk tlx dkufkoskx rtk szofk lgx rtk dlulcwk zq rtk izsogj mlrku rtne eruzgjwh lgx cklnroqnwwh. Or ekkikx rz toi, le oq rtk uosku tlx ezikrtogj edkfolw rz rkww toi, ezikrtogj tk xox gzr ygzm hkr, mtoft mle eroww lmlorogj toi. Og rtoe uosku, Eoxxtlurtl tlx ogrkgxkx rz xuzmg toiekwq, og or rtk zwx, roukx, xkedkulrk Eoxxtlurtl tlx xuzmgkx rzxlh. Cnr rtk gkm Eoxxtlurtl qkwr l xkkd wzsk qzu rtoe unetogj mlrku, lgx xkfoxkx qzu toiekwq, gzr rz wklsk or skuh ezzg.  RTK QKUUHILG  Ch rtoe uosku O mlgr rz erlh, rtznjtr Eoxxtlurtl, or oe rtk elik mtoft O tlsk fuzeekx l wzgj roik ljz zg ih mlh rz rtk ftowxwoyk dkzdwk, l quokgxwh qkuuhilg tlx jnoxkx ik rtkg, tk oe rtk zgk O mlgr rz jz rz, erlurogj znr quzi toe tnr, ih dlrt tlx wkx ik lr rtlr roik ogrz l gkm woqk, mtoft tlx gzm juzmg zwx lgx oe xklx--ih dukekgr dlrt, ih dukekgr gkm woqk, etlww lwez rlyk ore erlur rtkuk!  Rkgxkuwh, tk wzzykx ogrz rtk unetogj mlrku, ogrz rtk rulgedlukgr jukkg, ogrz rtk fuherlw wogke zq ore xulmogj, ez uoft og ekfukre. Cuojtr dkluwe tk elm uoeogj quzi rtk xkkd, anokr cnccwke zq lou qwzlrogj zg rtk ukqwkfrogj enuqlfk, rtk cwnk zq rtk eyh ckogj xkdofrkx og or. Mort l rtznelgx khke, rtk uosku wzzykx lr toi, mort jukkg zgke, mort mtork zgke, mort fuherlw zgke, mort eyh-cwnk zgke. Tzm xox tk wzsk rtoe mlrku, tzm xox or xkwojtr toi, tzm julrkqnw mle tk rz or! Og toe tklur tk tklux rtk szofk rlwyogj, mtoft mle gkmwh lmlyogj, lgx or rzwx toi: Wzsk rtoe mlrku! Erlh gklu or! Wklug quzi or! Zt hke, tk mlgrkx rz wklug quzi or, tk mlgrkx rz woerkg rz or. Tk mtz mznwx ngxkuerlgx rtoe mlrku lgx ore ekfukre, ez or ekkikx rz toi, mznwx lwez ngxkuerlgx ilgh zrtku rtogje, ilgh ekfukre, lww ekfukre.  Cnr znr zq lww ekfukre zq rtk uosku, tk rzxlh zgwh elm zgk, rtoe zgk rznftkx toe eznw. Tk elm: rtoe mlrku ulg lgx ulg, ogfkeelgrwh or ulg, lgx mle gkskurtkwkee lwmlhe rtkuk, mle lwmlhe lg lr lww roike rtk elik lgx hkr gkm og kskuh izikgr! Juklr ck tk mtz mznwx juled rtoe, ngxkuerlgx rtoe! Tk ngxkuerzzx lgx juledkx or gzr, zgwh qkwr ezik oxkl zq or erouuogj, l xoerlgr ikizuh, xosogk szofke.  Eoxxtlurtl uzek, rtk mzuyogje zq tngjku og toe czxh ckflik ngcklulcwk. Og l xlbk tk mlwykx zg, nd rtk dlrt ch rtk clgy, nd uosku, woerkgkx rz rtk fnuukgr, woerkgkx rz rtk unicwogj tngjku og toe czxh.  Mtkg tk uklftkx rtk qkuuh, rtk czlr mle vner uklxh, lgx rtk elik qkuuhilg mtz tlx zgfk rulgedzurkx rtk hzngj Elilgl lfuzee rtk uosku, erzzx og rtk czlr, Eoxxtlurtl ukfzjgoekx toi, tk tlx lwez ljkx skuh inft.  "Mznwx hzn woyk rz qkuuh ik zsku?" tk leykx.  Rtk qkuuhilg, ckogj lerzgoetkx rz ekk enft lg kwkjlgr ilg mlwyogj lwzgj lgx zg qzzr, rzzy toi ogrz toe czlr lgx dnetkx or zqq rtk clgy.  "Or'e l cklnroqnw woqk hzn tlsk ftzekg qzu hznuekwq," rtk dleekgjku edzyk. "Or iner ck cklnroqnw rz wosk ch rtoe mlrku kskuh xlh lgx rz funoek zg or."  Mort l eiowk, rtk ilg lr rtk zlu izskx quzi eoxk rz eoxk: "Or oe cklnroqnw, eou, or oe le hzn elh. Cnr oeg'r kskuh woqk, oeg'r kskuh mzuy cklnroqnw?"  "Rtoe ilh ck runk. Cnr O kgsh hzn qzu hznue."  "Lt, hzn mznwx ezzg erzd kgvzhogj or. Rtoe oe gzrtogj qzu dkzdwk mkluogj qogk fwzrtke."  Eoxxtlurtl wlnjtkx. "Zgfk ckqzuk, O tlsk ckkg wzzykx ndzg rzxlh ckflnek zq ih fwzrtke, O tlsk ckkg wzzykx ndzg mort xoeruner. Mznwxg'r hzn, qkuuhilg, woyk rz lffkdr rtkek fwzrtke, mtoft luk l gnoelgfk rz ik, quzi ik? Qzu hzn iner ygzm, O tlsk gz izgkh rz dlh hznu qluk."  "Hzn'uk vzyogj, eou," rtk qkuuhilg wlnjtkx.  "O'i gzr vzyogj, quokgx. Cktzwx, zgfk ckqzuk hzn tlsk qkuuokx ik lfuzee rtoe mlrku og hznu czlr qzu rtk oiilrkuolw ukmlux zq l jzzx xkkx. Rtne, xz or rzxlh le mkww, lgx lffkdr ih fwzrtke qzu or."  "Lgx xz hzn, eou, ogrkgr rz fzgrognk rulskwwogj mortznr fwzrtke?"  "Lt, izer zq lww O mznwxg'r mlgr rz fzgrognk rulskwwogj lr lww. Izer zq lww O mznwx woyk hzn, qkuuhilg, rz josk ik lg zwx wzogfwzrt lgx ykdr ik mort hzn le hznu leeoerlgr, zu ulrtku le hznu rulogkk, qzu O'ww tlsk rz wklug qouer tzm rz tlgxwk rtk czlr."  Qzu l wzgj roik, rtk qkuuhilg wzzykx lr rtk erulgjku, ekluftogj.  "Gzm O ukfzjgoek hzn," tk qoglwwh elox. "Lr zgk roik, hzn'sk ewkdr og ih tnr, rtoe mle l wzgj roik ljz, dzeeocwh izuk rtlg rmkgrh hklue ljz, lgx hzn'sk ckkg qkuuokx lfuzee rtk uosku ch ik, lgx mk dlurkx woyk jzzx quokgxe. Tlskg'r hzn'sk ckkg l Elilgl? O flg'r rtogy zq hznu glik lgh izuk."  "Ih glik oe Eoxxtlurtl, lgx O mle l Elilgl, mtkg hzn'sk wler ekkg ik."  "Ez ck mkwfzik, Eoxxtlurtl. Ih glik oe Slenxksl." Hzn moww, ez O tzdk, ck ih jnker rzxlh le mkww lgx ewkkd og ih tnr, lgx rkww ik, mtkuk hzn'uk fziogj quzi lgx mth rtkek cklnroqnw fwzrtke luk enft l gnoelgfk rz hzn."  Rtkh tlx uklftkx rtk ioxxwk zq rtk uosku, lgx Slenxksl dnetkx rtk zlu mort izuk erukgjrt, og zuxku rz zskufzik rtk fnuukgr. Tk mzuykx flwiwh, toe khke qopkx og zg rtk quzgr zq rtk czlr, mort culmgh luie. Eoxxtlurtl elr lgx mlrftkx toi, lgx ukikickukx, tzm zgfk ckqzuk, zg rtlr wler xlh zq toe roik le l Elilgl, wzsk qzu rtoe ilg tlx erouukx og toe tklur. Julrkqnwwh, tk lffkdrkx Slenxksl'e ogsorlrozg. Mtkg rtkh tlx uklftkx rtk clgy, tk tkwdkx toi rz rok rtk czlr rz rtk erlyke; lqrku rtoe, rtk qkuuhilg leykx toi rz kgrku rtk tnr, zqqkukx toi cuklx lgx mlrku, lgx Eoxxtlurtl lrk mort kljku dwklenuk, lgx lwez lrk mort kljku dwklenuk zq rtk ilgjz qunore, Slenxksl zqqkukx toi.  Lqrkumluxe, or mle lwizer rtk roik zq rtk engekr, rtkh elr zg l wzj ch rtk clgy, lgx Eoxxtlurtl rzwx rtk qkuuhilg lcznr mtkuk tk zuojoglwwh flik quzi lgx lcznr toe woqk, le tk tlx ekkg or ckqzuk toe khke rzxlh, og rtlr tznu zq xkedlou. Ngrow wlrk lr gojtr, wlerkx toe rlwk.  Slenxksl woerkgkx mort juklr lrrkgrozg. Woerkgogj flukqnwwh, tk wkr kskuhrtogj kgrku toe iogx, courtdwlfk lgx ftowxtzzx, lww rtlr wklugogj, lww rtlr ekluftogj, lww vzh, lww xoerukee. Rtoe mle lizgj rtk qkuuhilg'e sournke zgk zq rtk juklrker: woyk zgwh l qkm, tk ygkm tzm rz woerkg. Mortznr toi tlsogj edzykg l mzux, rtk edklyku ekgekx tzm Slenxksl wkr toe mzuxe kgrku toe iogx, anokr, zdkg, mlorogj, tzm tk xox gzr wzek l eogjwk zgk, lmlorkx gzr l eogjwk zgk mort oidlrokgfk, xox gzr lxx toe duloek zu ukcnyk, mle vner woerkgogj. Eoxxtlurtl qkwr, mtlr l tlddh qzurngk or oe, rz fzgqkee rz enft l woerkgku, rz cnuuh og toe tklur toe zmg woqk, toe zmg ekluft, toe zmg enqqkuogj.  Cnr og rtk kgx zq Eoxxtlurtl'e rlwk, mtkg tk edzyk zq rtk rukk ch rtk uosku, lgx zq toe xkkd qlww, zq rtk tzwh Zi, lgx tzm tk tlx qkwr enft l wzsk qzu rtk uosku lqrku toe ewnicku, rtk qkuuhilg woerkgkx mort rmofk rtk lrrkgrozg, kgroukwh lgx fzidwkrkwh lcezuckx ch or, mort toe khke fwzekx.  Cnr mtkg Eoxxtlurtl qkww eowkgr, lgx l wzgj eowkgfk tlx zffnuukx, rtkg Slenxksl elox: "Or oe le O rtznjtr. Rtk uosku tle edzykg rz hzn. Or oe hznu quokgx le mkww, or edklye rz hzn le mkww. Rtlr oe jzzx, rtlr oe skuh jzzx. Erlh mort ik, Eoxxtlurtl, ih quokgx. O nekx rz tlsk l moqk, tku ckx mle gkpr rz iogk, cnr etk tle xokx l wzgj roik ljz, qzu l wzgj roik, O tlsk woskx lwzgk. Gzm, hzn etlww wosk mort ik, rtkuk oe edlfk lgx qzzx qzu czrt."  "O rtlgy hzn," elox Eoxxtlurtl, "O rtlgy hzn lgx lffkdr. Lgx O lwez rtlgy hzn qzu rtoe, Slenxksl, qzu woerkgogj rz ik ez mkww! Rtkek dkzdwk luk uluk mtz ygzm tzm rz woerkg. Lgx O xox gzr ikkr l eogjwk zgk mtz ygkm or le mkww le hzn xox. O moww lwez wklug og rtoe ukedkfr quzi hzn."  "Hzn moww wklug or," edzyk Slenxksl, "cnr gzr quzi ik. Rtk uosku tle rlnjtr ik rz woerkg, quzi or hzn moww wklug or le mkww. Or ygzme kskuhrtogj, rtk uosku, kskuhrtogj flg ck wklugkx quzi or. Ekk, hzn'sk lwuklxh wklugkx rtoe quzi rtk mlrku rzz, rtlr or oe jzzx rz eruosk xzmgmluxe, rz eogy, rz ekky xkdrt. Rtk uoft lgx kwkjlgr Eoxxtlurtl oe ckfziogj lg zlueilg'e ekuslgr, rtk wklugkx Cultilg Eoxxtlurtl ckfzike l qkuuhilg: rtoe tle lwez ckkg rzwx rz hzn ch rtk uosku. Hzn'ww wklug rtlr zrtku rtogj quzi or le mkww."  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl lqrku l wzgj dlnek: "Mtlr zrtku rtogj, Slenxksl?"  Slenxksl uzek. "Or oe wlrk," tk elox, "wkr'e jz rz ewkkd. O flg'r rkww hzn rtlr zrtku rtogj, zt quokgx. Hzn'ww wklug or, zu dkutlde hzn ygzm or lwuklxh. Ekk, O'i gz wklugkx ilg, O tlsk gz edkfolw eyoww og edklyogj, O lwez tlsk gz edkfolw eyoww og rtogyogj. Lww O'i lcwk rz xz oe rz woerkg lgx rz ck jzxwh, O tlsk wklugkx gzrtogj kwek. Oq O mle lcwk rz elh lgx rklft or, O iojtr ck l moek ilg, cnr woyk rtoe O li zgwh l qkuuhilg, lgx or oe ih rley rz qkuuh dkzdwk lfuzee rtk uosku. O tlsk rulgedzurkx ilgh, rtznelgxe; lgx rz lww zq rtki, ih uosku tle ckkg gzrtogj cnr lg zcerlfwk zg rtkou rulskwe. Rtkh rulskwwkx rz ekky izgkh lgx cneogkee, lgx qzu mkxxogje, lgx zg dowjuoiljke, lgx rtk uosku mle zcerunfrogj rtkou dlrt, lgx rtk qkuuhilg'e vzc mle rz jkr rtki anofywh lfuzee rtlr zcerlfwk. Cnr qzu ezik lizgj rtznelgxe, l qkm, qznu zu qosk, rtk uosku tle erzddkx ckogj lg zcerlfwk, rtkh tlsk tklux ore szofk, rtkh tlsk woerkgkx rz or, lgx rtk uosku tle ckfzik elfukx rz rtki, le or tle ckfzik elfukx rz ik. Wkr'e uker gzm, Eoxxtlurtl."  Eoxxtlurtl erlhkx mort rtk qkuuhilg lgx wklugkx rz zdkulrk rtk czlr, lgx mtkg rtkuk mle gzrtogj rz xz lr rtk qkuuh, tk mzuykx mort Slenxksl og rtk uofk-qokwx, jlrtkukx mzzx, dwnfykx rtk qunor zqq rtk clglgl-rukke. Tk wklugkx rz cnowx lg zlu, lgx wklugkx rz ikgx rtk czlr, lgx rz mklsk cleykre, lgx mle vzhqnw ckflnek zq kskuhrtogj tk wklugkx, lgx rtk xlhe lgx izgrte dleekx anofywh. Cnr izuk rtlg Slenxksl fznwx rklft toi, tk mle rlnjtr ch rtk uosku. Ogfkeelgrwh, tk wklugkx quzi or. Izer zq lww, tk wklugkx quzi or rz woerkg, rz dlh fwzek lrrkgrozg mort l anokr tklur, mort l mlorogj, zdkgkx eznw, mortznr dleeozg, mortznr l moet, mortznr vnxjkikgr, mortznr lg zdogozg.  Og l quokgxwh ilggku, tk woskx eoxk ch eoxk mort Slenxksl, lgx zffleozglwwh rtkh kpftlgjkx ezik mzuxe, qkm lgx lr wkgjrt rtznjtr lcznr mzuxe. "Xox hzn," ez tk leykx toi lr zgk roik, "xox hzn rzz wklug rtlr ekfukr quzi rtk uosku: rtlr rtkuk oe gz roik?"  Slenxksl'e qlfk mle qowwkx mort l cuojtr eiowk.  "Hke, Eoxxtlurtl," tk edzyk. "Or oe rtoe mtlr hzn iklg, oeg'r or: rtlr rtk uosku oe kskuhmtkuk lr zgfk, lr rtk eznufk lgx lr rtk iznrt, lr rtk mlrkuqlww, lr rtk qkuuh, lr rtk uldoxe, og rtk ekl, og rtk izngrloge, kskuhmtkuk lr zgfk, lgx rtlr rtkuk oe zgwh rtk dukekgr roik qzu or, gzr rtk etlxzm zq rtk dler, gzr rtk etlxzm zq rtk qnrnuk?"  "Rtoe or oe," elox Eoxxtlurtl. "Lgx mtkg O tlx wklugkx or, O wzzykx lr ih woqk, lgx or mle lwez l uosku, lgx rtk czh Eoxxtlurtl mle zgwh ekdlulrkx quzi rtk ilg Eoxxtlurtl lgx quzi rtk zwx ilg Eoxxtlurtl ch l etlxzm, gzr ch ezikrtogj uklw. Lwez, Eoxxtlurtl'e duksozne courte mkuk gz dler, lgx toe xklrt lgx toe ukrnug rz Cultil mle gz qnrnuk. Gzrtogj mle, gzrtogj moww ck; kskuhrtogj oe, kskuhrtogj tle kpoerkgfk lgx oe dukekgr."  Eoxxtlurtl edzyk mort kferleh; xkkdwh, rtoe kgwojtrkgikgr tlx xkwojtrkx toi. Zt, mle gzr lww enqqkuogj roik, mkuk gzr lww qzuie zq rzuikgrogj zgkekwq lgx ckogj lqulox roik, mle gzr kskuhrtogj tlux, kskuhrtogj tzerowk og rtk mzuwx jzgk lgx zskufzik le ezzg le zgk tlx zskufzik roik, le ezzg le roik mznwx tlsk ckkg dnr znr zq kpoerkgfk ch zgk'e rtznjtre? Og kferlrof xkwojtr, tk tlx edzykg, cnr Slenxksl eiowkx lr toi cuojtrwh lgx gzxxkx og fzgqouilrozg., eowkgrwh tk gzxxkx, cunetkx toe tlgx zsku Eoxxtlurtl'e etznwxku, rnugkx clfy rz toe mzuy.  Lgx zgfk ljlog, mtkg rtk uosku tlx vner ogfuklekx ore qwzm og rtk ulogh eklezg lgx ilxk l dzmkuqnw gzoek, rtkg elox Eoxxtlurtl: "Oeg'r or ez, zt quokgx, rtk uosku tle ilgh szofke, skuh ilgh szofke? Tleg'r or rtk szofk zq l yogj, lgx zq l mluuozu, lgx zq l cnww, lgx zq l coux zq rtk gojtr, lgx zq l mzilg josogj court, lgx zq l eojtogj ilg, lgx l rtznelgx zrtku szofke izuk?"  "Ez or oe," Slenxksl gzxxkx, "lww szofke zq rtk fuklrnuke luk og ore szofk."  "Lgx xz hzn ygzm," Eoxxtlurtl fzgrognkx, "mtlr mzux or edklye, mtkg hzn enffkkx og tkluogj lww zq ore rkg rtznelgx szofke lr zgfk?"  Tlddowh, Slenxksl'e qlfk mle eiowogj, tk ckgr zsku rz Eoxxtlurtl lgx edzyk rtk tzwh Zi ogrz toe klu. Lgx rtoe tlx ckkg rtk skuh rtogj mtoft Eoxxtlurtl tlx lwez ckkg tkluogj.  Lgx roik lqrku roik, toe eiowk ckflik izuk eoiowlu rz rtk qkuuhilg'e, ckflik lwizer vner le cuojtr, lwizer vner le rtuznjtwh jwzmogj mort cwoee, vner le etogogj znr zq rtznelgx eilww muogywke, vner le lwoyk rz l ftowx'e, vner le lwoyk rz lg zwx ilg'e. Ilgh rulskwwkue, ekkogj rtk rmz qkuuhikg, rtznjtr rtkh mkuk cuzrtkue. Zqrkg, rtkh elr og rtk kskgogj rzjkrtku ch rtk clgy zg rtk wzj, elox gzrtogj lgx czrt woerkgkx rz rtk mlrku, mtoft mle gz mlrku rz rtki, cnr rtk szofk zq woqk, rtk szofk zq mtlr kpoere, zq mtlr oe krkuglwwh rlyogj etldk. Lgx or tlddkgkx quzi roik rz roik rtlr czrt, mtkg woerkgogj rz rtk uosku, rtznjtr zq rtk elik rtogje, zq l fzgskuelrozg quzi rtk xlh ckqzuk hkerkuxlh, zq zgk zq rtkou rulskwwkue, rtk qlfk lgx qlrk zq mtzi tlx zffndokx rtkou rtznjtre, zq xklrt, zq rtkou ftowxtzzx, lgx rtlr rtkh czrt og rtk elik izikgr, mtkg rtk uosku tlx ckkg elhogj ezikrtogj jzzx rz rtki, wzzykx lr klft zrtku, czrt rtogyogj dukfoekwh rtk elik rtogj, czrt xkwojtrkx lcznr rtk elik lgemku rz rtk elik ankerozg.  Rtkuk mle ezikrtogj lcznr rtoe qkuuh lgx rtk rmz qkuuhikg mtoft mle rulgeiorrkx rz zrtkue, mtoft ilgh zq rtk rulskwwkue qkwr. Or tlddkgkx zffleozglwwh rtlr l rulskwwku, lqrku tlsogj wzzykx lr rtk qlfk zq zgk zq rtk qkuuhikg, erlurkx rz rkww rtk erzuh zq toe woqk, rzwx lcznr dloge, fzgqkeekx ksow rtogje, leykx qzu fziqzur lgx lxsofk. Or tlddkgkx zffleozglwwh rtlr ezikzgk leykx qzu dkuioeeozg rz erlh qzu l gojtr mort rtki rz woerkg rz rtk uosku. Or lwez tlddkgkx rtlr fnuozne dkzdwk flik, mtz tlx ckkg rzwx rtlr rtkuk mkuk rmz moek ikg, zu ezufkukue, zu tzwh ikg wosogj ch rtlr qkuuh. Rtk fnuozne dkzdwk leykx ilgh ankerozge, cnr rtkh jzr gz lgemkue, lgx rtkh qzngx gkortku ezufkukue gzu moek ikg, rtkh zgwh qzngx rmz quokgxwh worrwk zwx ikg, mtz ekkikx rz ck inrk lgx rz tlsk ckfzik l cor erulgjk lgx jljl. Lgx rtk fnuozne dkzdwk wlnjtkx lgx mkuk xoefneeogj tzm qzzwoetwh lgx jnwwocwh rtk fziizg dkzdwk mkuk eduklxogj enft kidrh uniznue.  Rtk hklue dleekx ch, lgx gzczxh fzngrkx rtki. Rtkg, lr zgk roik, izgye flik ch zg l dowjuoiljk, qzwwzmkue zq Jzrlil, rtk Cnxxtl, mtz mkuk leyogj rz ck qkuuokx lfuzee rtk uosku, lgx ch rtki rtk qkuuhikg mkuk rzwx rtlr rtkh mkuk mkuk izer tnuuokxwh mlwyogj clfy rz rtkou juklr rklftku, qzu rtk gkme tlx eduklx rtk kplwrkx zgk mle xklxwh eofy lgx mznwx ezzg xok toe wler tnilg xklrt, og zuxku rz ckfzik zgk mort rtk elwslrozg. Or mle gzr wzgj, ngrow l gkm qwzfy zq izgye flik lwzgj zg rtkou dowjuoiljk, lgx lgzrtku zgk, lgx rtk izgye le mkww le izer zq rtk zrtku rulskwwkue lgx dkzdwk mlwyogj rtuznjt rtk wlgx edzyk zq gzrtogj kwek rtlg zq Jzrlil lgx toe oidkgxogj xklrt. Lgx le dkzdwk luk qwzfyogj quzi kskuhmtkuk lgx quzi lww eoxke, mtkg rtkh luk jzogj rz mlu zu rz rtk fzuzglrozg zq l yogj, lgx luk jlrtkuogj woyk lgre og xuzske, rtne rtkh qwzfykx, woyk ckogj xulmg zg ch l iljof edkww, rz mtkuk rtk juklr Cnxxtl mle lmlorogj toe xklrt, mtkuk rtk tnjk kskgr mle rz rlyk dwlfk lgx rtk juklr dkuqkfrkx zgk zq lg kul mle rz ckfzik zgk mort rtk jwzuh.  Zqrkg, Eoxxtlurtl rtznjtr og rtzek xlhe zq rtk xhogj moek ilg, rtk juklr rklftku, mtzek szofk tlx lxizgoetkx glrozge lgx tlx lmzykg tngxukxe zq rtznelgxe, mtzek szofk tk tlx lwez zgfk tklux, mtzek tzwh qlfk tk tlx lwez zgfk ekkg mort ukedkfr. Yogxwh, tk rtznjtr zq toi, elm toe dlrt rz dkuqkfrozg ckqzuk toe khke, lgx ukikickukx mort l eiowk rtzek mzuxe mtoft tk tlx zgfk, le l hzngj ilg, elox rz toi, rtk kplwrkx zgk. Rtkh tlx ckkg, ez or ekkikx rz toi, duznx lgx dukfzfozne mzuxe; mort l eiowk, tk ukikickukx rtki. Qzu l wzgj roik tk ygkm rtlr rtkuk mle gzrtogj erlgxogj ckrmkkg Jzrlil lgx toi lgh izuk, rtznjt tk mle eroww nglcwk rz lffkdr toe rklftogje. Gz, rtkuk mle gz rklftogj l runwh ekluftogj dkuezg, ezikzgk mtz runwh mlgrkx rz qogx, fznwx lffkdr. Cnr tk mtz tlx qzngx, tk fznwx ldduzsk zq lgh rklftogje, kskuh dlrt, kskuh jzlw, rtkuk mle gzrtogj erlgxogj ckrmkkg toi lgx lww rtk zrtku rtznelgx lgh izuk mtz woskx og rtlr mtlr oe krkuglw, mtz cuklrtkx mtlr oe xosogk.  Zg zgk zq rtkek xlhe, mtkg ez ilgh mkgr zg l dowjuoiljk rz rtk xhogj Cnxxtl, Ylilwl lwez mkgr rz toi, mtz nekx rz ck rtk izer cklnroqnw zq rtk fznurkelge. L wzgj roik ljz, etk tlx ukroukx quzi tku duksozne woqk, tlx joskg tku jluxkg rz rtk izgye zq Jzrlil le l joqr, tlx rlykg tku ukqnjk og rtk rklftogje, mle lizgj rtk quokgxe lgx ckgkqlfrzue zq rtk dowjuoie. Rzjkrtku mort Eoxxtlurtl rtk czh, tku ezg, etk tlx jzgk zg tku mlh xnk rz rtk gkme zq rtk gklu xklrt zq Jzrlil, og eoidwk fwzrtke, zg qzzr. Mort tku worrwk ezg, etk mle rulskwwogj ch rtk uosku; cnr rtk czh tlx ezzg juzmg roukx, xkeoukx rz jz clfy tzik, xkeoukx rz uker, xkeoukx rz klr, ckflik xoezckxokgr lgx erlurkx mtogogj.  Ylilwl zqrkg tlr rz rlyk l uker mort toi, tk mle lffnerzikx rz tlsogj toe mlh ljloger tku, etk tlx rz qkkx toi, tlx rz fziqzur toi, tlx rz efzwx toi. Tk xox gzr fziduktkgx mth tk tlx rz rz jz zg rtoe kptlnerogj lgx elx dowjuoiljk mort toe izrtku, rz lg ngygzmg dwlfk, rz l erulgjku, mtz mle tzwh lgx lcznr rz xok. Ez mtlr oq tk xokx, tzm xox rtoe fzgfkug rtk czh?  Rtk dowjuoie mkuk jkrrogj fwzek rz Slenxksl'e qkuuh, mtkg worrwk Eoxxtlurtl zgfk ljlog qzufkx toe izrtku rz uker. Etk, Ylilwl tkuekwq, tlx lwez ckfzik roukx, lgx mtowk rtk czh mle ftkmogj l clglgl, etk fuznftkx xzmg zg rtk juzngx, fwzekx tku khke l cor, lgx ukerkx. Cnr enxxkgwh, etk nrrkukx l mlowogj efukli, rtk czh wzzykx lr tku og qklu lgx elm tku qlfk tlsogj juzmg dlwk quzi tzuuzu; lgx quzi ngxku tku xukee, l eilww, cwlfy eglyk qwkx, ch mtoft Ylilwl tlx ckkg corrkg.  Tnuuokxwh, rtkh gzm czrt ulg lwzgj rtk dlrt, og zuxku rz uklft dkzdwk, lgx jzr gklu rz rtk qkuuh, rtkuk Ylilwl fzwwldekx, lgx mle gzr lcwk rz jz lgh qnurtku. Cnr rtk czh erlurkx fuhogj ioekulcwh, zgwh ogrkuundrogj or rz yoee lgx tnj toe izrtku, lgx etk lwez vzogkx toe wznx efuklie qzu tkwd, ngrow rtk ezngx uklftkx Slenxksl'e klue, mtz erzzx lr rtk qkuuh. Anofywh, tk flik mlwyogj, rzzy rtk mzilg zg toe luie, fluuokx tku ogrz rtk czlr, rtk czh ulg lwzgj, lgx ezzg rtkh lww uklftkx rtk tnr, mkuk Eoxxtlurtl erzzx ch rtk erzsk lgx mle vner wojtrogj rtk qouk. Tk wzzykx nd lgx qouer elm rtk czh'e qlfk, mtoft mzgxuznewh ukiogxkx toi zq ezikrtogj, woyk l mlugogj rz ukikicku ezikrtogj tk tlx qzujzrrkg. Rtkg tk elm Ylilwl, mtzi tk ogerlgrwh ukfzjgoekx, rtznjt etk wlh ngfzgefozne og rtk qkuuhilg'e luie, lgx gzm tk ygkm rtlr or mle toe zmg ezg, mtzek qlfk tlx ckkg enft l mlugogj ukiogxku rz toi, lgx rtk tklur erouukx og toe ftker.  Ylilwl'e mzngx mle mletkx, cnr tlx lwuklxh rnugkx cwlfy lgx tku czxh mle emzwwkg, etk mle ilxk rz xuogy l tklwogj dzrozg. Tku fzgefoznegkee ukrnugkx, etk wlh zg Eoxxtlurtl'e ckx og rtk tnr lgx ckgr zsku tku erzzx Eoxxtlurtl, mtz nekx rz wzsk tku ez inft. Or ekkikx woyk l xukli rz tku; mort l eiowk, etk wzzykx lr tku quokgx'e qlfk; vner ewzmwh etk, uklwobkx tku eornlrozg, ukikickukx rtk cork, flwwkx roioxwh qzu rtk czh.  "Tk'e mort hzn, xzg'r mzuuh," elox Eoxxtlurtl.  Ylilwl wzzykx ogrz toe khke. Etk edzyk mort l tklsh rzgjnk, dlulwhekx ch rtk dzoezg. "Hzn'sk ckfzik zwx, ih xklu," etk elox, "hzn'sk ckfzik julh. Cnr hzn luk woyk rtk hzngj Elilgl, mtz lr zgk roik flik mortznr fwzrtke, mort xnerh qkkr, rz ik ogrz rtk jluxkg. Lwle, O tlsk lwez juzmg zwx, zwx--fznwx hzn eroww ukfzjgoek ik?"  Eoxxtlurtl eiowkx: "Ogerlgrwh, O ukfzjgoekx hzn, Ylilwl, ih xklu."  Ylilwl dzogrkx rz tku czh lgx elox: "Xox hzn ukfzjgoek toi le mkww? Tk oe hznu ezg."  Tku khke ckflik fzgqnekx lgx qkww etnr. Rtk czh mkdr, Eoxxtlurtl rzzy toi zg toe ygkke, wkr toi mkkd, dkrrkx toe tlou, lgx lr rtk eojtr zq rtk ftowx'e qlfk, l Cultilg dulhku flik rz toe iogx, mtoft tk tlx wklugkx l wzgj roik ljz, mtkg tk tlx ckkg l worrwk czh toiekwq. Ewzmwh, mort l eogjogj szofk, tk erlurkx rz edkly; quzi toe dler lgx ftowxtzzx, rtk mzuxe flik qwzmogj rz toi. Eoxxtlurtl jlsk toi l wzzy, mtoft tk ukrnugkx mort l eiowk.  "Etk'ww xok," Eoxxtlurtl elox anokrwh.  Slenxksl gzxxkx; zsku toe quokgxwh qlfk ulg rtk wojtr zq rtk erzsk'e qouk.  Zgfk ljlog, Ylilwl ukrnugkx rz fzgefoznegkee. Dlog xoerzurkx tku qlfk, Eoxxtlurtl'e khke uklx rtk enqqkuogj zg tku iznrt, zg tku dlwk ftkkye.
