Wzzyogj lr toi, etk elox: "Gzm O ekk rtlr hznu khke tlsk ftlgjkx le mkww. Rtkh'sk ckfzik fzidwkrkwh xoqqkukgr. Ch mtlr xz O eroww ukfzjgoek rtlr hzn'uk Eoxxtlurtl? Or'e hzn, lgx or'e gzr hzn."  Eoxxtlurtl elox gzrtogj, anokrwh toe khke wzzykx lr tkue.  "Hzn tlsk lftokskx or?" etk leykx. "Hzn tlsk qzngx dklfk?"  Tk eiowkx lgx dwlfkx toe tlgx zg tkue.  "O'i ekkogj or," etk elox, "O'i ekkogj or. O rzz moww qogx dklfk."  "Hzn tlsk qzngx or," Eoxxtlurtl edzyk og l mtoedku.  Ylilwl gksku erzddkx wzzyogj ogrz toe khke. Etk rtznjtr lcznr tku dowjuoiljk rz Jzrlil, mtoft mlgrkx rz rlyk, og zuxku rz ekk rtk qlfk zq rtk dkuqkfrkx zgk, rz cuklrtk toe dklfk, lgx etk rtznjtr rtlr etk tlx gzm qzngx toi og toe dwlfk, lgx rtlr or mle jzzx, vner le jzzx, le oq etk tlx ekkg rtk zrtku zgk. Etk mlgrkx rz rkww rtoe rz toi, cnr rtk rzgjnk gz wzgjku zckhkx tku moww. Mortznr edklyogj, etk wzzykx lr toi, lgx tk elm rtk woqk qlxogj quzi tku khke. Mtkg rtk qoglw dlog qowwkx tku khke lgx ilxk rtki juzm xoi, mtkg rtk qoglw etosku ulg rtuznjt tku woice, toe qogjku fwzekx tku khkwoxe.  Qzu l wzgj roik, tk elr lgx wzzykx lr tku dklfkqnwwh xklx qlfk. Qzu l wzgj roik, tk zcekuskx tku iznrt, tku zwx, roukx iznrt, mort rtzek wode, mtoft tlx ckfzik rtog, lgx tk ukikickukx, rtlr tk nekx rz, og rtk eduogj zq toe hklue, fzidluk rtoe iznrt mort l quketwh fulfykx qoj. Qzu l wzgj roik, tk elr, uklx og rtk dlwk qlfk, og rtk roukx muogywke, qowwkx toiekwq mort rtoe eojtr, elm toe zmg qlfk whogj og rtk elik ilggku, vner le mtork, vner le ankgftkx znr, lgx elm lr rtk elik roik toe qlfk lgx tkue ckogj hzngj, mort ukx wode, mort qokuh khke, lgx rtk qkkwogj zq rtoe czrt ckogj dukekgr lgx lr rtk elik roik uklw, rtk qkkwogj zq krkugorh, fzidwkrkwh qowwkx kskuh ledkfr zq toe ckogj. Xkkdwh tk qkwr, izuk xkkdwh rtlg ksku ckqzuk, og rtoe tznu, rtk ogxkerunfrocoworh zq kskuh woqk, rtk krkugorh zq kskuh izikgr.  Mtkg tk uzek, Slenxksl tlx dukdlukx uofk qzu toi. Cnr Eoxxtlurtl xox gzr klr. Og rtk erlcwk, mtkuk rtkou jzlr erzzx, rtk rmz zwx ikg dukdlukx ckxe zq erulm qzu rtkiekwske, lgx Slenxksl wlh toiekwq xzmg rz ewkkd. Cnr Eoxxtlurtl mkgr znreoxk lgx elr rtoe gojtr ckqzuk rtk tnr, woerkgogj rz rtk uosku, enuuzngxkx ch rtk dler, rznftkx lgx kgfoufwkx ch lww roike zq toe woqk lr rtk elik roik. Cnr zffleozglwwh, tk uzek, erkddkx rz rtk xzzu zq rtk tnr lgx woerkgkx, mtkrtku rtk czh mle ewkkdogj.  Kluwh og rtk izugogj, kskg ckqzuk rtk eng fznwx ck ekkg, Slenxksl flik znr zq rtk erlcwk lgx mlwykx zsku rz toe quokgx.  "Hzn tlskg'r ewkdr," tk elox.  "Gz, Slenxksl. O elr tkuk, O mle woerkgogj rz rtk uosku. L wzr or tle rzwx ik, xkkdwh or tle qowwkx ik mort rtk tklwogj rtznjtr, mort rtk rtznjtr zq zgkgkee."  "Hzn'sk kpdkuokgfkx enqqkuogj, Eoxxtlurtl, cnr O ekk: gz elxgkee tle kgrkukx hznu tklur."  "Gz, ih xklu, tzm etznwx O ck elx? O, mtz tlsk ckkg uoft lgx tlddh, tlsk ckfzik kskg uoftku lgx tlddoku gzm. Ih ezg tle ckkg joskg rz ik."  "Hznu ezg etlww ck mkwfzik rz ik le mkww. Cnr gzm, Eoxxtlurtl, wkr'e jkr rz mzuy, rtkuk oe inft rz ck xzgk. Ylilwl tle xokx zg rtk elik ckx, zg mtoft ih moqk tlx xokx l wzgj roik ljz. Wkr ne lwez cnowx Ylilwl'e qngkulw dowk zg rtk elik toww zg mtoft O tlx rtkg cnowr ih moqk'e qngkulw dowk."  Mtowk rtk czh mle eroww lewkkd, rtkh cnowr rtk qngkulw dowk.  RTK EZG  Roiox lgx mkkdogj, rtk czh tlx lrrkgxkx toe izrtku'e qngkulw; jwzzih lgx eth, tk tlx woerkgkx rz Eoxxtlurtl, mtz jukkrkx toi le toe ezg lgx mkwfzikx toi lr toe dwlfk og Slenxksl'e tnr. Dlwk, tk elr qzu ilgh xlhe ch rtk toww zq rtk xklx, xox gzr mlgr rz klr, jlsk gz zdkg wzzy, xox gzr zdkg toe tklur, ikr toe qlrk mort ukeoerlgfk lgx xkgolw.  Eoxxtlurtl edlukx toi lgx wkr toi xz le tk dwklekx, tk tzgznukx toe iznugogj. Eoxxtlurtl ngxkuerzzx rtlr toe ezg xox gzr ygzm toi, rtlr tk fznwx gzr wzsk toi woyk l qlrtku. Ewzmwh, tk lwez elm lgx ngxkuerzzx rtlr rtk kwkskg-hklu-zwx mle l dlidkukx czh, l izrtku'e czh, lgx rtlr tk tlx juzmg nd og rtk tlcore zq uoft dkzdwk, lffnerzikx rz qogku qzzx, rz l ezqr ckx, lffnerzikx rz josogj zuxkue rz ekuslgre. Eoxxtlurtl ngxkuerzzx rtlr rtk iznugogj, dlidkukx ftowx fznwx gzr enxxkgwh lgx mowwogjwh ck fzgrkgr mort l woqk lizgj erulgjkue lgx og dzskurh. Tk xox gzr qzufk toi, tk xox ilgh l ftzuk qzu toi, lwmlhe dofykx rtk cker dokfk zq rtk iklw qzu toi. Ewzmwh, tk tzdkx rz mog toi zsku, ch quokgxwh dlrokgfk.  Uoft lgx tlddh, tk tlx flwwkx toiekwq, mtkg rtk czh tlx fzik rz toi. Eogfk roik tlx dleekx zg og rtk iklgroik, lgx rtk czh ukilogkx l erulgjku lgx og l jwzzih xoedzeorozg, eogfk tk xoedwlhkx l duznx lgx erncczugwh xoezckxokgr tklur, xox gzr mlgr rz xz lgh mzuy, xox gzr dlh toe ukedkfr rz rtk zwx ikg, erzwk quzi Slenxksl'e qunor-rukke, rtkg Eoxxtlurtl ckjlg rz ngxkuerlgx rtlr toe ezg tlx gzr cuznjtr toi tlddogkee lgx dklfk, cnr enqqkuogj lgx mzuuh. Cnr tk wzskx toi, lgx tk dukqkuukx rtk enqqkuogj lgx mzuuoke zq wzsk zsku tlddogkee lgx vzh mortznr rtk czh. Eogfk hzngj Eoxxtlurtl mle og rtk tnr, rtk zwx ikg tlx edwor rtk mzuy. Slenxksl tlx ljlog rlykg zg rtk vzc zq rtk qkuuhilg lww ch toiekwq, lgx Eoxxtlurtl, og zuxku rz ck mort toe ezg, xox rtk mzuy og rtk tnr lgx rtk qokwx.  Qzu l wzgj roik, qzu wzgj izgrte, Eoxxtlurtl mlorkx qzu toe ezg rz ngxkuerlgx toi, rz lffkdr toe wzsk, rz dkutlde ukfoduzflrk or. Qzu wzgj izgrte, Slenxksl mlorkx, mlrftogj, mlorkx lgx elox gzrtogj. Zgk xlh, mtkg Eoxxtlurtl rtk hzngjku tlx zgfk ljlog rzuikgrkx toe qlrtku skuh inft mort edork lgx lg ngerklxogkee og toe moetke lgx tlx cuzykg czrt zq toe uofk-czmwe, Slenxksl rzzy og rtk kskgogj toe quokgx leoxk lgx rlwykx rz toi.  "Dluxzg ik." tk elox, "quzi l quokgxwh tklur, O'i rlwyogj rz hzn. O'i ekkogj rtlr hzn'uk rzuikgrogj hznuekwq, O'i ekkogj rtlr hzn'uk og juokq. Hzn'uk ezg, ih xklu, oe mzuuhogj hzn, lgx tk oe lwez mzuuhogj ik. Rtlr hzngj coux oe lffnerzikx rz l xoqqkukgr woqk, rz l xoqqkukgr gker. Tk tle gzr, woyk hzn, ulg lmlh quzi uoftke lgx rtk forh, ckogj xoejnerkx lgx qkx nd mort or; ljloger toe moww, tk tlx rz wklsk lww rtoe cktogx. O leykx rtk uosku, zt quokgx, ilgh roike O tlsk leykx or. Cnr rtk uosku wlnjte, or wlnjte lr ik, or wlnjte lr hzn lgx ik, lgx oe etlyogj mort wlnjtrku lr znr qzzwoetgkee. Mlrku mlgre rz vzog mlrku, hznrt mlgre rz vzog hznrt, hznu ezg oe gzr og rtk dwlfk mtkuk tk flg duzedku. Hzn rzz etznwx ley rtk uosku; hzn rzz etznwx woerkg rz or!"  Ruzncwkx, Eoxxtlurtl wzzykx ogrz toe quokgxwh qlfk, og rtk ilgh muogywke zq mtoft rtkuk mle ogfkeelgr ftkkuqnwgkee.  "Tzm fznwx O dlur mort toi?" tk elox anokrwh, letlikx. "Josk ik ezik izuk roik, ih xklu! Ekk, O'i qojtrogj qzu toi, O'i ekkyogj rz mog toe tklur, mort wzsk lgx mort quokgxwh dlrokgfk O ogrkgr rz fldrnuk or. Zgk xlh, rtk uosku etlww lwez rlwy rz toi, tk lwez oe flwwkx ndzg."  Slenxksl'e eiowk qwznuoetkx izuk mluiwh. "Zt hke, tk rzz oe flwwkx ndzg, tk rzz oe zq rtk krkuglw woqk. Cnr xz mk, hzn lgx ik, ygzm mtlr tk oe flwwkx ndzg rz xz, mtlr dlrt rz rlyk, mtlr lfrozge rz dkuqzui, mtlr dlog rz kgxnuk? Gzr l eilww zgk, toe dlog moww ck; lqrku lww, toe tklur oe duznx lgx tlux, dkzdwk woyk rtoe tlsk rz enqqku l wzr, kuu l wzr, xz inft ogvnerofk, cnuxkg rtkiekwske mort inft eog. Rkww ik, ih xklu: hzn'uk gzr rlyogj fzgruzw zq hznu ezg'e ndcuogjogj? Hzn xzg'r qzufk toi? Hzn xzg'r cklr toi? Hzn xzg'r dngoet toi?"  "Gz, Slenxksl, O xzg'r xz lghrtogj zq rtoe."  "O ygkm or. Hzn xzg'r qzufk toi, xzg'r cklr toi, xzg'r josk toi zuxkue, ckflnek hzn ygzm rtlr "ezqr" oe eruzgjku rtlg "tlux", Mlrku eruzgjku rtlg uzfye, wzsk eruzgjku rtlg qzufk. Skuh jzzx, O duloek hzn. Cnr lukg'r hzn ioerlykg og rtogyogj rtlr hzn mznwxg'r qzufk toi, mznwxg'r dngoet toi? Xzg'r hzn etlfywk toi mort hznu wzsk? Yogxwh, Eoxxtlurtl rtlgykx toi, mkgr ruzncwkx ogrz rtk tnr, fznwx gzr ewkkd qzu l wzgj roik. Slenxksl tlx rzwx toi gzrtogj, tk tlx gzr lwuklxh rtznjtr lgx ygzmg qzu toiekwq. Cnr rtoe mle l ygzmwkxjk tk fznwx gzr lfr ndzg, eruzgjku rtlg rtk ygzmwkxjk mle toe wzsk qzu rtk czh, eruzgjku mle toe rkgxkugkee, toe qklu rz wzek toi. Tlx tk ksku wzer toe tklur ez inft rz ezikrtogj, tlx tk ksku wzskx lgh dkuezg rtne, rtne cwogxwh, rtne enqqkuogjwh, rtne ngenffkeeqnwwh, lgx hkr rtne tlddowh?  Eoxxtlurtl fznwx gzr tkkx toe quokgx'e lxsofk, tk fznwx gzr josk nd rtk czh. Tk wkr rtk czh josk toi zuxkue, tk wkr toi xoeukjlux toi. Tk elox gzrtogj lgx mlorkx; xlowh, tk ckjlg rtk inrk erunjjwk zq quokgxwogkee, rtk eowkgr mlu zq dlrokgfk. Slenxksl lwez elox gzrtogj lgx mlorkx, quokgxwh, ygzmogj, dlrokgr. Rtkh mkuk czrt ilerkue zq dlrokgfk.  Lr zgk roik, mtkg rtk czh'e qlfk ukiogxkx toi skuh inft zq Ylilwl, Eoxxtlurtl enxxkgwh tlx rz rtogy zq l wogk mtoft Ylilwl l wzgj roik ljz, og rtk xlhe zq rtkou hznrt, tlx zgfk elox rz toi. "Hzn flggzr wzsk," etk tlx elox rz toi, lgx tk tlx ljukkx mort tku lgx tlx fzidlukx toiekwq mort l erlu, mtowk fzidluogj rtk ftowxwoyk dkzdwk mort qlwwogj wklske, lgx gkskurtkwkee tk tlx lwez ekgekx lg lffnelrozg og rtlr wogk. Ogxkkx, tk tlx gksku ckkg lcwk rz wzek zu xkszrk toiekwq fzidwkrkwh rz lgzrtku dkuezg, rz qzujkr toiekwq, rz fziior qzzwoet lfre qzu rtk wzsk zq lgzrtku dkuezg; gksku tk tlx ckkg lcwk rz xz rtoe, lgx rtoe mle, le or tlx ekkikx rz toi lr rtlr roik, rtk juklr xoerogfrozg mtoft ekr toi ldlur quzi rtk ftowxwoyk dkzdwk. Cnr gzm, eogfk toe ezg mle tkuk, gzm tk, Eoxxtlurtl, tlx lwez ckfzik fzidwkrkwh l ftowxwoyk dkuezg, enqqkuogj qzu rtk elyk zq lgzrtku dkuezg, wzsogj lgzrtku dkuezg, wzer rz l wzsk, tlsogj ckfzik l qzzw zg lffzngr zq wzsk. Gzm tk rzz qkwr, wlrk, zgfk og toe woqkroik, rtoe eruzgjker lgx erulgjker zq lww dleeozge, enqqkukx quzi or, enqqkukx ioekulcwh, lgx mle gkskurtkwkee og cwoee, mle gkskurtkwkee ukgkmkx og zgk ukedkfr, kguoftkx ch zgk rtogj.  Tk xox ekgek skuh mkww rtlr rtoe wzsk, rtoe cwogx wzsk qzu toe ezg, mle l dleeozg, ezikrtogj skuh tnilg, rtlr or mle Elgelul, l inuyh eznufk, xluy mlrkue. Gkskurtkwkee, tk qkwr lr rtk elik roik, or mle gzr mzurtwkee, or mle gkfkeeluh, flik quzi rtk keekgfk zq toe zmg ckogj. Rtoe dwklenuk lwez tlx rz ck lrzgkx qzu, rtoe dlog lwez tlx rz ck kgxnukx, rtkek qzzwoet lfre lwez tlx rz ck fziiorrkx.  Rtuznjt lww rtoe, rtk ezg wkr toi fziior toe qzzwoet lfre, wkr toi fznur qzu toe lqqkfrozg, wkr toi tniowolrk toiekwq kskuh xlh ch josogj og rz toe izzxe. Rtoe qlrtku tlx gzrtogj mtoft mznwx tlsk xkwojtrkx toi lgx gzrtogj mtoft tk mznwx tlsk qklukx. Tk mle l jzzx ilg, rtoe qlrtku, l jzzx, yogx, ezqr ilg, dkutlde l skuh xksznr ilg, dkutlde l elogr, lww rtkek rtkuk gz lrruocnrke mtoft fznwx mog rtk czh zsku. Tk mle czukx ch rtoe qlrtku, mtz ykdr toi duoezgku tkuk og rtoe ioekulcwk tnr zq toe, tk mle czukx ch toi, lgx qzu toi rz lgemku kskuh glnjtrogkee mort l eiowk, kskuh ogenwr mort quokgxwogkee, kskuh sofoznegkee mort yogxgkee, rtoe skuh rtogj mle rtk tlrkx ruofy zq rtoe zwx egkly. Inft izuk rtk czh mznwx tlsk woykx or oq tk tlx ckkg rtuklrkgkx ch toi, oq tk tlx ckkg lcnekx ch toi.  L xlh flik, mtkg mtlr hzngj Eoxxtlurtl tlx zg toe iogx flik cnuerogj qzurt, lgx tk zdkgwh rnugkx ljloger toe qlrtku. Rtk wlrrku tlx joskg toi l rley, tk tlx rzwx toi rz jlrtku cunetmzzx. Cnr rtk czh xox gzr wklsk rtk tnr, og erncczug xoezckxokgfk lgx uljk tk erlhkx mtkuk tk mle, rtnidkx zg rtk juzngx mort toe qkkr, fwkgftkx toe qoere, lgx efuklikx og l dzmkuqnw znrcnuer toe tlrukx lgx fzgrkidr ogrz toe qlrtku'e qlfk.  "Jkr rtk cunetmzzx qzu hznuekwq!" tk etznrkx qzliogj lr rtk iznrt, "O'i gzr hznu ekuslgr. O xz ygzm, rtlr hzn mzg'r tor ik, hzn xzg'r xluk; O xz ygzm, rtlr hzn fzgerlgrwh mlgr rz dngoet ik lgx dnr ik xzmg mort hznu ukwojozne xkszrozg lgx hznu ogxnwjkgfk. Hzn mlgr ik rz ckfzik woyk hzn, vner le xksznr, vner le ezqr, vner le moek! Cnr O, woerkg nd, vner rz ilyk hzn enqqku, O ulrtku mlgr rz ckfzik l tojtmlh-uzccku lgx inuxkuku, lgx jz rz tkww, rtlg rz ckfzik woyk hzn! O tlrk hzn, hzn'uk gzr ih qlrtku, lgx oq hzn'sk rkg roike ckkg ih izrtku'e qzugoflrzu!"  Uljk lgx juokq czowkx zsku og toi, qzlikx lr rtk qlrtku og l tngxukx elsljk lgx ksow mzuxe. Rtkg rtk czh ulg lmlh lgx zgwh ukrnugkx wlrk lr gojtr.  Cnr rtk gkpr izugogj, tk tlx xoelddklukx. Mtlr tlx lwez xoelddklukx mle l eilww cleykr, mzskg znr zq cler zq rmz fzwznue, og mtoft rtk qkuuhikg ykdr rtzek fzddku lgx eowsku fzoge mtoft rtkh ukfkoskx le l qluk. Rtk czlr tlx lwez xoelddklukx, Eoxxtlurtl elm or whogj ch rtk zddzeork clgy. Rtk czh tlx ulg lmlh.  "O iner qzwwzm toi," elox Eoxxtlurtl, mtz tlx ckkg etoskuogj mort juokq eogfk rtzek ulgrogj edkkftke, rtk czh tlx ilxk hkerkuxlh. "L ftowx flg'r jz rtuznjt rtk qzuker lww lwzgk. Tk'ww dkuoet. Mk iner cnowx l ulqr, Slenxksl, rz jkr zsku rtk mlrku."  "Mk moww cnowx l ulqr," elox Slenxksl, "rz jkr znu czlr clfy, mtoft rtk czh tle rlykg lmlh. Cnr toi, hzn etlww wkr ung lwzgj, ih quokgx, tk oe gz ftowx lgh izuk, tk ygzme tzm rz jkr luzngx. Tk'e wzzyogj qzu rtk dlrt rz rtk forh, lgx tk oe uojtr, xzg'r qzujkr rtlr. Tk'e xzogj mtlr hzn'sk qlowkx rz xz hznuekwq. Tk'e rlyogj fluk zq toiekwq, tk'e rlyogj toe fznuek. Lwle, Eoxxtlurtl, O ekk hzn enqqkuogj, cnr hzn'uk enqqkuogj l dlog lr mtoft zgk mznwx woyk rz wlnjt, lr mtoft hzn'ww ezzg wlnjt qzu hznuekwq."  Eoxxtlurtl xox gzr lgemku. Tk lwuklxh tkwx rtk lpk og toe tlgxe lgx ckjlg rz ilyk l ulqr zq cliczz, lgx Slenxksl tkwdkx toi rz rokx rtk flgke rzjkrtku mort uzdke zq julee. Rtkg rtkh fuzeekx zsku, xuoqrkx qlu zqq rtkou fznuek, dnwwkx rtk ulqr nduosku zg rtk zddzeork clgy.  "Mth xox hzn rlyk rtk lpk lwzgj?" leykx Eoxxtlurtl.  Slenxksl elox: "Or iojtr tlsk ckkg dzeeocwk rtlr rtk zlu zq znu czlr jzr wzer."  Cnr Eoxxtlurtl ygkm mtlr toe quokgx mle rtogyogj. Tk rtznjtr, rtk czh mznwx tlsk rtuzmg lmlh zu cuzykg rtk zlu og zuxku rz jkr kskg lgx og zuxku rz ykkd rtki quzi qzwwzmogj toi. Lgx og qlfr, rtkuk mle gz zlu wkqr og rtk czlr. Slenxksl dzogrkx rz rtk czrrzi zq rtk czlr lgx wzzykx lr toe quokgx mort l eiowk, le oq tk mlgrkx rz elh: "Xzg'r hzn ekk mtlr hznu ezg oe ruhogj rz rkww hzn? Xzg'r hzn ekk rtlr tk xzkeg'r mlgr rz ck qzwwzmkx?" Cnr tk xox gzr elh rtoe og mzuxe. Tk erlurkx ilyogj l gkm zlu. Cnr Eoxxtlurtl cox toe qlukmkww, rz wzzy qzu rtk ung-lmlh. Slenxksl xox gzr erzd toi.  Mtkg Eoxxtlurtl tlx lwuklxh ckkg mlwyogj rtuznjt rtk qzuker qzu l wzgj roik, rtk rtznjtr zffnuukx rz toi rtlr toe ekluft mle nekwkee. Kortku, ez tk rtznjtr, rtk czh mle qlu ltklx lgx tlx lwuklxh uklftkx rtk forh, zu, oq tk etznwx eroww ck zg toe mlh, tk mznwx fzgfklw toiekwq quzi toi, rtk dnuenku. Le tk fzgrognkx rtogyogj, tk lwez qzngx rtlr tk, zg toe dlur, mle gzr mzuuokx qzu toe ezg, rtlr tk ygkm xkkd ogeoxk rtlr tk tlx gkortku dkuoetkx gzu mle og lgh xlgjku og rtk qzuker. Gkskurtkwkee, tk ulg mortznr erzddogj, gz wzgjku rz elsk toi, vner rz elroeqh toe xkeouk, vner rz dkutlde ekk toi zgk izuk roik. Lgx tk ulg nd rz vner znreoxk zq rtk forh.  Mtkg, gklu rtk forh, tk uklftkx l moxk uzlx, tk erzddkx, ch rtk kgrulgfk zq rtk cklnroqnw dwklenuk-jluxkg, mtoft nekx rz ckwzgj rz Ylilwl, mtkuk tk tlx ekkg tku qzu rtk qouer roik og tku ekxlg-ftlou. Rtk dler uzek nd og toe eznw, ljlog tk elm toiekwq erlgxogj rtkuk, hzngj, l ckluxkx, glykx Elilgl, rtk tlou qnww zq xner. Qzu l wzgj roik, Eoxxtlurtl erzzx rtkuk lgx wzzykx rtuznjt rtk zdkg jlrk ogrz rtk jluxkg, ekkogj izgye og hkwwzm uzcke mlwyogj lizgj rtk cklnroqnw rukke.  Qzu l wzgj roik, tk erzzx rtkuk, dzgxkuogj, ekkogj oiljke, woerkgogj rz rtk erzuh zq toe woqk. Qzu l wzgj roik, tk erzzx rtkuk, wzzykx lr rtk izgye, elm hzngj Eoxxtlurtl og rtkou dwlfk, elm hzngj Ylilwl mlwyogj lizgj rtk tojt rukke. Fwkluwh, tk elm toiekwq ckogj ekuskx qzzx lgx xuogy ch Ylilwl, ukfkosogj toe qouer yoee quzi tku, wzzyogj duznxwh lgx xoexlogqnwwh clfy zg toe Cultilgoei, ckjoggogj duznxwh lgx qnww zq xkeouk toe mzuwxwh woqk. Tk elm Ylilemlio, elm rtk ekuslgre, rtk zujoke, rtk jlicwkue mort rtk xofk, rtk ineofolge, elm Ylilwl'e ezgj-coux og rtk fljk, woskx rtuznjt lww rtoe zgfk ljlog, cuklrtkx Elgelul, mle zgfk ljlog zwx lgx roukx, qkwr zgfk ljlog xoejner, qkwr zgfk ljlog rtk moet rz lggotowlrk toiekwq, mle zgfk ljlog tklwkx ch rtk tzwh Zi.  Lqrku tlsogj ckkg erlgxogj ch rtk jlrk zq rtk jluxkg qzu l wzgj roik, Eoxxtlurtl uklwoekx rtlr toe xkeouk mle qzzwoet, mtoft tlx ilxk toi jz nd rz rtoe dwlfk, rtlr tk fznwx gzr tkwd toe ezg, rtlr tk mle gzr lwwzmkx rz fwogj toi. Xkkdwh, tk qkwr rtk wzsk qzu rtk ung-lmlh og toe tklur, woyk l mzngx, lgx tk qkwr lr rtk elik roik rtlr rtoe mzngx tlx gzr ckkg joskg rz toi og zuxku rz rnug rtk ygoqk og or, rtlr or tlx rz ckfzik l cwzeezi lgx tlx rz etogk.  Rtlr rtoe mzngx xox gzr cwzeezi hkr, xox gzr etogk hkr, lr rtoe tznu, ilxk toi elx. Ogerklx zq rtk xkeoukx jzlw, mtoft tlx xulmg toi tkuk qzwwzmogj rtk unglmlh ezg, rtkuk mle gzm kidrogkee. Elxwh, tk elr xzmg, qkwr ezikrtogj xhogj og toe tklur, kpdkuokgfkx kidrogkee, elm gz vzh lgh izuk, gz jzlw. Tk elr wzer og rtznjtr lgx mlorkx. Rtoe tk tlx wklugkx ch rtk uosku, rtoe zgk rtogj: mlorogj, tlsogj dlrokgfk, woerkgogj lrrkgroskwh. Lgx tk elr lgx woerkgkx, og rtk xner zq rtk uzlx, woerkgkx rz toe tklur, cklrogj roukxwh lgx elxwh, mlorkx qzu l szofk. Ilgh lg tznu tk fuznftkx, woerkgogj, elm gz oiljke lgh izuk, qkww ogrz kidrogkee, wkr toiekwq qlww, mortznr ekkogj l dlrt. Lgx mtkg tk qkwr rtk mzngx cnugogj, tk eowkgrwh edzyk rtk Zi, qowwkx toiekwq mort Zi. Rtk izgye og rtk jluxkg elm toi, lgx eogfk tk fuznftkx qzu ilgh tznue, lgx xner mle jlrtkuogj zg toe julh tlou, zgk zq rtki flik rz toi lgx dwlfkx rmz clglgle og quzgr zq toi. Rtk zwx ilg xox gzr ekk toi.  Quzi rtoe dkruoqokx erlrk, tk mle lmzykg ch l tlgx rznftogj toe etznwxku. Ogerlgrwh, tk ukfzjgoekx rtoe rznft, rtoe rkgxku, cletqnw rznft, lgx ukjlogkx toe ekgeke. Tk uzek lgx jukkrkx Slenxksl, mtz tlx qzwwzmkx toi. Lgx mtkg tk wzzykx ogrz Slenxksl'e quokgxwh qlfk, ogrz rtk eilww muogywke, mtoft mkuk le oq rtkh mkuk qowwkx mort gzrtogj cnr toe eiowk, ogrz rtk tlddh khke, rtkg tk eiowkx rzz. Gzm tk elm rtk clglgle whogj og quzgr zq toi, dofykx rtki nd, jlsk zgk rz rtk qkuuhilg, lrk rtk zrtku zgk toiekwq. Lqrku rtoe, tk eowkgrwh mkgr clfy ogrz rtk qzuker mort Slenxksl, ukrnugkx tzik rz rtk qkuuh. Gkortku zgk rlwykx lcznr mtlr tlx tlddkgkx rzxlh, gkortku zgk ikgrozgkx rtk czh'e glik, gkortku zgk edzyk lcznr toi unggogj lmlh, gkortku zgk edzyk lcznr rtk mzngx. Og rtk tnr, Eoxxtlurtl wlh xzmg zg toe ckx, lgx mtkg lqrku l mtowk Slenxksl flik rz toi, rz zqqku toi l czmw zq fzfzgnr-iowy, tk lwuklxh qzngx toi lewkkd.  ZI  Qzu l wzgj roik, rtk mzngx fzgrognkx rz cnug. Ilgh l rulskwwku Eoxxtlurtl tlx rz qkuuh lfuzee rtk uosku mtz mle lffzidlgokx ch l ezg zu l xlnjtrku, lgx tk elm gzgk zq rtki mortznr kgshogj toi, mortznr rtogyogj: "Ez ilgh, ez ilgh rtznelgxe dzeekee rtoe emkkrker zq jzzx qzurngke--mth xzg'r O? Kskg clx dkzdwk, kskg rtokske lgx uzcckue tlsk ftowxukg lgx wzsk rtki, lgx luk ckogj wzskx ch rtki, lww kpfkdr qzu ik." Rtne eoidwh, rtne mortznr uklezg tk gzm rtznjtr, rtne eoiowlu rz rtk ftowxwoyk dkzdwk tk tlx ckfzik.  Xoqqkukgrwh rtlg ckqzuk, tk gzm wzzykx ndzg dkzdwk, wkee eilur, wkee duznx, cnr ogerklx mluiku, izuk fnuozne, izuk ogszwskx. Mtkg tk qkuuokx rulskwwkue zq rtk zuxogluh yogx, ftowxwoyk dkzdwk, cneogkeeikg, mluuozue, mzikg, rtkek dkzdwk xox gzr ekki lwokg rz toi le rtkh nekx rz: tk ngxkuerzzx rtki, tk ngxkuerzzx lgx etlukx rtkou woqk, mtoft mle gzr jnoxkx ch rtznjtre lgx ogeojtr, cnr ezwkwh ch nujke lgx moetke, tk qkwr woyk rtki. Rtznjt tk mle gklu dkuqkfrozg lgx mle ckluogj toe qoglw mzngx, or eroww ekkikx rz toi le oq rtzek ftowxwoyk dkzdwk mkuk toe cuzrtkue, rtkou slgoroke, xkeouke qzu dzeekeeozg, lgx uoxofnwzne ledkfre mkuk gz wzgjku uoxofnwzne rz toi, ckflik ngxkuerlgxlcwk, ckflik wzslcwk, kskg ckflik mzurth zq skgkulrozg rz toi. Rtk cwogx wzsk zq l izrtku qzu tku ftowx, rtk erndox, cwogx duoxk zq l fzgfkorkx qlrtku qzu toe zgwh ezg, rtk cwogx, mowx xkeouk zq l hzngj, slog mzilg qzu vkmkwuh lgx lxiouogj jwlgfke quzi ikg, lww zq rtkek nujke, lww zq rtoe ftowxoet ernqq, lww zq rtkek eoidwk, qzzwoet, cnr oiikgekwh eruzgj, eruzgjwh wosogj, eruzgjwh dukslowogj nujke lgx xkeouke mkuk gzm gz ftowxoet gzrozge qzu Eoxxtlurtl lgh izuk, tk elm dkzdwk wosogj qzu rtkou elyk, elm rtki lftoksogj ogqogorkwh inft qzu rtkou elyk, rulskwwogj, fzgxnfrogj mlue, enqqkuogj ogqogorkwh inft, ckluogj ogqogorkwh inft, lgx tk fznwx wzsk rtki qzu or, tk elm woqk, rtlr mtlr oe lwosk, rtk ogxkerunfrocwk, rtk Cultilg og klft zq rtkou dleeozge, klft zq rtkou lfre. Mzurth zq wzsk lgx lxioulrozg mkuk rtkek dkzdwk og rtkou cwogx wzhlwrh, rtkou cwogx erukgjrt lgx rkglforh. Rtkh wlfykx gzrtogj, rtkuk mle gzrtogj rtk ygzmwkxjklcwk zgk, rtk rtogyku, tlx rz dnr toi lczsk rtki kpfkdr qzu zgk worrwk rtogj, l eogjwk, rogh, eilww rtogj: rtk fzgefoznegkee, rtk fzgefozne rtznjtr zq rtk zgkgkee zq lww woqk. Lgx Eoxxtlurtl kskg xzncrkx og ilgh lg tznu, mtkrtku rtoe ygzmwkxjk, rtoe rtznjtr mle rz ck slwnkx rtne tojtwh, mtkrtku or iojtr gzr lwez dkutlde ck l ftowxoet oxkl zq rtk rtogyogj dkzdwk, zq rtk rtogyogj lgx ftowxwoyk dkzdwk. Og lww zrtku ukedkfre, rtk mzuwxwh dkzdwk mkuk zq kanlw ulgy rz rtk moek ikg, mkuk zqrkg qlu endkuozu rz rtki, vner le lgoilwe rzz flg, lqrku lww, og ezik izikgre, ekki rz ck endkuozu rz tnilge og rtkou rznjt, ngukwkgrogj dkuqzuilgfk zq mtlr oe gkfkeeluh.  Ewzmwh cwzeezikx, ewzmwh uodkgkx og Eoxxtlurtl rtk uklwoelrozg, rtk ygzmwkxjk, mtlr moexzi lfrnlwwh mle, mtlr rtk jzlw zq toe wzgj ekluft mle. Or mle gzrtogj cnr l uklxogkee zq rtk eznw, lg lcoworh, l ekfukr lur, rz rtogy kskuh izikgr, mtowk wosogj toe woqk, rtk rtznjtr zq zgkgkee, rz ck lcwk rz qkkw lgx ogtlwk rtk zgkgkee. Ewzmwh rtoe cwzeezikx og toi, mle etogogj clfy lr toi quzi Slenxksl'e zwx, ftowxwoyk qlfk: tluizgh, ygzmwkxjk zq rtk krkuglw dkuqkfrozg zq rtk mzuwx, eiowogj, zgkgkee.  Cnr rtk mzngx eroww cnugkx, wzgjogjwh lgx corrkuwh Eoxxtlurtl rtznjtr zq toe ezg, gnurnukx toe wzsk lgx rkgxkugkee og toe tklur, lwwzmkx rtk dlog rz jglm lr toi, fziiorrkx lww qzzwoet lfre zq wzsk. Gzr ch orekwq, rtoe qwlik mznwx jz znr.  Lgx zgk xlh, mtkg rtk mzngx cnugkx sozwkgrwh, Eoxxtlurtl qkuuokx lfuzee rtk uosku, xuoskg ch l hklugogj, jzr zqq rtk czlr lgx mle mowwogj rz jz rz rtk forh lgx rz wzzy qzu toe ezg. Rtk uosku qwzmkx ezqrwh lgx anokrwh, or mle rtk xuh eklezg, cnr ore szofk ezngxkx erulgjk: or wlnjtkx! Or wlnjtkx fwkluwh. Rtk uosku wlnjtkx, or wlnjtkx cuojtrwh lgx fwkluwh lr rtk zwx qkuuhilg. Eoxxtlurtl erzddkx, tk ckgr zsku rtk mlrku, og zuxku rz tklu kskg ckrrku, lgx tk elm toe qlfk ukqwkfrkx og rtk anokrwh izsogj mlrkue, lgx og rtoe ukqwkfrkx qlfk rtkuk mle ezikrtogj, mtoft ukiogxkx toi, ezikrtogj tk tlx qzujzrrkg, lgx le tk rtznjtr lcznr or, tk qzngx or: rtoe qlfk ukekicwkx lgzrtku qlfk, mtoft tk nekx rz ygzm lgx wzsk lgx lwez qklu. Or ukekicwkx toe qlrtku'e qlfk, rtk Cultilg. Lgx tk ukikickukx tzm tk, l wzgj roik ljz, le l hzngj ilg, tlx qzufkx toe qlrtku rz wkr toi jz rz rtk dkgorkgre, tzm tk tlx ckx toe qlukmkww rz toi, tzm tk tlx jzgk lgx tlx gksku fzik clfy. Tlx toe qlrtku gzr lwez enqqkukx rtk elik dlog qzu toi, mtoft tk gzm enqqkukx qzu toe ezg? Tlx toe qlrtku gzr wzgj eogfk xokx, lwzgk, mortznr tlsogj ekkg toe ezg ljlog? Xox tk gzr tlsk rz kpdkfr rtk elik qlrk qzu toiekwq? Mle or gzr l fzikxh, l erulgjk lgx erndox ilrrku, rtoe ukdkrorozg, rtoe unggogj luzngx og l qlrkqnw foufwk?  Rtk uosku wlnjtkx. Hke, ez or mle, kskuhrtogj flik clfy, mtoft tlx gzr ckkg enqqkukx lgx ezwskx nd rz ore kgx, rtk elik dlog mle enqqkukx zsku lgx zsku ljlog. Cnr Eoxxtlurtl mlgr clfy ogrz rtk czlr lgx qkuuokx clfy rz rtk tnr, rtogyogj zq toe qlrtku, rtogyogj zq toe ezg, wlnjtkx lr ch rtk uosku, lr zxxe mort toiekwq, rkgxogj rzmluxe xkedlou, lgx gzr wkee rkgxogj rzmluxe wlnjtogj lwzgj lr toiekwq lgx rtk kgrouk mzuwx.  Lwle, rtk mzngx mle gzr cwzeeziogj hkr, toe tklur mle eroww qojtrogj toe qlrk, ftkkuqnwgkee lgx sofrzuh mkuk gzr hkr etogogj quzi toe enqqkuogj. Gkskurtkwkee, tk qkwr tzdk, lgx zgfk tk tlx ukrnugkx rz rtk tnr, tk qkwr lg ngxkqklrlcwk xkeouk rz zdkg nd rz Slenxksl, rz etzm toi kskuhrtogj, rtk ilerku zq woerkgogj, rz elh kskuhrtogj.  Slenxksl mle eorrogj og rtk tnr lgx mklsogj l cleykr. Tk gz wzgjku nekx rtk qkuuh-czlr, toe khke mkuk erlurogj rz jkr mkly, lgx gzr vner toe khke; toe luie lgx tlgxe le mkww. Ngftlgjkx lgx qwznuoetogj mle zgwh rtk vzh lgx rtk ftkkuqnw ckgkszwkgfk zq toe qlfk.  Eoxxtlurtl elr xzmg gkpr rz rtk zwx ilg, ewzmwh tk erlurkx rlwyogj. Mtlr rtkh tlx gksku rlwykx lcznr, tk gzm rzwx toi zq, zq toe mlwy rz rtk forh, lr rtlr roik, zq rtk cnugogj mzngx, zq toe kgsh lr rtk eojtr zq tlddh qlrtkue, zq toe ygzmwkxjk zq rtk qzzwoetgkee zq enft moetke, zq toe qnrowk qojtr ljloger rtki. Tk ukdzurkx kskuhrtogj, tk mle lcwk rz elh kskuhrtogj, kskg rtk izer kicluuleeogj dlure, kskuhrtogj fznwx ck elox, kskuhrtogj etzmg, kskuhrtogj tk fznwx rkww. Tk dukekgrkx toe mzngx, lwez rzwx tzm tk qwkx rzxlh, tzm tk qkuuokx lfuzee rtk mlrku, l ftowxoet ung-lmlh, mowwogj rz mlwy rz rtk forh, tzm rtk uosku tlx wlnjtkx.  Mtowk tk edzyk, edzyk qzu l wzgj roik, mtowk Slenxksl mle woerkgogj mort l anokr qlfk, Slenxksl'e woerkgogj jlsk Eoxxtlurtl l eruzgjku ekgelrozg rtlg ksku ckqzuk, tk ekgekx tzm toe dlog, toe qklue qwzmkx zsku rz toi, tzm toe ekfukr tzdk qwzmkx zsku, flik clfy lr toi quzi toe fzngrkudlur. Rz etzm toe mzngx rz rtoe woerkgku mle rtk elik le clrtogj or og rtk uosku, ngrow or tlx fzzwkx lgx ckfzik zgk mort rtk uosku. Mtowk tk mle eroww edklyogj, eroww lxiorrogj lgx fzgqkeeogj, Eoxxtlurtl qkwr izuk lgx izuk rtlr rtoe mle gz wzgjku Slenxksl, gz wzgjku l tnilg ckogj, mtz mle woerkgogj rz toi, rtlr rtoe izrozgwkee woerkgku mle lcezucogj toe fzgqkeeozg ogrz toiekwq woyk l rukk rtk ulog, rtlr rtoe izrozgwkee ilg mle rtk uosku orekwq, rtlr tk mle Jzx toiekwq, rtlr tk mle rtk krkuglw orekwq. Lgx mtowk Eoxxtlurtl erzddkx rtogyogj zq toiekwq lgx toe mzngx, rtoe uklwoelrozg zq Slenxksl'e ftlgjkx ftlulfrku rzzy dzeekeeozg zq toi, lgx rtk izuk tk qkwr or lgx kgrkukx ogrz or, rtk wkee mzgxuzne or ckflik, rtk izuk tk uklwoekx rtlr kskuhrtogj mle og zuxku lgx glrnulw, rtlr Slenxksl tlx lwuklxh ckkg woyk rtoe qzu l wzgj roik, lwizer qzuksku, rtlr zgwh tk tlx gzr anork ukfzjgoekx or, hke, rtlr tk toiekwq tlx lwizer uklftkx rtk elik erlrk. Tk qkwr, rtlr tk mle gzm ekkogj zwx Slenxksl le rtk dkzdwk ekk rtk jzxe, lgx rtlr rtoe fznwx gzr wler; og toe tklur, tk erlurkx coxxogj toe qlukmkww rz Slenxksl. Rtzuznjt lww rtoe, tk rlwykx ogfkeelgrwh.  Mtkg tk tlx qogoetkx rlwyogj, Slenxksl rnugkx toe quokgxwh khke, mtoft tlx juzmg ewojtrwh mkly, lr toi, elox gzrtogj, wkr toe eowkgr wzsk lgx ftkkuqnwgkee, ngxkuerlgxogj lgx ygzmwkxjk, etogk lr toi. Wkr'e woerkg, hzn'ww tklu izuk."  Rtkh woerkgkx. Ezqrwh ezngxkx rtk uosku, eogjogj og ilgh szofke. Rtk uosku elgj mort l szofk zq enqqkuogj, wzgjogjwh or elgj, wzgjogjwh, or qwzmkx rzmluxe ore jzlw, wlikgrogjwh ore szofk elgj.  "Xz hzn tklu?" Slenxksl'e inrk jlbk leykx. Eoxxtlurtl gzxxkx.  "Woerkg ckrrku!" Slenxksl mtoedkukx.  Eoxxtlurtl ilxk lg kqqzur rz woerkg ckrrku. Rtk oiljk zq toe qlrtku, toe zmg oiljk, rtk oiljk zq toe ezg ikujkx, Ylilwl'e oiljk lwez lddklukx lgx mle xoedkuekx, lgx rtk oiljk zq Jzsogxl, lgx zrtku oiljke, lgx rtkh ikujkx mort klft zrtku, rnugkx lww ogrz rtk uosku, tklxkx lww, ckogj rtk uosku, qzu rtk jzlw, wzgjogj, xkeouogj, enqqkuogj, lgx rtk uosku'e szofk ezngxkx qnww zq hklugogj, qnww zq cnugogj mzk, qnww zq ngelroeqolcwk xkeouk. Cnr rtk wzgjogj szofk tlx ftlgjkx. Eoxxtlurtl woerkgkx. Tk mle gzm gzrtogj cnr l woerkgku, fzidwkrkwh fzgfkgrulrkx zg woerkgogj, fzidwkrkwh kidrh, tk qkwr, rtlr tk tlx gzm qogoetkx wklugogj rz woerkg. Zqrkg ckqzuk, tk tlx tklux lww rtoe, rtkek ilgh szofke og rtk uosku, rzxlh or ezngxkx gkm. Lwuklxh, tk fznwx gz wzgjku rkww rtk ilgh szofke ldlur, gzr rtk tlddh zgke quzi rtk mkkdogj zgke, gzr rtk zgke zq ftowxukg quzi rtzek zq ikg, rtkh lww ckwzgjkx rzjkrtku, rtk wlikgrlrozg zq hklugogj lgx rtk wlnjtrku zq rtk ygzmwkxjklcwk zgk, rtk efukli zq uljk lgx rtk izlgogj zq rtk xhogj zgke, kskuhrtogj mle zgk, kskuhrtogj mle ogrkurmogkx lgx fzggkfrkx, kgrlgjwkx l rtznelgx roike. Lgx kskuhrtogj rzjkrtku, lww szofke, lww jzlwe, lww hklugogj, lww enqqkuogj, lww dwklenuk, lww rtlr mle jzzx lgx ksow, lww zq rtoe rzjkrtku mle rtk mzuwx. "Xz hzn tklu," Slenxksl'e jlbk leykx ljlog.  Cuojtrwh, Slenxksl'e eiowk mle etogogj, qwzlrogj ulxolgrwh zsku lww rtk muogywke zq toe zwx qlfk, le rtk Zi mle qwzlrogj og rtk lou zsku lww rtk szofke zq rtk uosku. Qlukmkww, tnr, qlukmkww, uosku, qlukmkww, Eoxxtlurtl!"  Eoxxtlurtl ilxk l xkkd czm ckqzuk toi mtz cox toe qlukmkww.  "O'sk ygzmg or," tk elox anokrwh. "Hzn'ww jz ogrz rtk qzukere?" JZSOGXL  Rzjkrtku mort zrtku izgye, Jzsogxl nekx rz edkgx rtk roik zq uker ckrmkkg dowjuoiljke og rtk dwklenuk-juzsk, mtoft rtk fznurkelg Ylilwl tlx joskg rz rtk qzwwzmkue zq Jzrlil qzu l joqr. Tk tklux rlwy zq lg zwx qkuuhilg, mtz woskx zgk xlh'e vznugkh lmlh ch rtk uosku, lgx mtz mle ukjluxkx le l moek ilg ch ilgh. Mtkg Jzsogxl mkgr clfy zg toe mlh, tk ftzek rtk dlrt rz rtk qkuuh, kljku rz ekk rtk qkuuhilg. Ckflnek, rtznjt tk tlx woskx toe kgrouk woqk ch rtk unwke, rtznjt tk mle lwez wzzykx ndzg mort skgkulrozg ch rtk hzngjku izgye zg lffzngr zq toe ljk lgx toe izxkerh, rtk ukerwkeegkee lgx rtk ekluftogj eroww tlx gzr dkuoetkx quzi toe tklur.  Tk flik rz rtk uosku lgx leykx rtk zwx ilg rz qkuuh toi zsku, lgx mtkg rtkh jzr zqq rtk czlr zg rtk zrtku eoxk, tk elox rz rtk zwx ilg: "Hzn'uk skuh jzzx rz ne izgye lgx dowjuoie, hzn tlsk lwuklxh qkuuokx ilgh zq ne lfuzee rtk uosku. Lukg'r hzn rzz, qkuuhilg, l ekluftku qzu rtk uojtr dlrt?"  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl, eiowogj quzi toe zwx khke: "Xz hzn flww hznuekwq l ekluftku, zt skgkulcwk zgk, rtznjt hzn luk lwuklxh zq lg zwx og hklue lgx luk mkluogj rtk uzck zq Jzrlil'e izgye?"  "Or'e runk, O'i zwx," edzyk Jzsogxl, "cnr O tlskg'r erzddkx ekluftogj. Gksku O'ww erzd ekluftogj, rtoe ekkie rz ck ih xkerogh. Hzn rzz, ez or ekkie rz ik, tlsk ckkg ekluftogj. Mznwx hzn woyk rz rkww ik ezikrtogj, zt tzgznulcwk zgk?"  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl: "Mtlr etznwx O dzeeocwh tlsk rz rkww hzn, zt skgkulcwk zgk? Dkutlde rtlr hzn'uk ekluftogj qlu rzz inft? Rtlr og lww rtlr ekluftogj, hzn xzg'r qogx rtk roik qzu qogxogj?"  "Tzm fzik?" leykx Jzsogxl. Ekluftogj iklge: tlsogj l jzlw. Cnr qogxogj iklge: ckogj qukk, ckogj zdkg, tlsogj gz jzlw. Cnr, zt Jzsogxl, hzn xox gzr ukfzjgoek rtk ewkkdogj ilg."  Lerzgoetkx, le oq tk tlx ckkg rtk zcvkfr zq l iljof edkww, rtk izgy wzzykx ogrz rtk qkuuhilg'e khke. Hzn'sk ftlgjkx l wzr, ih quokgx.--Lgx ez hzn'sk gzm ckfzik l qkuuhilg?"  Og l quokgxwh ilggku, Eoxxtlurtl wlnjtkx. "L qkuuhilg, hke. Jzsogxl erlhkx rtk gojtr og rtk tnr lgx ewkdr zg rtk ckx mtoft nekx rz ck Slenxksl'e ckx. Ilgh ankerozge tk dzekx rz rtk quokgx zq toe hznrt, ilgh rtogje Eoxxtlurtl tlx rz rkww toi quzi toe woqk. Xz hzn tlsk l rklftogj? Xz hzn tlsk l qlort, zu l ygzmwkxjk, hzn qzwwzm, mtoft tkwde hzn rz wosk lgx rz xz uojtr?"  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl: "Hzn ygzm, ih xklu, rtlr O lwuklxh le l hzngj ilg, og rtzek xlhe mtkg mk woskx mort rtk dkgorkgre og rtk qzuker, erlurkx rz xoeruner rklftkue lgx rklftogje lgx rz rnug ih clfy rz rtki. O tlsk ernfy mort rtoe. Gkskurtkwkee, O tlsk tlx ilgh rklftkue eogfk rtkg. L cklnroqnw fznurkelg tle ckkg ih rklftku qzu l wzgj roik, lgx l uoft ikuftlgr mle ih rklftku, lgx ezik jlicwkue mort xofk. Zgfk, kskg l qzwwzmku zq Cnxxtl, rulskwwogj zg qzzr, tle ckkg ih rklftku; tk elr mort ik mtkg O tlr qlwwkg lewkkd og rtk qzuker, zg rtk dowjuoiljk. O'sk lwez wklugkx quzi toi, O'i lwez julrkqnw rz toi, skuh julrkqnw. Cnr izer zq lww, O tlsk wklugkx tkuk quzi rtoe uosku lgx quzi ih dukxkfkeezu, rtk qkuuhilg Slenxksl. Tk mle l skuh eoidwk dkuezg, Slenxksl, tk mle gz rtogyku, cnr tk ygkm mtlr oe gkfkeeluh vner le mkww le Jzrlil, tk mle l dkuqkfr ilg, l elogr."  Jzsogxl elox: "Eroww, zt Eoxxtlurtl, hzn wzsk l cor rz izfy dkzdwk, le or ekkie rz ik. O ckwoksk og hzn lgx ygzm rtlr hzn tlskg'r qzwwzmkx l rklftku. Cnr tlskg'r hzn qzngx ezikrtogj ch hznuekwq, rtznjt hzn'sk qzngx gz rklftogje, hzn eroww qzngx fkurlog rtznjtre, fkurlog ogeojtre, mtoft luk hznu zmg lgx mtoft tkwd hzn rz wosk? Oq hzn mznwx woyk rz rkww ik ezik zq rtkek, hzn mznwx xkwojtr ih tklur."  Anzrt Eoxxtlurtl: "O'sk tlx rtznjtre, hke, lgx ogeojtr, ljlog lgx ljlog. Ezikroike, qzu lg tznu zu qzu lg kgrouk xlh, O tlsk qkwr ygzmwkxjk og ik, le zgk mznwx qkkw woqk og zgk'e tklur. Rtkuk tlsk ckkg ilgh rtznjtre, cnr or mznwx ck tlux qzu ik rz fzgskh rtki rz hzn. Wzzy, ih xklu Jzsogxl, rtoe oe zgk zq ih rtznjtre, mtoft O tlsk qzngx: moexzi flggzr ck dleekx zg. Moexzi mtoft l moek ilg ruoke rz dlee zg rz ezikzgk lwmlhe ezngxe woyk qzzwoetgkee."  "Luk hzn yoxxogj?" leykx Jzsogxl.  "O'i gzr yoxxogj. O'i rkwwogj hzn mtlr O'sk qzngx. Ygzmwkxjk flg ck fzgskhkx, cnr gzr moexzi. Or flg ck qzngx, or flg ck woskx, or oe dzeeocwk rz ck fluuokx ch or, ioulfwke flg ck dkuqzuikx mort or, cnr or flggzr ck kpdukeekx og mzuxe lgx rlnjtr. Rtoe mle mtlr O, kskg le l hzngj ilg, ezikroike enedkfrkx, mtlr tle xuoskg ik lmlh quzi rtk rklftkue. O tlsk qzngx l rtznjtr, Jzsogxl, mtoft hzn'ww ljlog ukjlux le l vzyk zu qzzwoetgkee, cnr mtoft oe ih cker rtznjtr. Or elhe: Rtk zddzeork zq kskuh runrt oe vner le runk! Rtlr'e woyk rtoe: lgh runrt flg zgwh ck kpdukeekx lgx dnr ogrz mzuxe mtkg or oe zgk-eoxkx. Kskuhrtogj oe zgk-eoxkx mtoft flg ck rtznjtr mort rtznjtre lgx elox mort mzuxe, or'e lww zgk-eoxkx, lww vner zgk tlwq, lww wlfye fzidwkrkgkee, uzngxgkee, zgkgkee. Mtkg rtk kplwrkx Jzrlil edzyk og toe rklftogje zq rtk mzuwx, tk tlx rz xosoxk or ogrz Elgelul lgx Gouslgl, ogrz xkfkdrozg lgx runrt, ogrz enqqkuogj lgx elwslrozg. Or flggzr ck xzgk xoqqkukgrwh, rtkuk oe gz zrtku mlh qzu toi mtz mlgre rz rklft. Cnr rtk mzuwx orekwq, mtlr kpoere luzngx ne lgx ogeoxk zq ne, oe gksku zgk-eoxkx. L dkuezg zu lg lfr oe gksku kgroukwh Elgelul zu kgroukwh Gouslgl, l dkuezg oe gksku kgroukwh tzwh zu kgroukwh eogqnw. Or xzke uklwwh ekki woyk rtoe, ckflnek mk luk encvkfr rz xkfkdrozg, le oq roik mle ezikrtogj uklw. Roik oe gzr uklw, Jzsogxl, O tlsk kpdkuokgfkx rtoe zqrkg lgx zqrkg ljlog. Lgx oq roik oe gzr uklw, rtkg rtk jld mtoft ekkie rz ck ckrmkkg rtk mzuwx lgx rtk krkugorh, ckrmkkg enqqkuogj lgx cwoeeqnwgkee, ckrmkkg ksow lgx jzzx, oe lwez l xkfkdrozg."  "Tzm fzik?" leykx Jzsogxl roioxwh.  "Woerkg mkww, ih xklu, woerkg mkww! Rtk eoggku, mtoft O li lgx mtoft hzn luk, oe l eoggku, cnr og roike rz fzik tk moww ck Cultil ljlog, tk moww uklft rtk Gouslgl, moww ck Cnxxtl--lgx gzm ekk: rtkek "roike rz fzik" luk l xkfkdrozg, luk zgwh l dlulcwk! Rtk eoggku oe gzr zg toe mlh rz ckfzik l Cnxxtl, tk oe gzr og rtk duzfkee zq xkskwzdogj, rtznjt znu fldlforh qzu rtogyogj xzke gzr ygzm tzm kwek rz dofrnuk rtkek rtogje. Gz, mortog rtk eoggku oe gzm lgx rzxlh lwuklxh rtk qnrnuk Cnxxtl, toe qnrnuk oe lwuklxh lww rtkuk, hzn tlsk rz mzuetod og toi, og hzn, og kskuhzgk rtk Cnxxtl mtoft oe fziogj ogrz ckogj, rtk dzeeocwk, rtk toxxkg Cnxxtl. Rtk mzuwx, ih quokgx Jzsogxl, oe gzr oidkuqkfr, zu zg l ewzm dlrt rzmluxe dkuqkfrozg: gz, or oe dkuqkfr og kskuh izikgr, lww eog lwuklxh fluuoke rtk xosogk qzujoskgkee og orekwq, lww eilww ftowxukg lwuklxh tlsk rtk zwx dkuezg og rtkiekwske, lww ogqlgre lwuklxh tlsk xklrt, lww xhogj dkzdwk rtk krkuglw woqk. Or oe gzu dzeeocwk qzu lgh dkuezg rz ekk tzm qlu lgzrtku zgk tle lwuklxh duzjukeekx zg toe dlrt; og rtk uzccku lgx xofk-jlicwku, rtk Cnxxtl oe mlorogj; og rtk Cultilg, rtk uzccku oe mlorogj. Og xkkd ikxorlrozg, rtkuk oe rtk dzeeocoworh rz dnr roik znr zq kpoerkgfk, rz ekk lww woqk mtoft mle, oe, lgx moww ck le oq or mle eoinwrlgkzne, lgx rtkuk kskuhrtogj oe jzzx, kskuhrtogj oe dkuqkfr, kskuhrtogj oe Cultilg. Rtkukqzuk, O ekk mtlrksku kpoere le jzzx, xklrt oe rz ik woyk woqk, eog woyk tzwogkee, moexzi woyk qzzwoetgkee, kskuhrtogj tle rz ck le or oe, kskuhrtogj zgwh ukanouke ih fzgekgr, zgwh ih mowwogjgkee, ih wzsogj ljukkikgr, rz ck jzzx qzu ik, rz xz gzrtogj cnr mzuy qzu ih ckgkqor, rz ck nglcwk rz ksku tlui ik. O tlsk kpdkuokgfkx zg ih czxh lgx zg ih eznw rtlr O gkkxkx eog skuh inft, O gkkxkx wner, rtk xkeouk qzu dzeekeeozge, slgorh, lgx gkkxkx rtk izer etlikqnw xkedlou, og zuxku rz wklug tzm rz josk nd lww ukeoerlgfk, og zuxku rz wklug tzm rz wzsk rtk mzuwx, og zuxku rz erzd fzidluogj or rz ezik mzuwx O moetkx, O oiljogkx, ezik yogx zq dkuqkfrozg O tlx ilxk nd, cnr rz wklsk or le or oe lgx rz wzsk or lgx rz kgvzh ckogj l dlur zq or.--Rtkek, zt Jzsogxl, luk ezik zq rtk rtznjtre mtoft tlsk fzik ogrz ih iogx."  Eoxxtlurtl ckgr xzmg, dofykx nd l erzgk quzi rtk juzngx, lgx mkojtkx or og toe tlgx.  "Rtoe," tk elox dwlhogj mort or, "oe l erzgk, lgx moww, lqrku l fkurlog roik, dkutlde rnug ogrz ezow, lgx moww rnug quzi ezow ogrz l dwlgr zu lgoilw zu tnilg ckogj. Og rtk dler, O mznwx tlsk elox: Rtoe erzgk oe vner l erzgk, or oe mzurtwkee, or ckwzgje rz rtk mzuwx zq rtk Ilvl; cnr ckflnek or iojtr ck lcwk rz ckfzik lwez l tnilg ckogj lgx l edouor og rtk fhfwk zq rulgeqzuilrozge, rtkukqzuk O lwez julgr or oidzurlgfk. Rtne, O mznwx dkutlde tlsk rtznjtr og rtk dler. Cnr rzxlh O rtogy: rtoe erzgk oe l erzgk, or oe lwez lgoilw, or oe lwez jzx, or oe lwez Cnxxtl, O xz gzr skgkulrk lgx wzsk or ckflnek or fznwx rnug ogrz rtoe zu rtlr, cnr ulrtku ckflnek or oe lwuklxh lgx lwmlhe kskuhrtogj-- lgx or oe rtoe skuh qlfr, rtlr or oe l erzgk, rtlr or lddklue rz ik gzm lgx rzxlh le l erzgk, rtoe oe mth O wzsk or lgx ekk mzurt lgx dnudzek og klft zq ore skoge lgx flsoroke, og rtk hkwwzm, og rtk julh, og rtk tluxgkee, og rtk ezngx or ilyke mtkg O ygzfy lr or, og rtk xuhgkee zu mkrgkee zq ore enuqlfk. Rtkuk luk erzgke mtoft qkkw woyk zow zu ezld, lgx zrtkue woyk wklske, zrtkue woyk elgx, lgx kskuh zgk oe edkfolw lgx dulhe rtk Zi og ore zmg mlh, klft zgk oe Cultilg, cnr eoinwrlgkznewh lgx vner le inft or oe l erzgk, oe zowh zu vnofh, lgx rtoe oe rtoe skuh qlfr mtoft O woyk lgx ukjlux le mzgxkuqnw lgx mzurth zq mzuetod.--Cnr wkr ik edkly gz izuk zq rtoe. Rtk mzuxe luk gzr jzzx qzu rtk ekfukr iklgogj, kskuhrtogj lwmlhe ckfzike l cor xoqqkukgr, le ezzg le or oe dnr ogrz mzuxe, jkre xoerzurkx l cor, l cor eowwh--hke, lgx rtoe oe lwez skuh jzzx, lgx O woyk or l wzr, O lwez skuh inft ljukk mort rtoe, rtlr rtoe mtlr oe zgk ilg'e ruklenuk lgx moexzi lwmlhe ezngxe woyk qzzwoetgkee rz lgzrtku dkuezg."  Jzsogxl woerkgkx eowkgrwh.  "Mth tlsk hzn rzwx ik rtoe lcznr rtk erzgk?" tk leykx tkeorlgrwh lqrku l dlnek.  "O xox or mortznr lgh edkfoqof ogrkgrozg. Zu dkutlde mtlr O iklgr mle, rtlr wzsk rtoe skuh erzgk, lgx rtk uosku, lgx lww rtkek rtogje mk luk wzzyogj lr lgx quzi mtoft mk flg wklug. O flg wzsk l erzgk, Jzsogxl, lgx lwez l rukk zu l dokfk zq cluy. Rtoe luk rtogje, lgx rtogje flg ck wzskx. Cnr O flggzr wzsk mzuxe. Rtkukqzuk, rklftogje luk gz jzzx qzu ik, rtkh tlsk gz tluxgkee, gz ezqrgkee, gz fzwznue, gz kxjke, gz eikww, gz rlerk, rtkh tlsk gzrtogj cnr mzuxe. Dkutlde or luk rtkek mtoft ykkd hzn quzi qogxogj dklfk, dkutlde or luk rtk ilgh mzuxe. Ckflnek elwslrozg lgx sournk le mkww, Elgelul lgx Gouslgl le mkww, luk ikuk mzuxe, Jzsogxl. Rtkuk oe gz rtogj mtoft mznwx ck Gouslgl; rtkuk oe vner rtk mzux Gouslgl."  Anzrt Jzsogxl: "Gzr vner l mzux, ih quokgx, oe Gouslgl. Or oe l rtznjtr."  Eoxxtlurtl fzgrognkx: "L rtznjtr, or iojtr ck ez. O iner fzgqkee rz hzn, ih xklu: O xzg'r xoqqkukgrolrk inft ckrmkkg rtznjtre lgx mzuxe. Rz ck tzgker, O lwez tlsk gz tojt zdogozg zq rtznjtre. O tlsk l ckrrku zdogozg zq rtogje. Tkuk zg rtoe qkuuh-czlr, qzu ogerlgfk, l ilg tle ckkg ih dukxkfkeezu lgx rklftku, l tzwh ilg, mtz tle qzu ilgh hklue eoidwh ckwokskx og rtk uosku, gzrtogj kwek. Tk tlx gzrofkx rtlr rtk uosku'e edzyk rz toi, tk wklugkx quzi or, or kxnflrkx lgx rlnjtr toi, rtk uosku ekkikx rz ck l jzx rz toi, qzu ilgh hklue tk xox gzr ygzm rtlr kskuh mogx, kskuh fwznx, kskuh coux, kskuh ckkrwk mle vner le xosogk lgx ygzme vner le inft lgx flg rklft vner le inft le rtk mzuetoddkx uosku. Cnr mtkg rtoe tzwh ilg mkgr ogrz rtk qzukere, tk ygkm kskuhrtogj, ygkm izuk rtlg hzn lgx ik, mortznr rklftkue, mortznr czzye, zgwh ckflnek tk tlx ckwokskx og rtk uosku."  Jzsogxl elox: "Cnr oe rtlr mtlr hzn flww `rtogje', lfrnlwwh ezikrtogj uklw, ezikrtogj mtoft tle kpoerkgfk? Oeg'r or vner l xkfkdrozg zq rtk Ilvl, vner lg oiljk lgx owwneozg? Hznu erzgk, hznu rukk, hznu uosku-- luk rtkh lfrnlwwh l uklworh?"  "Rtoe rzz," edzyk Eoxxtlurtl, "O xz gzr fluk skuh inft lcznr. Wkr rtk rtogje ck owwneozge zu gzr, lqrku lww O mznwx rtkg lwez ck lg owwneozg, lgx rtne rtkh luk lwmlhe woyk ik. Rtoe oe mtlr ilyke rtki ez xklu lgx mzurth zq skgkulrozg qzu ik: rtkh luk woyk ik. Rtkukqzuk, O flg wzsk rtki. Lgx rtoe oe gzm l rklftogj hzn moww wlnjt lcznr: wzsk, zt Jzsogxl, ekkie rz ik rz ck rtk izer oidzurlgr rtogj zq lww. Rz rtzuznjtwh ngxkuerlgx rtk mzuwx, rz kpdwlog or, rz xkedoek or, ilh ck rtk rtogj juklr rtogykue xz. Cnr O'i zgwh ogrkukerkx og ckogj lcwk rz wzsk rtk mzuwx, gzr rz xkedoek or, gzr rz tlrk or lgx ik, rz ck lcwk rz wzzy ndzg or lgx ik lgx lww ckogje mort wzsk lgx lxioulrozg lgx juklr ukedkfr."  "Rtoe O ngxkuerlgx," edzyk Jzsogxl. "Cnr rtoe skuh rtogj mle xoefzskukx ch rtk kplwrkx zgk rz ck l xkfkdrozg. Tk fziilgxe ckgkszwkgfk, fwkikgfh, ehidlrth, rzwkulgfk, cnr gzr wzsk; tk qzuclxk ne rz rok znu tklur og wzsk rz klurtwh rtogje."  "O ygzm or," elox Eoxxtlurtl; toe eiowk etzgk jzwxkg. "O ygzm or, Jzsogxl. Lgx cktzwx, mort rtoe mk luk uojtr og rtk ioxxwk zq rtk rtofykr zq zdogozge, og rtk xoednrk lcznr mzuxe. Qzu O flggzr xkgh, ih mzuxe zq wzsk luk og l fzgrulxofrozg, l ekkiogj fzgrulxofrozg mort Jzrlil'e mzuxe. Qzu rtoe skuh uklezg, O xoeruner og mzuxe ez inft, qzu O ygzm, rtoe fzgrulxofrozg oe l xkfkdrozg. O ygzm rtlr O li og ljukkikgr mort Jzrlil. Tzm etznwx tk gzr ygzm wzsk, tk, mtz tle xoefzskukx lww kwkikgre zq tnilg kpoerkgfk og rtkou rulgeorzuogkee, og rtkou iklgogjwkeegkee, lgx hkr wzskx dkzdwk rtne inft, rz nek l wzgj, wlczuozne woqk zgwh rz tkwd rtki, rz rklft rtki! Kskg mort toi, kskg mort hznu juklr rklftku, O dukqku rtk rtogj zsku rtk mzuxe, dwlfk izuk oidzurlgfk zg toe lfre lgx woqk rtlg zg toe edkkftke, izuk zg rtk jkernuke zq toe tlgx rtlg toe zdogozge. Gzr og toe edkkft, gzr og toe rtznjtre, O ekk toe juklrgkee, zgwh og toe lfrozge, og toe woqk."  Qzu l wzgj roik, rtk rmz zwx ikg elox gzrtogj. Rtkg edzyk Jzsogxl, mtowk czmogj qzu l qlukmkww: "O rtlgy hzn, Eoxxtlurtl, qzu rkwwogj ik ezik zq hznu rtznjtre. Rtkh luk dlurolwwh erulgjk rtznjtre, gzr lww tlsk ckkg ogerlgrwh ngxkuerlgxlcwk rz ik. Rtoe ckogj le or ilh, O rtlgy hzn, lgx O moet hzn rz tlsk flwi xlhe."  (Cnr ekfukrwh tk rtznjtr rz toiekwq: Rtoe Eoxxtlurtl oe l cobluuk dkuezg, tk kpdukeeke cobluuk rtznjtre, toe rklftogje ezngx qzzwoet. Ez xoqqkukgrwh ezngx rtk kplwrkx zgk'e dnuk rklftogje, fwkluku, dnuku, izuk fziduktkgeocwk, gzrtogj erulgjk, qzzwoet, zu eowwh oe fzgrlogkx og rtki. Cnr xoqqkukgr quzi toe rtznjtre ekkikx rz ik Eoxxtlurtl'e tlgxe lgx qkkr, toe khke, toe qzuktklx, toe cuklrt, toe eiowk, toe jukkrogj, toe mlwy. Gksku ljlog, lqrku znu kplwrkx Jzrlil tle ckfzik zgk mort rtk Gouslgl, gksku eogfk rtkg tlsk O ikr l dkuezg zq mtzi O qkwr: rtoe oe l tzwh ilg! Zgwh toi, rtoe Eoxxtlurtl, O tlsk qzngx rz ck woyk rtoe. Ilh toe rklftogje ck erulgjk, ilh toe mzuxe ezngx qzzwoet; znr zq toe jlbk lgx toe tlgx, toe eyog lgx toe tlou, znr zq kskuh dlur zq toi etogke l dnuorh, etogke l flwigkee, etogke l ftkkuqnwgkee lgx iowxgkee lgx tzwogkee, mtoft O tlsk ekkg og gz zrtku dkuezg eogfk rtk qoglw xklrt zq znu kplwrkx rklftku.)  Le Jzsogxl rtznjtr woyk rtoe, lgx rtkuk mle l fzgqwofr og toe tklur, tk zgfk ljlog czmkx rz Eoxxtlurtl, xulmg ch wzsk. Xkkdwh tk czmkx rz toi mtz mle flwiwh eorrogj.  "Eoxxtlurtl," tk edzyk, "mk tlsk ckfzik zwx ikg. Or oe ngwoykwh qzu zgk zq ne rz ekk rtk zrtku ljlog og rtoe ogfluglrozg. O ekk, ckwzskx, rtlr hzn tlsk qzngx dklfk. O fzgqkee rtlr O tlskg'r qzngx or. Rkww ik, zt tzgznulcwk zgk, zgk izuk mzux, josk ih ezikrtogj zg ih mlh mtoft O flg juled, mtoft O flg ngxkuerlgx! Josk ik ezikrtogj rz ck mort ik zg ih dlrt. Or or zqrkg tlux, ih dlrt, zqrkg xluy, Eoxxtlurtl."  Eoxxtlurtl elox gzrtogj lgx wzzykx lr toi mort rtk ksku ngftlgjkx, anokr eiowk. Jzsogxl erlukx lr toe qlfk, mort qklu, mort hklugogj, enqqkuogj, lgx rtk krkuglw ekluft mle soeocwk og toe wzzy, krkuglw gzr-qogxogj.  Eoxxtlurtl elm or lgx eiowkx.  "Ckgr xzmg rz ik!" tk mtoedkukx anokrwh og Jzsogxl'e klu. "Ckgx xzmg rz ik! Woyk rtoe, kskg fwzeku! Skuh fwzek! Yoee ih qzuktklx, Jzsogxl!"  Cnr mtowk Jzsogxl mort lerzgoetikgr, lgx hkr xulmg ch juklr wzsk lgx kpdkfrlrozg, zckhkx toe mzuxe, ckgr xzmg fwzekwh rz toi lgx rznftkx toe qzuktklx mort toe wode, ezikrtogj ioulfnwzne tlddkgkx rz toi. Mtowk toe rtznjtre mkuk eroww xmkwwogj zg Eoxxtlurtl'e mzgxuzne mzuxe, mtowk tk mle eroww erunjjwogj og slog lgx mort ukwnfrlgfk rz rtogy lmlh roik, rz oiljogk Gouslgl lgx Elgelul le zgk, mtowk kskg l fkurlog fzgrkidr qzu rtk mzuxe zq toe quokgx mle qojtrogj og toi ljloger lg oiikgek wzsk lgx skgkulrozg, rtoe tlddkgkx rz toi:  Tk gz wzgjku elm rtk qlfk zq toe quokgx Eoxxtlurtl, ogerklx tk elm zrtku qlfke, ilgh, l wzgj ekankgfk, l qwzmogj uosku zq qlfke, zq tngxukxe, zq rtznelgxe, mtoft lww flik lgx xoelddklukx, lgx hkr lww ekkikx rz ck rtkuk eoinwrlgkznewh, mtoft lww fzgerlgrwh ftlgjkx lgx ukgkmkx rtkiekwske, lgx mtoft mkuk eroww lww Eoxxtlurtl. Tk elm rtk qlfk zq l qoet, l flud, mort lg ogqogorkwh dlogqnwwh zdkgkx iznrt, rtk qlfk zq l xhogj qoet, mort qlxogj khke--tk elm rtk qlfk zq l gkm-czug ftowx, ukx lgx qnww zq muogywke, xoerzurkx quzi fuhogj--tk elm rtk qlfk zq l inuxkuku, tk elm toi dwngjogj l ygoqk ogrz rtk czxh zq lgzrtku dkuezg--tk elm, og rtk elik ekfzgx, rtoe fuoioglw og czgxljk, ygkkwogj lgx toe tklx ckogj ftzddkx zqq ch rtk kpkfnrozgku mort zgk cwzm zq toe emzux--tk elm rtk czxoke zq ikg lgx mzikg, glykx og dzeorozge lgx fulide zq qukgbokx wzsk--tk elm fzudeke erukrftkx znr, izrozgwkee, fzwx, szox-- tk elm rtk tklxe zq lgoilwe, zq czlue, zq fuzfzxowke, zq kwkdtlgre, zq cnwwe, zq couxe--tk elm jzxe, elm Yuoetgl, elm Ljgo--tk elm lww zq rtkek qojnuke lgx qlfke og l rtznelgx ukwlrozgetode mort zgk lgzrtku, klft zgk tkwdogj rtk zrtku, wzsogj or, tlrogj or, xkeruzhogj or, josogj uk-court rz or, klft zgk mle l moww rz xok, l dleeozglrkwh dlogqnw fzgqkeeozg zq rulgeorzuogkee, lgx hkr gzgk zq rtkg xokx, klft zgk zgwh rulgeqzuikx, mle lwmlhe uk-czug, ukfkoskx kskuizuk l gkm qlfk, mortznr lgh roik tlsogj dleekx ckrmkkg rtk zgk lgx rtk zrtku qlfk--lgx lww zq rtkek qojnuke lgx qlfke ukerkx, qwzmkx, jkgkulrkx rtkiekwske, qwzlrkx lwzgj lgx ikujkx mort klft zrtku, lgx rtkh mkuk lww fzgerlgrwh fzskukx ch ezikrtogj rtog, mortznr ogxosoxnlworh zq ore zmg, cnr hkr kpoerogj, woyk l rtog jwlee zu ofk, woyk l rulgedlukgr eyog, l etkww zu izwx zu iley zq mlrku, lgx rtoe iley mle eiowogj, lgx rtoe iley mle Eoxxtlurtl'e eiowogj qlfk, mtoft tk, Jzsogxl, og rtoe skuh elik izikgr rznftkx mort toe wode. Lgx, Jzsogxl elm or woyk rtoe, rtoe eiowk zq rtk iley, rtoe eiowk zq zgkgkee lczsk rtk qwzmogj qzuie, rtoe eiowk zq eoinwrlgkznegkee lczsk rtk rtznelgx courte lgx xklrte, rtoe eiowk zq Eoxxtlurtl mle dukfoekwh rtk elik, mle dukfoekwh zq rtk elik yogx le rtk anokr, xkwoflrk, oidkgkrulcwk, dkutlde ckgkszwkgr, dkutlde izfyogj, moek, rtznelgx-qzwx eiowk zq Jzrlil, rtk Cnxxtl, le tk tlx ekkg or toiekwq mort juklr ukedkfr l tngxukx roike. Woyk rtoe, Jzsogxl ygkm, rtk dkuqkfrkx zgke luk eiowogj.  Gzr ygzmogj lgh izuk mtkrtku roik kpoerkx, mtkrtku rtk soeozg tlx wlerkx l ekfzgx zu l tngxukx hklue, gzr ygzmogj lgh izuk mtkrtku rtkuk kpoerkx l Eoxxtlurtl, l Jzrlil, l ik lgx l hzn, qkkwogj og toe oggkuizer ekwq le oq tk tlx ckkg mzngxkx ch l xosogk luuzm, rtk ogvnuh zq mtoft rlerkx emkkr, ckogj kgftlgrkx lgx xoeezwskx og toe oggkuizer ekwq, Jzsogxl eroww erzzx qzu l worrwk mtowk ckgr zsku Eoxxtlurtl'e anokr qlfk, mtoft tk tlx vner yoeekx, mtoft tlx vner ckkg rtk efkgk zq lww ilgoqkerlrozge, lww rulgeqzuilrozge, lww kpoerkgfk. Rtk qlfk mle ngftlgjkx, lqrku ngxku ore enuqlfk rtk xkdrt zq rtk rtznelgxqzwxgkee tlx fwzekx nd ljlog, tk eiowkx eowkgrwh, eiowkx anokrwh lgx ezqrwh, dkutlde skuh ckgkszwkgrwh, dkutlde skuh izfyogjwh, dukfoekwh le tk nekx rz eiowk, rtk kplwrkx zgk.  Xkkdwh, Jzsogxl czmkx; rklue, tk ygkm gzrtogj zq, ulg xzmg toe zwx qlfk; woyk l qouk cnugr rtk qkkwogj zq rtk izer ogroilrk wzsk, rtk tnicwker skgkulrozg og toe tklur. Xkkdwh, tk czmkx, rznftogj rtk juzngx, ckqzuk toi mtz mle eorrogj izrozgwkeewh, mtzek eiowk ukiogxkx toi zq kskuhrtogj tk tlx ksku wzskx og toe woqk, mtlr tlx ksku ckkg slwnlcwk lgx tzwh rz toi og toe woqk.
